śatayājaṃ sa yajate nainaṃ dunvanty agnayaḥ
jinvanti viśve taṃ devā yo brāhmaṇa ṛṣabham ājuhoti
brāhmaṇebhya ṛṣabhaṃ dattvā varīyaḥ kṛṇute manaḥ
puṣṭiṃ so aghnyānāṃ sve goṣṭhe 'va paśyate
gāvaḥ santu prajāḥ santv atho astu tanūbalam
tat sarvam anu manyantāṃ devā ṛṣabhadāyine
ayaṃ pipāna indra id rayiṃ dadhātu cetanīm
ayaṃ dhenuṃ sudughāṃ nityavatsāṃ vaśaṃ duhāṃ vipaścitaṃ paro divaḥ
piśaṅgarūpo nabhaso vayodhā aindraḥ śuṣmo viśvarūpo na āgan
āyur asmabhyaṃ dadhat prajāṃ ca rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacatām
upehopaparcanāsmin goṣṭha upa pṛñca naḥ
upa ṛṣabhasya yad reta upendra tava vīryam
etaṃ vo yuvānaṃ prati dadhmo atra tena krīḍantīś carata vaśāṃ anu
mā no hāsiṣṭa januṣā subhāgā rāyaś ca poṣair abhi naḥ sacadhvam
ā nayaitam ā rabhasva sukṛtāṃ lokam api gachatu prajānan
tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā mahānty ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam
indrāya bhāgaṃ pari tvā nayāmy asmin yajñe yajamānāya sūrim
ye no dviṣanty anu tān rabhasvānāgaso yajamānasya vīrāḥ
pra pado 'va nenigdhi duścaritaṃ yac cacāra śuddhaiḥ śaphair ā kramatāṃ prajānan
tīrtvā tamāṃsi bahudhā vipaśyann ajo nākam ā kramatāṃ tṛtīyam
anuchya śyāmena tvacam etāṃ viśastar yathāparv asinā mābhi maṃsthāḥ
mābhi druhaḥ paruśaḥ kalpayainaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayainam
ṛcā kumbhīm adhy agnau śrayāmy ā siñcodakam ava dhehy enam
paryādhattāgninā śamitāraḥ śṛto gachatu sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ
ut krāmātaḥ pari ced ataptas taptāc caror adhi nākaṃ tṛtīyam
agner agnir adhi saṃ babhūvitha jyotiṣmantam abhi lokaṃ jayaitam
ajo agnir ajam u jyotir āhur ajaṃ jīvatā brahmaṇe deyam āhuḥ
ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ
pañcaudanaḥ pañcadhā vi kramatām ākraṃsyamānas trīṇi jyotīṃṣi
ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ prehi madhyaṃ tṛtīye nāke adhi vi śrayasva
ajā roha sukṛtāṃ yatra lokaḥ śarabho na catto 'ti durgāny eṣaḥ
pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamānaḥ sa dātāraṃ tṛptyā tarpayāti
ajas trināke tridive tripṛṣṭhe nākasya pṛṣṭhe dadivāṃsaṃ dadhāti
pañcaudano brahmaṇe dīyamāno viśvarūpā dhenuḥ kāmadughāsy ekā
etad vo jyotiḥ pitaras tṛtīyaṃ pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti
ajas tamāṃsy apa hanti dūram asmiṃl loke śraddadhānena dattaḥ
ījānānāṃ sukṛtāṃ lokam īpsan pañcaudanaṃ brahmaṇe 'jaṃ dadāti
sa vyāptim abhi lokaṃ jayaitaṃ śivo 'smabhyaṃ pratigṛhīto astu
ajo hy agner ajaniṣṭa śokād vipro viprasya sahaso vipaścit
iṣṭaṃ pūrtam abhipūrtaṃ vaṣaṭkṛtaṃ tad devā ṛtuśaḥ kalpayantu
amotaṃ vāso dadyād dhiraṇyam api dakṣiṇām
tathā lokānt sam āpnoti ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ
etās tvājopa yantu dhārāḥ somyā devīr ghṛtapṛṣṭhā madhuścutaḥ
stabhān pṛthivīm uta dyāṃ nākasya pṛṣṭhe 'dhi saptaraśmau
ajo 'sy aja svargo 'si tvayā lokam aṅgirasaḥ prājānan
taṃ lokaṃ puṇyaṃ pra jñeṣam
yenā sahasraṃ vahasi yenāgne sarvavedasam
tenemaṃ yajñaṃ no vaha svar deveṣu gantave
ajaḥ pakvaḥ svarge loke dadhāti pañcaudano nirṛtiṃ bādhamānaḥ
tena lokānt sūryavato jayema
yaṃ brāhmaṇe nidadhe yaṃ ca vikṣu yā vipruṣa odanānām ajasya
sarvaṃ tad agne sukṛtasya loke jānītān naḥ saṃgamane pathīnām
ajo vā idam agne vy akramata tasyora iyam abhavad dyauḥ pṛṣṭiham
antarikṣaṃ madhyam diśaḥ pārśve samudrau kukṣī
satyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca cakṣuṣī viśvaṃ satyaṃ śraddhā prāṇo virāṭ śiraḥ
eṣa vā aparimito yajño yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
aparimitam eva yajñam āpnoty aparimitaṃ lokam ava runddhe
yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti
nāsyāsthīni bhindyān na majjño nir dhayet
sarvam enaṃ samādāyedamidaṃ pra veśayet
idamidam evāsya rūpaṃ bhavati tenainaṃ saṃ gamayati
iṣaṃ maha ūrjam asmai duhe yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti
pañca rukmā pañca navāni vastrā pañcāsmai dhenavaḥ kāmadughā bhavanti
yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti
pañca rukmā jyotir asmai bhavanti varma vāsāṃsi tanve bhavanti
svargaṃ lokam aśnute yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanaṃ dakṣiṇājyotiṣam dadāti
yā pūrvaṃ patiṃ vittvā 'thānyaṃ vindate 'param
pañcaudanaṃ ca tāv ajaṃ dadāto na vi yoṣataḥ
samānaloko bhavati punarbhuvāparaḥ patiḥ
yo 'jaṃ pañcaudanam dakṣiṇājyotiṣaṃ dadāti
anupūrvavatsāṃ dhenum anaḍvāham upabarhaṇam
vāso hiraṇyaṃ dattvā te yanti divam uttamām
ātmānaṃ pitaraṃ putraṃ pautraṃ pitāmaham
jāyāṃ janitrīṃ mātaraṃ ye priyās tān upa hvaye
yo vai naidāghaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda
eṣa vai naidāgho nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
nir evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ dahati bhavaty ātmanā
yo vai kurvantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda
kurvatīṃkurvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte
eṣa vai kurvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
yo vai saṃyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda
saṃyatīṃsaṃyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte
eṣa vai saṃyan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
yo vai pinvantaṃ nāma rtum veda
pinvatīṃpinvatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte
eṣa vai pinvan nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
yo vā udyantaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda
udyatīṃudyatīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte
eṣa vā udyann nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
yo vā abhibhuvaṃ nāma rtuṃ veda
abhibhavantīmabhibhavantīm evāpriyasya bhrātṛvyasya śriyaṃ ā datte
eṣa vā abhibhūr nāma rtur yad ajaḥ pañcaudanaḥ
ajaṃ ca pacata pañca caudanān
sarvā diśaḥ saṃmanasaḥ sadhrīcīḥ sāntardeśāḥ prati gṛhnantu ta etam
tās te rakṣantu tava tubhyam etaṃ tābhya ājyaṃ havir idaṃ juhomi
yo vidyād brahma pratyakṣaṃ parūṃṣi yasya saṃbhārā ṛco yasyānūkyam
sāmāni yasya lomāni yajur hṛdayam ucyate paristaraṇam id dhaviḥ
yad vā atithipatir atithīn pratipaśyati devayajanaṃ prekṣate
yad abhivadati dīkṣām upaiti yad udakaṃ yācaty apaḥ pra ṇayati
yā eva yajña āpaḥ praṇīyante tā eva tāḥ
yat tarpaṇam āharanti ya evāgnīṣomīyaḥ paśur badhyate sa eva saḥ
yad āvasathān kalpayanti sadohavirdhānāny eva tat kalpayanti
yad upastṛṇanti barhir eva tat
yad upariśayanam āharanti svargam eva tena lokam ava runddhe
yat kaśipūpabarhaṇam āharanti paridhaya eva te
yad āñjanābhyañjanam āharanty ājyam eva tat
yat purā pariveṣāt svādam āharanti purodāśāv eva tau
yad aśanakṛtaṃ hvayanti haviṣkṛtam eva tad dhvayanti
ye vrīhayo yavā nirupyante 'ṃśava eva te
yāny ulūkhalamusalāni grāvāṇa eva te
śūrpaṃ pavitraṃ tuṣā ṛjīṣābhiṣavaṇīr āpaḥ
srug darvir nekṣaṇam āyavanaṃ droṇakalaśāḥ kumbhyo vāyavyāni pātrāṇīyam eva kṛṣṇājinam
yajamānabrāhmaṇaṃ vā etad atithipatiḥ kurute yad āhāryāṇi prekṣata idaṃ bhūyā3 idā3m iti
yad āha bhūya ud dhareti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kurute
upa harati havīṃṣy ā sādayati
teṣām āsannānām atithir ātman juhoti
srucā hastena prāṇe yūpe srukkāreṇa vaṣaṭkāreṇa
ete vai priyāś cāpriyāś ca rtvijaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti yad atithayaḥ
sa ya evaṃ vidvān na dviṣann aśnīyān na dviṣato 'nnam aśnīyān na mīmāṃsitasya na mīmāṃsamānasya
sarvo vā eṣa jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam aśnanti
sarvo vā eso 'jagdhapāpmā yasyānnam nāśnanti
sarvadā vā eṣa yuktagrāvārdrapavitro vitatādhvara āhṛtayajñakratur ya upaharati
prājāpatyo vā etasya yajño vitato ya upaharati
prajāpater vā eṣa vikramān anuvikramate ya upaharati
yo 'tithīnāṃ sa āhavanīyo yo veśmani sa gārhapatyo yasmin pacanti sa dakṣiṇāgniḥ
iṣṭaṃ ca vā eṣa pūrtaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
payaś ca vā eṣa rasaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
ūrjāṃ ca vā eṣa sphātiṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
prajāṃ vā eṣa paśūṃś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
kīrtiṃ vā eṣa yaśaś ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
śriyaṃ vā eṣa saṃvidaṃ ca gṛhāṇām aśnāti yaḥ pūrvo 'tither aśnāti
eṣa vā atithir yac chrotriyas tasmāt pūrvo nāśnīyāt
aśitāvaty atithāv aśnīyād yajñasya sātmatvāya yajñasyāvichedāya tad vratam
etad vā u svādīyo yad adhigavaṃ kṣīraṃ vā māṃsaṃ vā tad eva nāśnīyāt
sa ya evaṃ vidvān kṣīram upasicyopaharati
yāvad agniṣṭomeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe
sa ya evaṃ vidvānt sarpir upasicyopaharati
yāvad atirātreṇeṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe
sa ya evaṃ vidvān madhūpasicyopaharati
yāvad sattrasadyeneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe
sa ya evaṃ vidvān māṃsam upasicyopaharati
yāvad dvādaśāheneṣṭvā susamṛddhenāvarunddhe tāvad enenāva runddhe
sa ya evaṃ vidvān udakam upasicyopaharati
prajānāṃ prajananāya gachati pratiṣṭhāṃ priyaḥ prajānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān upasicyopaharati
tasmā uṣā hiṅ kṛṇoti savitā pra stauti
bṛhaspatir ūrjayod gāyati tvaṣṭā puṣṭyā prati harati viśve devā nidhanam
nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasmā udyant sūryo hiṅ kṛṇoti saṃgavaḥ pra stauti
madhyandina ud gāyaty aparāhṇaḥ prati haraty astaṃyan nidhanam
nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasmā abhro bhavan hiṅ kṛṇoti stanayan pra stauti
vidyotamānaḥ prati harati varṣann ud gāyaty udgṛhṇan nidhanam
nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
atithīn prati paśyati hiṅ kṛṇoty abhi vadati pra stauty udakam yācaty ud gāyati
upa harati prati haraty ucchiṣṭaṃ nidhanam
nidhanaṃ bhūtyāḥ prajāyāḥ paśūnāṃ bhavati ya evam veda
yat kṣattāraṃ hvayaty ā śrāvayaty eva tat
yat pratiśṛṇoti pratyāśrāvayaty eva tat
yat pariveṣṭāraḥ pātrahastāḥ pūrve cāpare ca prapadyante camasādhvaryava eva te
teṣāṃ na kaś canāhotā
yad vā atithipatir atithīn pariviṣya gṛhān upodaity avabhṛtham eva tad upāvaiti
yat sabhāgayati dakṣiṇāḥ sabhāgayati yad anutiṣṭhata udavasyaty eva tat
sa upahūtaḥ pṛthivyāṃ bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yat pṛthivyāṃ viśvarūpam
sa upahūto 'ntarikṣe bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam
sa upahūto divi bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam
sa upahūto deveṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam
sa upahūto lokeṣu bhakṣayaty upahūtas tasmin yad divi viśvarūpam
sa upahūta upahūtaḥ
āpnotīmaṃ lokam āpnoty amum
jyotiṣmato lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca śṛṅge indraḥ śiro agnir lalāṭaṃ yamaḥ kṛkāṭam
somo rājā mastiṣko dyaur uttarahanuḥ pṛthivy adharahanuḥ
vidyuj jihvā maruto dantā revatir grīvāḥ kṛttikā skandhā gharmo vahaḥ
viśvaṃ vāyuḥ svargo lokaḥ kṛṣṇadraṃ vidharaṇī niveṣyaḥ
śyenaḥ kroto 'ntarikṣaṃ pājasyaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ kakud bṛhatīḥ kīkasāḥ
devānāṃ patnīḥ pṛṣṭaya upasadaḥ parśavaḥ
mitraś ca varuṇaś cāṃsau tvaṣṭā cāryamā ca doṣaṇī mahādevo bāhū
indrāṇī bhasad vāyuḥ puchaṃ pavamāno bālāḥ
brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca śroṇī balam ūrū
dhātā ca savitā cāṣṭhīvantau jaṅghā gandharvā apsarasaḥ kuṣṭhikā aditiḥ śaphāḥ
ceto hṛdayaṃ yakṛn medhā vrataṃ purītat
kṣut kukṣir irā vaniṣṭhuḥ parvatāḥ plāśayaḥ
krodho vṛkkau manyur āṇḍau prajā śepaḥ
nadī sūtrī varṣasya pataya stanā stanayitnur ūdhaḥ
viśvavyacās carmauṣadhayo lomāni nakṣatrāṇi rūpam
devajanā gudā manuṣyā āntrāṇy atrā udaram
rakṣāṃsi lohitam itarajanā ūbadhyam
abhraṃ pībo majjā nidhanam
agnir āsīna utthito 'śvinā
indraḥ prāṅ tiṣṭhan dakṣiṇā tiṣṭhan yamaḥ
pratyaṅ tiṣṭhan dhātodaṅ tiṣṭhant savitā
tṛṇāni prāptaḥ somo rājā
mitra īkṣamāṇa āvṛtta ānandaḥ
yujyamāno vaiśvadevo yuktaḥ prajāpatir vimuktaḥ sarvam
etad vai viśvarūpaṃ sarvarūpaṃ gorūpam
upainaṃ viśvarūpāḥ sarvarūpāḥ paśavas tiṣṭhanti ya evaṃ veda
śīrṣaktiṃ śīrṣāmayaṃ karṇaśūlaṃ vilohitam
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
karṇābhyāṃ te kaṅkūṣebhyaḥ karṇaśūlaṃ visalpakam
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
yasya hetoḥ pracyavate yakṣmaḥ karṇato āsyataḥ
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
yaḥ kṛṇoti pramotam andhaṃ kṛṇoti pūruṣam
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
aṅgabhedam aṅgajvaram viśvāṅgyaṃ visalpakam
sarvaṃ śīrṣanyaṃ te rogaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
yasya bhīmaḥ pratīkāśa udvepayati pūruṣam
takmānaṃ viśvaśāradaṃ bahir nir mantrayāmahe
ya ūrū anusarpaty atho eti gavīnike
yakṣmaṃ te antar aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe
yadi kāmād apakāmād dhṛdayāj jāyate pari
hṛdo balāsam aṅgebhyo bahir nir mantrayāmahe
harimāṇaṃ te aṅgebhyo 'pvām antarodarāt
yakṣmodhām antar ātmano bahir nir mantrayāmahe
āso balāso bhavatu mūtraṃ bhavatv āmayat
yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat
bahir bilaṃ nir dravatu kāhābāhaṃ tavodarāt
yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat
udarāt te klomno nābhyā hṛdayād adhi
yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat
yāḥ sīmānaṃ virujanti mūrdhānaṃ praty arṣanīḥ
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
yā hṛdayam uparṣanty anutanvanti kīkasāḥ
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
yāḥ pārśve uparṣanty anunikṣanti pṛṣṭīḥ
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
yās tiraścīḥ uparṣanty arṣaṇīr vakṣaṇāsu te
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
yā gudā anusarpanty āntrāṇi mohayanti ca
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
yā majjño nirdhayanti parūṃṣi virujanti ca
ahiṃsantīr anāmayā nir dravantu bahir bilam
ye aṅgāni madayanti yakṣmāso ropaṇās tava
yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat
visalpasya vidradhasya vātīkārasya vālajeḥ
yakṣmāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ nir avocam ahaṃ tvat
pādābhyāṃ te jānubhyāṃ śroṇibhyāṃ pari bhaṃsasaḥ
anūkād arṣaṇīr uṣṇihābhyaḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśam
saṃ te śīrṣṇaḥ kapālāni hṛdayasya ca yo vidhuḥ
udyann āditya raśmibhiḥ śīrṣṇo rogam anīnaśo 'ṅgabhedam aśīśamaḥ
asya vāmasya palitasya hotus tasya bhrātā madhyamo asty aśnaḥ
tṛtīyo bhrātā ghṛtapṛṣṭho asyātrāpaśyaṃ viśpatiṃ saptaputram
sapta yuñjanti ratham ekacakram eko aśvo vahati saptanāmā
trinābhi cakram ajaram anarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhi tasthuḥ
imaṃ ratham adhi ye sapta tasthuḥ saptacakraṃ sapta vahanty aśvāḥ
sapta svasāro abhi saṃ navanta yatra gavām nihitā sapta nāma
ko dadarśa prathamaṃ jāyamānam asthanvantaṃ yad anasthā bibharti
bhūmyā asur asṛg ātmā kva svit ko vidvāṃsam upa gāt praṣṭum etat
iha bravītu ya īm aṅga vedāsya vāmasya nihitaṃ padaṃ veḥ
śīrṣṇaḥ kṣīraṃ duhrate gāvo asya vavriṃ vasānā udakaṃ padā 'puḥ
pākaḥ pṛchāmi manasā 'vijānan devānām enā nihitā padāni
vatse baṣkaye 'dhi sapta tantūn vi tatnire kavaya otavā u
acikitvāṃs cikituṣaś cid atra kavīn pṛchāmi vidvano na vidvān
vi yas tastambha ṣaṭ imā rajāṃsy ajasya rūpe kiṃ api svid ekam
mātā pitaram ṛta ā babhāja 'dhīty agre manasā saṃ hi jagme
sā bībhatsur garbharasā nividdhā namasvanta id upavākam īyuḥ
yuktā mātāsid dhuri dakṣiṇāyā atiṣṭhad garbho vṛjanīṣv antaḥ
amīmed vatso anu gām apaśyad viśvarūpyaṃ triṣu yoganeṣu
tisro matṝs trīn pitṝn bibhrad eka urdhvas tasthau nem ava glāpayanta
mantrayante divo amuṣya pṛṣṭhe viśvavido vācam aviśvavinnām
pañcāre cakre parivartamāne yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā
tasya nākṣas tapyate bhūribhāraḥ sanād eva na chidyate sanābhiḥ
pañcapādaṃ pitaraṃ dvādaśākṛtiṃ diva āhuḥ pare ardhe purīṣiṇam
atheme anya upare vicakṣaṇe saptacakre ṣaḍara āhur arpitam
dvādaśāraṃ nahi taj jarāya varvarti cakraṃ pari dyām ṛtasya
ā putrā agne mithunāso atra sapta śatāni viṃśatiś ca tasthuḥ
sanemi cakram ajaraṃ vi vavṛta uttānāyāṃ daśa yuktā vahanti
sūryasya cakṣū rajasaity āvṛtaṃ yasminn ātasthur bhuvanāni viśvā
striyaḥ satīs tām u me puṃsaḥ āhuḥ paśyad akṣaṇvānn vi cetad andhaḥ
kavir yaḥ putraḥ sa īm ā ciketa yas tā vijānāt sa pituṣ pitāsat
sākaṃjānāṃ saptatham āhur ekajaṃ ṣaḍ id yamā ṛṣayo devajā iti
teṣām iṣṭāni vihitāni dhāmaśa sthātre rejante vikṛtāni rūpaśaḥ
avaḥ pareṇa para enā avareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibhratī gaur ud asthāt
sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin
avaḥ pareṇa pitaraṃ yo asya vedāvaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa
kavīyamānaḥ ka iha pra vocad devaṃ manaḥ kuto adhi prajātam
ye arvāñcas tām u parāca āhur ye parāñcas tāṃ u arvāca āhuḥ
indraś ca yā cakrathuḥ soma tāni dhurā na yuktā rajaso vahanti
dvā suparṇā sayujā sakhāyā samānaṃ vṛkṣaṃ pari ṣasvajāte
tayor anyaḥ pippalaṃ svādv atty anaśnann anyo abhi cākaśīti
yasmin vṛkṣe madhvadaḥ suparṇā niviśante suvate cādhi viśve
tasya yad āhuḥ pippalaṃ svādv agre tan non naśad yaḥ pitaraṃ na veda
yatrā suparṇā amṛtasya bhakṣam animeṣaṃ vidathābhisvaranti
enā viśvasya bhuvanasya gopāḥ sa mā dhīraḥ pākam atrā viveśa
yad gāyatre adhi gāyatram āhitaṃ traiṣṭubhaṃ vā traiṣṭubhān niratakṣata
yad vā jagaj jagaty āhitaṃ padaṃ ya it tad vidus te amṛtatvam ānuśuḥ
gāyatreṇa prati mimīte arkam arkeṇa sāma traiṣṭubhena vākam
vākena vākaṃ dvipadā catuṣpadākṣareṇa mimate sapta vāṇīḥ
jagatā sindhuṃ divy askabhāyad rathaṃtare sūryaṃ pary apaśyat
gāyatrasya samidhas tisra āhus tato mahnā pra ririce mahitvā
upa hvaye sudughāṃ dhenum etāṃ suhasto godhug uta dohad enām
śreṣṭhaṃ savaṃ savitā sāviṣan no 'bhīddho gharmas tad u ṣu pra vocat
hiṅkṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnāṃ vatsam ichantī manasābhyāgāt
duhām aśvibhyāṃ payo aghnyeyaṃ sā vardhatāṃ mahate saubhagāya
gaur amīmed abhi vatsaṃ miṣantaṃ mūrdhānaṃ hiṅṅ akṛṇon mātavā u
sṛkvāṇaṃ gharmam abhi vāvaśānā mimāti māyuṃ payate payobhiḥ
ayaṃ sa śiṅkte yena gaur abhivṛtā mimāti mayuṃ dhvasanāv adhi śritā
sā cittibhir ni hi cakāra martyān vidyud bhavantī prati vavrim auhata
anac chaye turagātu jīvam ejad dhruvaṃ madhya ā pastyānām
jīvo mṛtasya carati svadhābhir amartyo martyenā sayoniḥ
vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe yuvānaṃ santaṃ palito jagāra
devasya paśya kāvyaṃ mahitvādya mamāra sa hyaḥ sam āna
ya īṃ cakāra na so asya veda ya īṃ dadarśa hirug in nu tasmāt
sa mātur yonā parivīto antar bahuprajā nirṛtir ā viveśa
apaśyaṃ gopām anipadyamānam ā ca parā ca pathibhiś carantam
sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīr vasāna ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antaḥ
dyaur naḥ pitā janitā nābhir atra bandhur no mātā pṛthivī mahīyam
uttānayoś camvor yonir antar atrā pitā duhitur garbham ādhāt
pṛchāmi tvā param antaṃ pṛthivyāḥ pṛchāmi vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ
pṛchāmi viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhiṃ pṛchāmi vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma
iyaṃ vediḥ paro antaḥ pṛthivyā ayaṃ somo vṛṣṇo aśvasya retaḥ
ayaṃ yajño viśvasya bhuvanasya nābhir brahmāyaṃ vācaḥ paramaṃ vyoma
na vi jānāmi yad ivedam asmi niṇyaḥ saṃnaddho manasā carāmi
yadā māgan prathamajā ṛtasyād id vāco aśnuve bhāgam asyāḥ
apāṅ prāṅ eti svadhayā gṛbhīto 'martyo martyenā sayoniḥ
tā śaśvantā viṣūcīnā viyantā ny anyaṃ cikyur na ni cikyur anyam
saptārdhagarbhā bhuvanasya reto viṣṇos tiṣṭhanti pradiśā vidharmaṇi
te dhītibhir manasā te vipaścitaḥ paribhuvaḥ pari bhavanti viśvataḥ
ṛco akṣare parame vyoman yasmin devā adhi viśve niṣeduḥ
yas tan na veda kim ṛcā kariṣyati ya it tad vidus te amī sam āsate
ṛcaḥ padaṃ mātrayā kalpayanto 'rdharcena cakḷpur viśvam ejat
tripād brahma pururūpaṃ vi taṣṭhe tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ
sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā adhā vayaṃ bhagavantaḥ syāma
addhi tṛṇam aghnye viśvadānīṃ piba śuddham udakam ācarantī
gaur in mimāya salilāni takṣatī ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī
aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti
kṛṣṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti
taṃ āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasyād id ghṛtena pṛthivīṃ vy ūduḥ
apād eti prathamā padvatīnāṃ kas tad vāṃ mitrāvaruṇā ciketa
garbho bhāraṃ bharaty ā cid asyā ṛtaṃ piparti anṛtaṃ ni pāti
virāḍ vāg virāṭ pṛthivī virāḍ antarikṣaṃ virāṭ prajāpatiḥ
virāṇ mṛtyuḥ sādhyānām adhirājo babhūva tasya bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe sa me bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ vaśe kṛṇotu
śakamayaṃ dhūmam ārād apaśyaṃ viṣūvatā para enāvareṇa
ukṣāṇaṃ pṛśnim apacanta vīrās tāni dharmāṇi prathamāny āsan
trayaḥ keśina ṛtuthā vi cakṣate saṃvatsare vapata eka eṣām
viśvam anyo abhicaṣṭe śacībhir dhrājir ekasya dadṛśe na rūpam
catvāri vāk parimitā padāni tāni vidur brāhmaṇā ye manīṣiṇaḥ
guhā trīṇi nihitā neṅgayanti turīyaṃ vāco manuṣyā vadanti
indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇam agnim āhur atho divyaḥ sa suparṇo garutmān
ekaṃ sad viprā bahudhā vadanty agniṃ yamaṃ mātariśvānam āhuḥ
yāṃ kalpayanti vahatau vadhūm iva viśvarūpāṃ hastakṛtāṃ cikitsavaḥ
sārād etv apa nudāma enām
śīrṣaṇvatī nasvatī karṇiṇī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā
sārād etv apa nudāma enām
śūdrakṛtā rājakṛtā strīkṛtā brahmabhiḥ kṛtā
jāyā patyā nutteva kartāraṃ bandhv ṛchatu
anayāham oṣadhyā sarvāḥ kṛtyā adūduṣam
yāṃ kṣetre cakrur yāṃ goṣu yāṃ vā te puruṣeṣu
agham astv aghakṛte śapathaḥ śapathīyate
pratyak pratiprahiṇmo yathā kṛtyākṛtaṃ hanat
pratīcīna āṅgiraso 'dhyakṣo naḥ purohitaḥ
pratīcīḥ kṛtyā ākṛtyāmūn kṛtyākṛto jahi
yas tvovāca parehīti pratikūlam udāyyam
taṃ kṛtye 'bhinivartasva māsmān icho anāgasaḥ
yas te parūṃṣi saṃdadhau rathasyeva rbhur dhiyā
taṃ gacha tatra te 'yanam ajñātas te 'yaṃ janaḥ
ye tvā kṛtvālebhire vidvalā abhicāriṇaḥ
śaṃbhv idaṃ kṛtyādūṣaṇaṃ prativartma punaḥsaraṃ tena tvā snapayāmasi
yad durbhagāṃ prasnapitāṃ mṛtavatsām upeyima
apaitu sarvaṃ mat pāpaṃ draviṇaṃ mopa tiṣṭhatu
yat te pitṛbhyo dadato yajñe vā nāma jagṛhuḥ
saṃdeśyāt sarvasmāt pāpād imā muñcantu tvauṣadhīḥ
devainasāt pitryān nāmagrāhāt saṃdeśyād abhiniṣkṛtāt
muñcantu tvā vīrudho vīryeṇa brahmaṇā ṛgbhiḥ payasā ṛṣīṇām
yathā vātaś cyāvayati bhūmyā reṇum antarikṣāc cābhram
evā mat sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ brahmanuttam apāyati
apa krāma nānadatī vinaddhā gardabhīva
kartṝn nakṣasveto nuttā brahmaṇā vīryāvatā
ayaṃ panthāḥ kṛtyeti tvā nayāmo 'bhiprahitāṃ prati tvā pra hiṇmaḥ
tenābhi yāhi bhañjaty anasvatīva vāhinī viśvarūpā kurūtinī
parāk te jyotir apathaṃ te arvāg anyatrāsmad ayanā kṛṇuṣva
pareṇehi navatiṃ nāvyā ati durgāḥ srotyā mā kṣaṇiṣṭhāḥ parehi
vāta iva vṛkṣān ni mṛṇīhi pādaya mā gām aśvaṃ puruṣam uc chiṣa eṣām
kartṝn nivṛtyetaḥ kṛtye 'prajāstvāya bodhaya
yāṃ te barhiṣi yāṃ śmaśāne kṣetre kṛtyāṃ valagaṃ vā nicakhnuḥ
agnau vā tvā gārhapatye 'bhiceruḥ pākaṃ santaṃ dhīratarā anāgasam
upāhṛtam anubuddhaṃ nikhātaṃ vairaṃ tsāry anv avidāma kartram
tad etu yata ābhṛtaṃ tatrāśva iva vi vartatāṃ hantu kṛtyākṛtaḥ prajām
svāyasā asayaḥ santi no gṛhe vidmā te kṛtye yatidhā parūṃṣi
ut tiṣṭhaiva parehīto 'jñāte kim ihechasi
grīvās te kṛtye pādau cāpi kartsyāmi nir drava
indrāgnī asmān rakṣatāṃ yau prajānāṃ prajāvatī
somo rājādhipā mṛḍitā ca bhūtasya naḥ patayo mṛḍayantu
bhavāśarvāv asyatāṃ pāpakṛte kṛtyākṛte
duṣkṛte vidyutaṃ devahetim
yady eyatha dvipadī catuṣpadī kṛtyākṛtā saṃbhṛtā viśvarūpā
seto 'ṣṭāpadī bhūtvā punaḥ parehi duchune
abhyaktāktā svaraṃkṛtā sarvaṃ bharantī duritaṃ parehi
jānīhi kṛtye kartāraṃ duhiteva pitaraṃ svam
parehi kṛtye mā tiṣṭho viddhasyeva padaṃ naya
mṛgaḥ sa mṛgayus tvaṃ na tvā nikartum arhati
uta hanti pūrvāsinaṃ pratyādāyāpara iṣvā
uta pūrvasya nighnato ni hanty aparaḥ prati
etad dhi śṛṇu me vaco 'thehi yata eyatha
yas tvā cakāra taṃ prati
anāgohatyā vai bhīmā kṛtye mā no gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ vadhīḥ
yatrayatrāsi nihitā tatas tvot thāpayāmasi parṇāl laghīyasī bhava
yadi stha tamasāvṛtā jālenabhihitā iva
sarvāḥ saṃlupyetaḥ kṛtyāḥ punaḥ kartre pra hiṇmasi
kṛtyākṛto valagino 'bhiniṣkāriṇaḥ prajām
mṛṇīhi kṛtye moc chiṣo 'mūn kṛtyākṛto jahi
yathā sūryo mucyate tamasas pari rātriṃ jahāty uṣasaśca ketūn
evāhaṃ sarvaṃ durbhūtaṃ kartraṃ kṛtyākṛtā kṛtaṃ hastīva rajo duritaṃ jahāmi
kena pārṣṇī ābhṛte pūruṣasya kena māṃsaṃ saṃbhṛtaṃ kena gulphau
kenāṅgulīḥ peśanīḥ kena khāni kenocchlaṅkhau madhyataḥ kaḥ pratiṣṭhām
kasmān nu gulphāv adharāv akṛṇvann aṣṭhīvantāv uttarau puruṣasya
jaṅghe nirṛtya ny adadhuḥ kva svij jānunoḥ saṃdhī ka u tac ciketa
catuṣṭayaṃ yujate saṃhitāntaṃ jānubhyām ūrdhvaṃ śithiraṃ kabandham
śroṇī yad ūrū ka u taj jajāna yābhyāṃ kusindhaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ babhūva
kati devāḥ katame ta āsan ya uro grīvāś cikyuḥ puruṣasya
kati stanau vy adadhuḥ kaḥ kaphodau kati skandhān kati pṛṣṭīr acinvan
ko asya bāhū sam abharad vīryāṃ karavād iti
aṃsau ko asya tad devaḥ kusindhe adhy ā dadhau
kaḥ sapta khāni vi tatarda śīrṣaṇi karṇāv imau nāsike cakṣaṇī mukham
yeṣāṃ purutrā vijayasya mahnani catuṣpādo dvipado yanti yāmam
hanvor hi jihvām adadhāt purūcīm adhā mahīm adhi śiśrāya vācam
sa ā varīvarti bhuvaneṣv antar apo vasānaḥ ka u tac ciketa
mastiṣkam asya yatamo lalātaṃ kakāṭikāṃ prathamo yaḥ kapālam
citvā cityaṃ hanvoḥ pūruṣasya divaṃ ruroha katamaḥ sa devaḥ
priyāpriyāṇi bahulā svapnaṃ saṃbādhatandyaḥ
ānandān ugro nandāṃś ca kasmād vahati pūruṣaḥ
ārtir avartir nirṛtiḥ kuto nu puruṣe 'matiḥ
rāddhiḥ samṛddhir avyṛddhir matir uditayaḥ kutaḥ
ko asminn āpo vy adadhāt viṣūvṛtaḥ purūvṛtaḥ sindhusṛtyāya jātāḥ
tīvrā aruṇā lohinīs tāmradhūmrā ūrdhvā avācīḥ puruṣe tiraścīḥ
ko asmin rūpam adadhāt ko mahmānaṃ ca nāma ca
gātuṃ ko asmin kaḥ ketuṃ kaś caritrāni puruṣe
ko asmin prāṇaṃ avayat ko apānaṃ vyānam u
samānam asmin ko devo 'dhi śiśrāya puruṣe
ko asmin yajñam adadhād eko devo 'dhi puruṣe
ko asmint satyaṃ ko 'nṛtaṃ kuto mṛtyuḥ kuto 'mṛtam
ko asmai vāsaḥ pary adadhāt ko asyāyur akalpayat
balaṃ ko asmai prāyachat ko asyākalpayaj javam
kenāpo anv atanuta kenāhar akarod ruce
uṣasaṃ kenānv ainddha kena sāyaṃbhavaṃ dade
ko asmin reto ny adadhāt tantur ā tāyatām iti
medhāṃ ko asminn adhy auhat ko bāṇaṃ ko nṛto dadhau
kenemāṃ bhūmim aurṇot kena pary abhavad divam
kenābhi mahnā parvatān kena karmāṇi puruṣaḥ
kena parjanyam anv eti kena somaṃ vicakṣaṇam
kena yajñam ca śraddhāṃ ca kenāsmin nihitaṃ manaḥ
kena śrotriyam āpnoti kenemaṃ parameṣṭhinam
kenemam agniṃ pūruṣaḥ kena saṃvatsaraṃ mame
brahma śrotriyam āpnoti brahmemaṃ parameṣṭhinam
brahmemam agniṃ pūruṣo brahma saṃvatsaraṃ mame
kena devāṃ anu kṣiyati kena daivajanīr viśaḥ
kenedam anyan nakṣatraṃ kena sat kṣatram ucyate
brahma devāṃ anu kṣiyati brahma daivajanīr viśaḥ
brahmedam anyan nakṣatraṃ brahma sat kṣatram ucyate
keneyaṃ bhūmir vihitā kena dyaur uttarā hitā
kenedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣam vyaco hitam
brahmaṇā bhūmir vihitā brahma dyaur uttarā hitā
brahmedam ūrdhvaṃ tiryak cāntarikṣaṃ vyaco hitam
mūrdhānam asya saṃsīvyātharvā hṛdayaṃ ca yat
mastiṣkād ūrdhvaḥ prairayat pavamāno 'dhi śīrṣataḥ
tad vā atharvaṇaḥ śiro devakośaḥ samubjitaḥ
tat prāṇo abhi rakṣati śiro annam atho manaḥ
ūrdhvo nu sṛṣṭā3s tiryaṅ nu sṛṣṭā3s sarvā diśaḥ puruṣa ā babhūvā3ṃ
puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate
yo vai tāṃ brahmaṇo vedāmṛtenāvṛtāṃ puram
tasmai brahma ca brāhmāś ca cakṣuḥ prāṇaṃ prajāṃ daduḥ
na vai tam cakṣur jahāti na prāṇo jarasaḥ purā
puraṃ yo brahmaṇo veda yasyāḥ puruṣa ucyate
aṣṭācakrā navadvārā devānāṃ pūr ayodhyā
tasyāṃ hiraṇyayaḥ kośaḥ svargo jyotiṣāvṛtaḥ
tasmin hiraṇyaye kośe tryare tripratiṣṭhite
tasmin yad yakṣam ātmanvat tad vai brahmavido viduḥ
prabhrājamānāṃ hariṇīṃ yaśasā saṃparīvṛtām
puraṃ hiraṇyayīṃ brahmā viveśāparājitām
ayaṃ me varaṇo maṇiḥ sapatnakṣayaṇo vṛṣā
tenā rabhasva tvaṃ śatrūn pra mṛṇīhi durasyataḥ
praiṇān chṛṇīhi pra mṛṇā rabhasva maṇis te astu puraetā purastāt
avārayanta varaṇena devā abhyācāram asurāṇāṃ śvaḥśvaḥ
ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo viśvabheṣajaḥ sahasrākṣo harito hiraṇyayaḥ
sa te śatrūn adharān pādayāti pūrvas tān dabhnuhi ye tvā dviṣanti
ayaṃ te kṛtyāṃ vitatām pauruṣeyād ayaṃ bhayāt
ayaṃ tvā sarvasmāt pāpād varaṇo vārayiṣyate
varaṇo vārayātā ayaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ
yakṣmo yo asminn āviṣṭas tam u devā avīvaran
svapnaṃ suptvā yadi paśyāsi pāpaṃ mṛgaḥ sṛtiṃ yati dhāvād ajuṣṭām
parikṣavāc chakuneḥ pāpavādād ayaṃ maṇir varaṇo vārayiṣyate
arātyās tvā nirṛtyā abhicārād atho bhayāt
mṛtyor ojīyaso vadhād varaṇo vārayiṣyate
yan me mātā yan me pitā bhrātaro yac ca me svā yad enaś cakṛmā vayam
tato no vārayiṣyate 'yaṃ devo vanaspatiḥ
varaṇena pravyathitā bhrātṛvyā me sabandhavaḥ
asūrtaṃ rajo apy agus te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ
ariṣṭo 'ham ariṣṭagur āyuṣmānt sarvapūruṣaḥ
tam māyaṃ varaṇo maṇiḥ pari pātu diśodiśaḥ
ayaṃ me varaṇa urasi rājā devo vanaspatiḥ
sa me śatrūn vi bādhatām indro dasyūn ivāsurān
imaṃ bibharmi varaṇam āyuṣmān chataśāradaḥ
sa me rāṣṭraṃ ca kṣatraṃ ca paśūn ojaś ca me dadhat
yathā vāto vanaspatīn vṛkṣān bhanakty ojasā
evā sapatnān me bhaṅgdhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu
yathā vātaś cāgniś ca vṛkṣān psāto vanaspatīn
evā sapatnān me psāhi pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu
yathā vātena prakṣīṇā vṛkṣāḥ śere nyarpitāḥ
evā sapatnāṃs tvaṃ mama pra kṣiṇīhi ny arpaya
pūrvān jātāṃ utāparān varaṇas tvābhi rakṣatu
tāṃs tvaṃ pra chinddhi varaṇa purā diṣṭāt purāyuṣaḥ
ya enaṃ paśuṣu dipsanti ye cāsya rāṣṭradipsavaḥ
yathā sūryo atibhāti yathāsmin teja āhitam
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśaś candramasy āditye ca nṛcakṣasi
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśaḥ pṛthivyāṃ yathāsmin jātavedasi
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśaḥ kanyāyāṃ yathāsmint saṃbhṛte rathe
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśaḥ somapīthe madhuparke yathā yaśaḥ
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśo 'gnihotre vaṣaṭkāre yathā yaśaḥ
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśo yajamāne yathāsmin yajña āhitam
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā yaśaḥ prajāpatau yathāsmin parameṣṭhini
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
yathā deveṣv amṛtaṃ yathaiṣu satyam āhitam
evā me varaṇo maṇiḥ kīrtiṃ bhūtiṃ ni yachatu
tejasā mā sam ukṣatu yaśasā sam anaktu mā
indrasya prathamo ratho devānām aparo ratho varuṇasya tṛtīya it
ahīnām apamā ratha sthānum ārad athārṣat
darbhaḥ śocis tarūṇakam aśvasya vāraḥ paruṣasya vāraḥ
rathasya bandhuram
ava śveta padā jahi pūrveṇa cāpareṇa ca
udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram
araṃghuṣo nimajyonmaja punar abravīt
udaplutam iva dārv ahīnām arasaṃ viṣaṃ vār ugram
paidvo hanti kasarṇīlaṃ paidvaḥ śvitram utāsitam
paidvo ratharvyāḥ śiraḥ saṃ bibheda pṛdākvāḥ
paidva prehi prathamo 'nu tvā vayam emasi
ahīn vy asyatāt patho yena smā vayam emasi
idaṃ paidvo ajāyatedam asya parāyaṇam
imāny arvataḥ padāhighnyo vājinīvataḥ
saṃyataṃ na vi ṣparad vyāttaṃ na saṃ yamat
asmin kṣetre dvāv ahī strī ca pumāṃś ca tāv ubhāv arasā
arasāsa ihāhayo ye anti ye ca dūrake
ghanena hanmi vṛścikam ahiṃ daṇḍenāgatam
aghāśvasyedaṃ bheṣajam ubhayo svajasya ca
indro me 'him aghāyantam ahiṃ paidvo arandhayat
paidvasya manmahe vayaṃ sthirasya sthiradhāmnaḥ
ime paścā pṛdākavaḥ pradīdhyata āsate
naṣṭāsavo naṣṭaviṣā hatā indreṇa vajriṇā
jaghānendro jaghnimā vayam
hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ
darviṃ karikrataṃ śvitraṃ darbheṣv asitaṃ jahi
kairātikā kumārikā sakā khanati bheṣajam
hiraṇyayībhir abhribhir girīnām upa sānuṣu
āyam agan yuvā bhiṣak pṛśnihāparājitaḥ
sa vai svajasya jambhana ubhayor vṛścikasya ca
indro me 'him arandhayan mitraś ca varuṇaś ca
vātāparjanyobhā
indro me 'him arandhayat pṛdākuṃ ca pṛdākvam
svajaṃ tiraścirājiṃ kasarṇīlaṃ daśonasim
indro jaghāna prathamaṃ janitāram ahe tava
teṣām u tṛhyamāṇānāṃ kaḥ svit teṣām asad rasaḥ
saṃ hi śīrṣāṇy agrabhaṃ pauñjiṣṭha iva karvaram
sindhor madhyaṃ paretya vy anijam aher viṣam
ahīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ viṣaṃ parā vahantu sindhavaḥ
hatās tiraścirājayo nipiṣṭāsaḥ pṛdākavaḥ
oṣadhīnām ahaṃ vṛṇa urvarīr iva sādhuyā
nayāmy arvatīr ivāhe niraitu viṣam
yad agnau sūrye viṣaṃ pṛthivyām oṣadhīṣu yat
kāndāviṣaṃ kanaknakaṃ niraitv aitu te viṣam
ye agnijā oṣadhijā ahīnāṃ ye apsujā vidyuta ābabhūvuḥ
yeṣāṃ jātāni bahudhā mahānti tebhyaḥ sarpebhyo namasā vidhema
taudī nāmāsi kanyā ghṛtācī nāma vā asi
adhaspadena te padam ā dade viṣadūṣaṇam
aṅgādaṅgāt pra cyāvaya hṛdayam pari varjaya
adhā viṣasya yat tejo 'vācīnaṃ tad etu te

agnir viṣam aher nir adhāt somo nir aṇayīt

sa mā jivīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā diksaṃśito manastejāḥ
diśo anu vi krame 'haṃ digbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāśāsaṃśito vātatejāḥ
āśā anu vi krame 'haṃ āśābhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā ṛksaṃśito sāmatejāḥ
ṛco 'nu vi krame 'haṃ ṛgbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā yajñasaṃśito brahmatejāḥ
yajñam anu vi krame 'haṃ yajñāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahauṣadhīsaṃśito somatejāḥ
oṣadhīr anu vi krame 'haṃ oṣadhībhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahāpsusaṃśito varuṇatejāḥ
apo 'nu vi krame 'haṃ adbhyas taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
viṣṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā kṛṣisaṃśito 'nnatejāḥ
kṛṣim anu vi krame 'haṃ kṛṣyās taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
visṇoḥ kramo 'si sapatnahā prāṇasaṃśitaḥ puruṣatejāḥ
prāṇam anu vi krame 'haṃ prāṇāt taṃ nir bhajāmo yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ vayaṃ dviṣmaḥ
sa mā jīvīt taṃ prāno jahātu
jitam asmākam udbhinnam asmākam abhy aṣṭhāṃ viśvāḥ pṛtanā arātīḥ
idam aham āmuṣyāyaṇasyāmuṣyāḥ putrasya varcas tejaḥ prāṇam āyur ni veṣṭayāmīdam enam adharāñcaṃ pādayāmi
sūryasyāvṛtam anvāvarte dakṣiṇām anv āvṛtam
sā me draviṇaṃ yachatu sā me brāhmaṇavarcasam
diśo jyotiṣmatīr abhyāvarte
tā me draviṇaṃ yachantu tā me brāhmaṇavarcasam
saptaṛṣīn abhyāvarte
te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam
brahmābhyāvarte
tan me draviṇaṃ yachantu tan me brāhmaṇavarcasam
brāhmaṇāṃ abhyāvarte
te me draviṇaṃ yachantu te me brāhmaṇavarcasam
yam vayaṃ mṛgayāmahe taṃ vadhai stṛṇavāmahai
vyātte parameṣṭhino brahmaṇāpīpadāma tam
vaiśvānarasya daṃṣṭrābhyāṃ hetis taṃ sam adhād abhi
iyaṃ taṃ psātv āhutiḥ samid devī sahīyasī
rājño varuṇasya bandho 'si
so 'mum āmuṣyāyaṇam amuṣyāḥ putram anne prāṇe badhāna
yat te annaṃ bhuvas pata ākṣiyati pṛthivīm anu
tasya nas tvaṃ bhuvas pate saṃprayacha prajāpate
apo divyā acāyiṣaṃ rasena sam apṛkṣmahi
payasvān agna āgamaṃ taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā
saṃ māgne varcasā sṛja saṃ prajayā sam āyuṣā
vidyur me asya devā indro vidyāt saha ṛṣibhiḥ
yad agne adya mithunā śapato yad vācas tṛṣṭaṃ janayanta rebhāḥ
manyor manasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān
parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parāgne rakṣo harasā śṛṇīhi
parārciṣā mūradevāṃ chṛṇīhi parāsutṛpaḥ śośucataḥ śṛṇīhi
apām asmai vajraṃ pra harāmi caturbhṛṣṭiṃ śīrṣabhidyāya vidvān
so asyāṅgāni pra śṛṇātu sarvā tan me devā anu jānantu viśve
arātīyor bhrātṛvyasya durhārdo dviṣataḥ śiraḥ
api vṛścāmy ojasā
varma mahyam ayaṃ maṇiḥ phālāj jātaḥ kariṣyati
pūrṇo manthena māgamad rasena saha varcasā
yat tvā śikvaḥ parāvadhīt takṣā hastena vāsyā
āpas tvā tasmaj jīvalāḥ punantu śucayaḥ śucim
hiraṇyasrag ayaṃ maṇiḥ śraddhāṃ yajñaṃ maho dadhat
gṛhe vasatu no 'tithiḥ
tasmai ghṛtaṃ suraṃ madhv annamannam kṣadāmahe
sa naḥ piteva putrebhyaḥ śreyaḥśreyaś cikitsatu bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvo devebhyo maṇir etya
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase
tam agniḥ praty amuñcata so asmai duha ājyaṃ bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ kadhiram ojase
tam indraḥ praty amuñcataujase vīryāya kam
so asmai balam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram kadhiram ojase
taṃ somaḥ praty amuñcata mahe śrotrāya cakṣase
so asmai varca id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvam dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugraṃ khadiram ojase
taṃ sūryaḥ praty amuñcata tenemā ajayad diśaḥ
so asmai bhūtim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir maṇiṃ phālaṃ ghṛtaścutam ugram khadiram ojase
tam bibhrac candramā maṇim asurāṇāṃ puro 'jayad dānavānāṃ hiraṇyayīḥ
so asmai śriyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
so asmai vājinam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
tenemāṃ maṇinā kṛṣim aśvināv abhi rakṣataḥ
sa bhiṣagbhyāṃ maho duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
tam bibhrat savitā maṇiṃ tenedam ajayat svaḥ
so asmai sūnṛtāṃ duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
tam āpo bibhratīr maṇiṃ sadā dhāvanty akṣitāḥ
sa ābhyo 'mṛtam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
tam rājā varuṇo maṇiṃ praty amuñcata śaṃbhuvam
so asmai satyam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
taṃ devā bibhrato maṇiṃ sarvāṃl lokān yudhājayan
sa ebhyo jitim id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir vātāya maṇim āśave
tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ praty amuñcanta śambhuvam
sa ābhyo viśvam id duhe bhūyobhūyaḥ śvaḥśvas tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
ṛtavas tam abadhnatārtavās tam abadhnata
saṃvatsaras taṃ baddhvā sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ vi rakṣati
antardeśā abadhnata pradiśas tam abadhnata
prajāpatisṛṣṭo maṇir dviṣato me 'dharāṃ akaḥ
atharvāṇo abadhnatātharvaṇā abadhnata
tair medino aṅgiraso dasyūnāṃ bibhiduḥ puras tena tvam dviṣato jahi
taṃ dhātā praty amuñcata sa bhūtaṃ vy akalpayat
tena tvaṃ dviṣato jahi
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad rasena saha varcasā
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha gobhir ajāvibhir annena prajayā saha
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat saha vrīhiyavābhyāṃ mahasā bhūtyā saha
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgaman madhor ghṛtasya dhārayā kīlālena maṇiḥ saha
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamad ūrjayā payasā saha draviṇena śriyā saha
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat tejasā tviṣyā saha yaśasā kīrtyā saha
yam abadhnād bṛhaspatir devebhyo asurakṣitim
sa māyaṃ maṇir āgamat sarvābhir bhūtibhiḥ saha
tam imaṃ devatā maṇiṃ mahyaṃ dadatu puṣṭaye
abhibhuṃ kṣatravardhanaṃ sapatnadambhanaṃ maṇim
brahmaṇā tejasā saha prati muñcāmi me śivam
asapatnaḥ sapatnahā sapatnān me 'dharāṃ akaḥ
uttaraṃ dviṣato mām ayaṃ maṇiḥ kṛṇotu devajāḥ
yasya lokā ime trayaḥ payo dugdham upāsate
sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ
yaṃ devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā upajīvanti sarvadā
sa māyam adhi rohatu maṇiḥ śraiṣṭhyāya mūrdhataḥ
yathā bījam urvarāyāṃ kṛṣṭe phālena rohati
evā mayi prajā paśavo 'nnamannaṃ vi rohatu
yasmai tvā yajñavardhana maṇe pratyamucaṃ śivam
taṃ tvaṃ śatadakṣiṇa maṇe śraiṣṭhyāya jinvatāt
etam idhmaṃ samāhitaṃ juṣaṇo agne prati harya homaiḥ
tasmin vidhema sumatiṃ svasti prajām cakṣuḥ paśūnt samiddhe jātavedasi brahmaṇā
kasminn aṅge tapo asyādhi tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅga ṛtam asyādhy āhitam
kva vrataṃ kva śraddhāsya tiṣṭhati kasminn aṅge satyam asya pratiṣṭhitam
kasmād aṅgād dīpyate agnir asya kasmād aṅgāt pavate mātariśva
kasmād aṅgād vi mimīte 'dhi candramā maha skambhasya mimāno aṅgam
kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhati bhūmir asya kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty antarikṣam
kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty āhitā dyauḥ kasminn aṅge tiṣṭhaty uttaraṃ divaḥ
kva prepsan dīpyata ūrdhvo agniḥ kva prepsan pavate mātariśvā
yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āvṛtaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
kvārdhamāsāḥ kva yanti māsāḥ saṃvatsareṇa saha saṃvidānāḥ
yatra yanty ṛtavo yatrārtavāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
kva prepsantī yuvatī virūpe ahorātre dravataḥ saṃvidāne
yatra prepsantīr abhiyanty āpaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasmint stabdhvā prajāpatir lokānt sarvāṃ adhārayat
skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yat paramam avamam yac ca madhyamaṃ prajāpatiḥ sasṛje viśvarūpam
kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra yan na prāviśat kiyat tad babhūva
kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa bhūtam kiyad bhaviṣyad anvāśaye 'sya
ekaṃ yad aṅgam akṛṇot sahasradhā kiyatā skambhaḥ pra viveśa tatra
yatra lokāmś ca kośāṃś cāpo brahma janā viduḥ
asac ca yatra sac cānta skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yatra tapaḥ parākramya vrataṃ dhārayaty uttaram
ṛtaṃ ca yatra śraddhā cāpo brahma samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasmin bhūmir antarikṣaṃ dyaur yasminn adhy āhitā
yatrāgniś candramāḥ sūryo vātas tiṣṭhanty ārpitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge sarve samāhitāḥ
skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yatra ṛṣayaḥ prathamajā ṛcaḥ sāma yajur mahī
ekarṣir yasminn ārpitaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yatrāmṛtaṃ ca mṛtyuś ca puruṣe 'dhi samāhite
samudro yasya nāḍyaḥ puruṣe 'dhi samāhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasya catasraḥ pradiśo nāḍyas tiṣṭhanti prathamāḥ
yajño yatra parākrāntaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
ye puruṣe brahma vidus te viduḥ parameṣṭhinam
yo veda parameṣṭhinaṃ yaś ca veda prajāpatim
jyeṣṭhaṃ ye brāhmaṇaṃ vidus te skambham anusaṃviduḥ
yasya śiro vaiśvānaraś cakṣur aṅgiraso 'bhavan
aṅgāni yasya yātavaḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasya brahma mukham āhur jihvāṃ madhukaśām uta
virājam ūdho yasyāhuḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasmād ṛco apātakṣan yajur yasmād apākaṣan
sāmāni yasya lomāny atharvāṅgiraso mukhaṃ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
asaccākhāṃ pratiṣṭhantīṃ paramam iva janā viduḥ
uto san manyante 'vare ye te śākhām upāsate
yatrādityāś ca rudrāś ca vasavaś ca samāhitāḥ
bhūtaṃ ca yatra bhavyaṃ ca sarve lokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
yasya trayastriṃśad devā nidhiṃ rakṣanti sarvadā
nidhiṃ tam adya ko veda yaṃ devā abhirakṣatha
yatra devā brahmavido brahma jyeṣṭham upāsate
yo vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣaṃ sa brahmā veditā syāt
bṛhanto nāma te devā ye 'sataḥ pari jajñire
ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasyāsad āhuḥ paro janāḥ
yatra skambhaḥ prajanayan purāṇaṃ vyavartayat
ekaṃ tad aṅgaṃ skambhasya purāṇam anusaṃviduḥ
yasya trayastriṃśad devā aṅge gātrā vibhejire
tān vai trayastriṃśad devān eke brahamvido viduḥ
hiraṇyagarbham paramam anatyudyaṃ janā viduḥ
skambhas tad agre prāsiñcad dhiraṇyaṃ loke antarā
skambhe lokāḥ skambhe tapaḥ skambhe 'dhy ṛtam āhitam
skambha tvā veda pratyakṣam indre sarvaṃ samāhitam
indre lokā indre tapa indre 'dhy ṛtam āhitam
indraṃ tvā veda pratyakṣaṃ skambhe sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
nāma nāmnā johavīti purā sūryāt puroṣasaḥ
yad ajaḥ prathamaṃ saṃbabhūva sa ha tat svarājyam iyāya yasmān nānyat param asti bhūtam
yasya bhūmiḥ pramāntarikṣam utodaram
divaṃ yaś cakre mūrdhānaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ
yasya sūryaś cakṣuś candramāś ca punarṇavaḥ
agniṃ yaś cakra āsyaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ
yasya vātaḥ prāṇāpānau cakṣur aṅgiraso 'bhavan
diśo yaś cakre prajñānīs tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ
skambho dādhāra dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime skambho dādhārorv antarikṣam
skambho dādhāra pradiśaḥ ṣaḍ urvīḥ skambha idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanam ā viveśa
yaḥ śramāt tapaso jāto lokānt sarvānt samānaśe
somaṃ yaś cakre kevalaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ
kathaṃ vāto nelayati kathaṃ na ramate manaḥ
kim āpaḥ satyaṃ prepsantīr nelayanti kadā cana
mahad yakṣaṃ bhuvanasya madhye tapasi krāntaṃ salilasya pṛṣṭhe
tasmin chrayante ya u ke ca devā vṛkṣasya skandhaḥ parita iva śākhāḥ
yasmai hastābhyāṃ pādābhyāṃ vācā śrotreṇa cakṣuṣā
yasmai devāḥ sadā baliṃ prayachanti vimite 'mitaṃ skambhaṃ taṃ brūhi katamaḥ svid eva saḥ
apa tasya hataṃ tamo vyāvṛttaḥ sa pāpmanā
sarvāṇi tasmin jyotīṃṣi yāni trīṇi prajāpatau
yo vetasaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ tiṣṭhantaṃ salile veda
sa vai guhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ
tantram eke yuvatī virūpe abhyākrāmaṃ vayataḥ ṣaṇmayūkham
prānyā tantūṃs tirate dhatte anyā nāpa vṛñjāte na gamāto antam
tayor ahaṃ parinṛtyantyor iva na vi jānāmi yatarā parastāt
pumān enad vayaty ud gṛṇanti pumān enad vi jabhārādhi nāke
ime mayūkhā upa tastabhur divaṃ sāmāni cakrus tasarāṇi vātave
yo bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca sarvaṃ yaś cādhitiṣṭhati
sv aryasya ca kevalaṃ tasmai jyeṣṭhāya brahmaṇe namaḥ
skambheneme viṣṭabhite dyauś ca bhūmiś ca tiṣṭhataḥ
skambha idaṃ sarvam ātmanvad yat prāṇan nimiṣac ca yat
tisro ha prajā atyāyam āyan ny anyā arkam abhito 'viśanta
bṛhan ha tasthau rajaso vimāno harito hariṇīr ā viveśa
dvādaśa pradhayaś cakram ekaṃ trīṇi nabhyāni ka u tac ciketa
tatrāhatās trīṇi śatāni śaṅkavaḥ ṣaṣṭiś ca khīlā avicācalā ye
idaṃ savitar vi jānīhi ṣaḍ yamā eka ekajaḥ
tasmin hāpitvam ichante ya eṣām eka ekajaḥ
āviḥ san nihitaṃ guhā jaran nāma mahat padam
tatredaṃ sarvam ārpitam ejat prāṇat pratiṣṭhitam
ekacakraṃ vartata ekanemi sahasrākṣaraṃ pra puro ni paścā
ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ kva tad babhūva
pañcavāhī vahatyagram eṣāṃ praṣṭayo yuktā anusaṃvahanti
ayātam asya dadṛśe na yātaṃ paraṃ nedīyo 'varaṃ davīyaḥ
tiryagbilaś camasa ūrdhvabudhnas tasmin yaśo nihitaṃ viśvarūpam
tad āsata ṛṣayaḥ sapta sākaṃ ye asya gopā mahato babhūvuḥ
yā purastād yujyate yā ca paścād yā viśvato yujyate yā ca sarvataḥ
yayā yajñaḥ prāṅ tāyate tāṃ tvā pṛchāmi katamā sā ṛcām
yad ejati patati yac ca tiṣṭhati prāṇad aprāṇan nimiṣac ca yad bhuvat
tad dādhāra pṛthivīṃ viśvarūpaṃ tat saṃbhūya bhavaty ekam eva
anantaṃ vitataṃ purutrānantam antavac cā samante
te nākapālaś carati vicinvan vidvān bhūtam uta bhavyam asya
prajāpatiś carati garbhe antar adṛśyamāno bahudhā vi jāyate
ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ katamaḥ sa ketuḥ
ūrdhvaṃ bharantam udakaṃ kumbhenevodahāryam
paśyanti sarve cakṣuṣā na sarve manasā viduḥ
dūre pūrṇena vasati dūra ūnena hīyate
mahad yakṣaṃ bhuvanasya madhye tasmai baliṃ rāṣṭrabhṛto bharanti
yataḥ sūryaḥ udety astaṃ yatra ca gachati
tad eva manye 'haṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ tad u nāty eti kiṃ cana
ye arvāṅ madhya uta vā purāṇaṃ vedaṃ vidvāṃsam abhito vadanti
ādityam eva te pari vadanti sarve agniṃ dvitīyaṃ trivṛtaṃ ca haṃsam
sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam
sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā
satyenordhvas tapati brahmaṇārvāṅ vi paśyati
prāṇena tiryaṅ prāṇati yasmin jyeṣṭham adhi śritam
yo vai te vidyād araṇī yābhyāṃ nirmathyate vasu
sa vidvān jyeṣṭhaṃ manyeta sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat
apād agre sam abhavat so agre svar ābharat
catuṣpād bhūtvā bhogyaḥ sarvam ādatta bhojanam
bhogyo bhavad atho annam adad bahu
yo devam uttarāvantam upāsātai sanātanam
sanātanam enam āhur utādya syāt punarṇavaḥ
ahorātre pra jāyete anyo anyasya rūpayoḥ
śataṃ sahasram ayutaṃ nyarbudam asaṃkhyeyaṃ svam asmin niviṣṭam
tad asya ghnanty abhipaśyata eva tasmād devo rocat eṣa etat
bālād ekam aṇīyaskam utaikaṃ neva dṛśyate
tataḥ pariṣvajīyasī devatā sā mama priyā
iyaṃ kalyāṇy ajarā martyasyāmṛtā gṛhe
yasmai kṛtā śaye sa yaś cakāra jajāra saḥ
tvaṃ strī tvaṃ pumān asi tvaṃ kumāra uta vā kumārī
tvaṃ jīrṇo daṇḍena vañcasi tvaṃ jāto bhavasi viśvatomukhaḥ
utaiṣāṃ pitota vā putra eṣām utaiṣāṃ jyeṣṭha uta vā kaniṣṭhaḥ
eko ha devo manasi praviṣṭaḥ prathamo jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ
pūrṇāt pūrṇam ud acati pūrṇaṃ pūrṇena sicyate
uto tad adya vidyāma yatas tat pariṣicyate
eṣā sanatnī sanam eva jātaiṣā purāṇī pari sarvaṃ babhūva
mahī devy uṣaso vibhātī saikenaikena miṣatā vi caṣṭe
avir vai nāma devatartenāste parīvṛtā
tasyā rūpeṇeme vṛkṣā haritā haritasrajaḥ
anti santaṃ na jahāty anti santaṃ na paśyati
devasya paśya kāvyaṃ na mamāra na jīryati
apūrveṇeṣitā vācas tā vadanti yathāyatham
vadantīr yatra gachanti tad āhur brāhmaṇaṃ mahat
yatra devāś ca manuṣyāś cārā nābhāv iva śritāḥ
apāṃ tvā puṣpaṃ pṛchāmi yatra tan māyayā hitam
yebhir vāta iṣitaḥ pravāti ye dadante pañca diśaḥ sadhrīcīḥ
ya āhutim atyamanyanta devā apāṃ netāraḥ katame ta āsan
imām eṣāṃ pṛthivīṃ vasta eko 'ntarikṣaṃ pary eko babhūva
divam eṣāṃ dadate yo vidhartā viśvā āśāḥ prati rakṣanty eke
yo vidyāt sūtraṃ vitataṃ yasminn otāḥ prajā imāḥ
sūtraṃ sūtrasya yo vidyād sa vidyād brāhmaṇaṃ mahat
vedāhaṃ sūtraṃ vitataṃ yasminn otāḥ prajā imāḥ
sūtraṃ sūtrasyāhaṃ vedātho yad brāhmaṇaṃ mahad
yad antarā dyāvāpṛthivī agnir ait pradahan viśvadāvyaḥ
yatrātiṣṭhann ekapatnīḥ parastāt kvevāsīn mātariśvā tadānīm
apsv āsīn mātariśvā praviṣṭaḥ praviṣṭā devāḥ salilāny āsan
bṛhan ha tasthau rajaso vimānaḥ pavamāno harita ā viveśa
uttareṇeva gayatrīm amṛte 'dhi vi cakrame
sāmnā ye sāma saṃvidur ajas tad dadṛśe kva
niveśanaḥ saṃgamano vasūnāṃ deva iva savitā satyadharmā
indro na tasthau samare dhanānām
puṇḍarīkaṃ navadvāraṃ tribhir guṇebhir āvṛtam
tasmin yad yakṣam ātmanvat tad vai brahmavido viduḥ
akāmo dhīro amṛtaḥ svayaṃbhū rasena tṛpto na kutaś canonaḥ
tam eva vidvān na bibhāya mṛtyor ātmānaṃ dhīram ajaraṃ yuvānam
aghāyatām api nahyā mukhāni sapatneṣu vajram arpayaitam
indreṇa dattā prathamā śataudanā bhrātṛvyaghnī yajamānasya gātuḥ
vediṣ ṭe carma bhavatu barhir lomāni yāni te
eṣā tvā raśanāgrabhīd grāvā tvaiṣo 'dhi nṛtyatu
bālās te prokṣaṇīḥ santu jīhvā saṃ mārṣṭu aghnye
śuddhā tvaṃ yajñiyā bhūtvā divaṃ prehi śataudane
yaḥ śataudanāṃ pacati kāmapreṇa sa kalpate
prītā hy asya ṛtvijaḥ sarve yanti yathāyatham
sa svargam ā rohati yatrādas tridivaṃ divaḥ
apūpanābhiṃ kṛtvā yo dadāti śataudanām
sa tāṃl lokānt sam āpnoti ye divyā ye ca pārthivāḥ
hiraṇyajyotiṣaṃ kṛtvā yo dadāti śataudanām
ye te devi śamitāraḥ paktāro ye ca te janāḥ
te tvā sarve gopsyanti maibhyo bhaiṣīḥ śataudane
vasavas tvā dakṣiṇata uttarān marutas tvā
ādityāḥ paścād gopsyanti sāgniṣṭomam ati drava
devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye
te tvā sarve gopsyanti sātirātram ati drava
antarikṣaṃ divaṃ bhūmim ādityān maruto diśaḥ
lokānt sa sarvān āpnoti yo dadāti śataudanām
ghṛtaṃ prokṣantī subhagā devī devān gamiṣyati
paktāram aghnye mā hiṃsīr divaṃ prehi śataudane
ye devā diviṣado antarikṣasadaś ca ye ye ceme bhūmyām adhi
tebhyas tvaṃ dhukṣva sarvadā kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te śiro yat te mukhaṃ yau karṇau ye ca te hanū
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yau ta oṣṭhau ye nāsike ye śṛṅge ye ca te 'kṣiṇī
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te klomā yad dhṛdayaṃ purītat sahakaṇṭhikā
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te yakṛd ye matasne yad āntram yāś ca te gudāḥ
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yas te plāśir yo vaniṣṭhur yau kukṣī yac ca carma te
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te majjā yad asthi yan maṃsaṃ yac ca lohitam
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yau te bāhū ye doṣaṇī yāv aṃsau yā ca te kakut
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yās te grīvā ye skandhā yāḥ pṛṣṭīr yāś ca parśavaḥ
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yau ta urū aṣṭhīvantau ye śroṇī yā ca te bhasat
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te puchaṃ ye te bālā yad ūdho ye ca te stanāḥ
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yās te jaṅghāḥ yāḥ kuṣṭhikā ṛcharā ye ca te śaphāḥ
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
yat te carma śataudane yāni lomāny aghnye
āmikṣāṃ duhratāṃ dātre kṣīraṃ sarpir atho madhu
kroḍau te stāṃ purodāśāv ājyenābhighāritau
tau pakṣau devi kṛtvā sā paktāraṃ divaṃ vaha
ulūkhale musale yaś ca carmaṇi yo vā śūrpe taṇḍulaḥ kaṇaḥ
yaṃ vā vāto mātariśvā pavamāno mamāthāgniṣ ṭad dhotā suhutaṃ kṛṇotu
apo devīr madhumatīr ghṛtaścuto brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi
yatkāma idam abhiṣiñcāmi vo 'haṃ tan me sarvaṃ saṃ padyatāṃ vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām
namas te jāyamānāyai jātāyā uta te namaḥ
bālebhyaḥ śaphebhyo rūpāyāghnye te namaḥ
yo vidyāt sapta pravataḥ sapta vidyāt parāvataḥ
śiro yajñasya yo vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt
vedāhaṃ sapta pravataḥ sapta veda parāvataḥ
śiro yajñasyāhaṃ veda somaṃ cāsyāṃ vicakṣaṇam
yayā dyaur yayā pṛthivī yayāpo gupitā imāḥ
vaśāṃ sahasradhārāṃ brahmaṇāchāvadāmasi
śataṃ kaṃsāḥ śataṃ dogdhāraḥ śataṃ goptāro adhi pṛṣṭhe asyāḥ
ye devās tasyāṃ prāṇanti te vaśāṃ vidur ekadhā
yajñapadīrākṣīrā svadhāprāṇā mahīlukā
vaśā parjanyapatnī devāṃ apy eti brahmaṇā
anu tvāgniḥ prāviśad anu somo vaśe tvā
ūdhas te bhadre parjanyo vidyutas te stanā vaśe
apas tvaṃ dhukṣe prathamā urvarā aparā vaśe
tṛtīyaṃ rāṣṭraṃ dhukṣe 'nnaṃ kṣīraṃ vaśe tvam
yad ādityair hūyamānopātiṣṭha ṛtavari
indraḥ sahasraṃ pātrānt somaṃ tvāpāyayad vaśe
yad anūcīndram air āt tvā ṛṣabho 'hvayat
tasmāt te vṛtrahā payaḥ kṣīraṃ kruddho 'harad vaśe
yat te kruddho dhanapatir ā kṣīram aharad vaśe
idaṃ tad adya nākas triṣu pātreṣu rakṣati
triṣu pātreṣu taṃ somam ā devy aharad vaśā
atharvā yatra dīkṣito barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye
saṃ hi somenāgata sam u sarveṇa padvatā
vaśā samudram adhy aṣṭhad gandharvaiḥ kalibhiḥ saha
saṃ hi vātenāgata sam u sarvaiḥ patatribhiḥ
vaśā samudre prānṛtyad ṛcaḥ sāmāni bibhratī
saṃ hi sūryeṇāgata sam u sarveṇa cakṣuṣā
vaśā samudram aty akhyad bhadrā jyotīṃṣi bibhratī
abhīvṛtā hiraṇyena yad atiṣṭha ṛtāvari
aśvaḥ samudro bhūtvādhy askandad vaśe tvā
tad bhadrāḥ sam agachanta vaśā deṣṭry atho svadhā
atharvā yatra dīkṣito barhiṣy āsta hiraṇyaye
vaśā mātā rājanyasya vaśā mātā svadhe tava
vaśāyā yajña āyudhaṃ tataś cittam ajāyata
ūrdhvo bindur ud acarad brahmaṇaḥ kakudād adhi
tatas tvaṃ jajñiṣe vaśe tato hotājāyata
āsnas te gāthā abhavann uṣṇihābhyo balaṃ vaśe
pājasyāj jajñe yajña stanebhyo raśmayas tava
īrmābhyām ayanaṃ jātaṃ sakthibhyāṃ ca vaśe tava
āntrebhyo jajñire atrā udarād adhi vīrudhaḥ
yad udaraṃ varuṇasyānuprāviśathā vaśe
tatas tvā brahmod ahvayat sa hi netram avet tava
sarve garbhād avepanta jāyamānād asūsvaḥ
sasūva hi tām āhu vaśeti brahmabhiḥ kḷptaḥ sa hy asyā bandhuḥ
yudha ekaḥ saṃ sṛjati yo asyā eka id vaśī
tarāṃsi yajñā abhavan tarasāṃ cakṣur abhavad vaśā
vaśā yajñaṃ praty agṛhṇād vaśā sūryam adhārayat
vaśāyām antar aviśad odano brahmaṇā saha
vaśām evāmṛtam āhur vaśāṃ mṛtyum upāsate
vaśedaṃ sarvam abhavad devā manuṣyā asurāḥ pitara ṛṣayaḥ
ya evaṃ vidyāt sa vaśāṃ prati gṛhṇīyāt
tathā hi yajñaḥ sarvapād duhe dātre 'napasphuran
tisro jihvā varuṇasyāntar dīdyaty āsani
tāsāṃ yā madhye rājati sā vaśā duṣpratigrahā
caturdhā reto abhavad vaśāyāḥ
āpas turīyam amṛtaṃ turīyaṃ yajñas turīyaṃ paśavas turīyam
vaśā dyaur vaśā pṛthivī vaśā viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiḥ
vaśāyā dugdham apibant sādhyā vasavaś ca ye
vaśāyā dugdhaṃ pītvā sādhyā vasavaś ca ye
te vai bradhnasya viṣṭapi payo asyā upāsate
somam enām eke duhre ghṛtam eka upāsate
ya evaṃ viduṣe vaśāṃ dadus te gatās tridivaṃ divaḥ
brāhmaṇebhyo vaśāṃ dattvā sarvāṃl lokānt sam aśnute
ṛtaṃ hy asyām ārpitam api brahmātho tapaḥ
vaśāṃ devā upa jīvanti vaśāṃ manuṣyā uta
vaśedaṃ sarvam abhavad yāvat sūryo vipaśyati
agne jāyasvāditir nāthiteyaṃ brahmaudanaṃ pacati putrakāmā
saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛtas te tvā manthantu prajayā saheha
kṛṇuta dhūmaṃ vṛṣaṇaḥ sakhāyo 'droghāvitā vācam acha
ayam agniḥ pṛtanāṣāṭ suvīro yena devā asahanta dasyūn
agne 'janiṣṭhā mahate vīryāya brahmaudanāya paktave jātavedaḥ
saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛtas te tvājījanann asyai rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha
samiddho agne samidhā sam idhyasva vidvān devān yajñiyāṃ eha vakṣaḥ
tebhyo haviḥ śrapayaṃ jātaveda uttamaṃ nākam adhi rohayemam
tredhā bhāgo nihito yaḥ purā vo devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ martyānām
aṃśāṃ jānīdhvaṃ vi bhajāmi tān vo yo devānāṃ sa imāṃ pārayāti
agne sahasvān abhibhūr abhīd asi nīco ny ubja dviṣataḥ sapatnān
iyaṃ mātrā mīyamānā mitā ca sajātāṃs te balihṛtaḥ kṛṇotu
sākaṃ sajātaiḥ payasā sahaidhy ud ubjaināṃ mahate vīryāya
ūrdhvo nākasyādhi roha viṣṭapaṃ svargo loka iti yaṃ vadanti
iyaṃ mahī prati gṛhṇātu carma pṛthivī devī sumanasyamānā
atha gachema sukṛtasya lokam
etau grāvāṇau sayujā yuṅdhi carmaṇi nirbindhy aṃśūn yajamānāya sādhu
avaghnatī ni jahi ya imāṃ pṛtanyava ūrdhvaṃ prajām udbharanty ud ūha
gṛhāṇa grāvāṇau sakṛtau vīra hasta ā te devā yajñiyā yajñam aguḥ
trayo varā yatamāṃs tvaṃ vṛṇīṣe tās te samṛddhīr iha rādhayāmi
iyaṃ te dhītir idam u te janitraṃ gṛhṇātu tvām aditiḥ śūraputrā
parā punīhi ya imāṃ pṛtanyavo 'syai rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ ni yacha
upaśvase druvaye sīdatā yūyaṃ vi vicyadhvaṃ yajñiyāsas tuṣaiḥ
śriyā samānān ati sarvānt syāmādhaspadaṃ dviṣatas pādayāmi
parehi nāri punar ehi kṣipram apāṃ tvā goṣṭho adhy arukṣad bharāya
tāsāṃ gṛhṇītād yatamā yajñiyā asan vibhājya dhīrītarā jahītāt
emā agur yoṣitaḥ śumbhamānā ut tiṣṭha nāri tavasaṃ rabhasva
supatnī patyā prajayā prajāvaty ā tvāgan yajñaḥ prati kumbhaṃ gṛbhāya
ūrjo bhāgo nihito yaḥ purā va ṛṣipraśiṣṭāpa ā bharaitāḥ
ayaṃ yajño gātuvin nāthavit prajāvid ugraḥ paśuvid vīravid vo astu
agne carur yajñiyas tvādhy arukṣac chucis tapiṣṭhas tapasā tapainam
ārṣeyā daivā abhisaṃgatya bhāgam imaṃ tapiṣṭhā ṛtubhis tapantu
śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā āpaś carum ava sarpantu śubhrāḥ
aduḥ prajāṃ bahulāṃ paśūn naḥ paktaudanasya sukṛtām etu lokam
brahmaṇā śuddhā uta pūtā ghṛtena somasyāṃśavas taṇḍulā yajñiyā ime
apaḥ pra viśata prati gṛhṇātu vaś carur imaṃ paktvā sukṛtām eta lokam
uruḥ prathasva mahatā mahimnā sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ sukṛtasya loke
pitāmahāḥ pitaraḥ prajopajāhaṃ paktā pañcadaśas te asmi
sahasrapṛṣṭhaḥ śatadhāro akṣito brahmaudano devayānaḥ svargaḥ
amūṃs ta ā dadhāmi prajayā reṣayainān balihārāya mṛḍatān mahyam eva
udehi vediṃ prajayā vardhayaināṃ nudasva rakṣaḥ prataraṃ dhehy enām
śriyā samānān ati sarvānt syāmādhaspadaṃ dviṣatas pādayāmi
abhyāvartasva paśubhiḥ sahaināṃ pratyaṅṅ enāṃ devatābhiḥ sahaidhi
mā tvā prāpac chapatho mābhicāraḥ sve kṣetre anamīvā vi rāja
ṛtena taṣṭā manasā hitaiṣā brahmaudanasya vihitā vedir agre
aṃsadhrīṃ śuddhām upa dhehi nāri tatraudanaṃ sādaya daivānām
aditer hastāṃ srucam etāṃ dvitīyāṃ saptaṛṣayo bhūtakṛto yām akṛṇvan
sā gātrāṇi viduṣy odanasya darvir vedyām adhy enaṃ cinotu
śṛtaṃ tvā havyam upa sīdantu daivā niḥsṛpyāgneḥ punar enān pra sīda
somena pūto jaṭhare sīda brahmaṇām ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ
soma rājant saṃjñānam ā vapaibhyaḥ subrāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān
ṛṣīn ārṣeyāṃs tapaso 'dhi jātān brahmaudane suhavā johavīmi
śuddhāḥ pūtā yoṣito yajñiyā imā brahmaṇāṃ hasteṣu prapṛthak sādayāmi
yatkāma idam abhiṣiñcāmi vo 'ham indro marutvānt sa dadād idaṃ me
idaṃ me jyotir amṛtaṃ hiraṇyaṃ pakvaṃ kṣetrāt kāmadughā ma eṣā
idaṃ dhanaṃ ni dadhe brāhmaṇeṣu kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ
agnau tuṣān ā vapa jātavedasi paraḥ kambūkāṃ apa mṛḍḍhi dūram
etaṃ śuśruma gṛharājasya bhāgam atho vidma nirṛter bhāgadheyam
śrāmyataḥ pacato viddhi sunvataḥ panthāṃ svargam adhi rohayainam
yena rohāt param āpadya yad vaya uttamaṃ nākaṃ paramaṃ vyoma
babhrer adhvaryo mukham etad vi mṛḍḍhy ājyāya lokaṃ kṛṇuhi pravidvān
ghṛtena gātrānu sarvā vi mṛḍḍhi kṛṇve panthāṃ pitṛṣu yaḥ svargaḥ
babhre rakṣaḥ samadam ā vapaibhyo 'brāhmaṇā yatame tvopasīdān
purīṣiṇaḥ prathamānāḥ purastād ārṣeyās te mā riṣan prāśitāraḥ
ārṣeyeṣu ni dadha odana tvā nānārṣeyāṇām apy asty atra
agnir me goptā marutaś ca sarve viśve devā abhi rakṣantu pakvam
yajñaṃ duhānaṃ sadam it prapīnaṃ pumāṃsaṃ dhenuṃ sadanaṃ rayīṇām
prajāmṛtatvam uta dīrgham āyū rāyaś ca poṣair upa tvā sadema
vṛṣabho 'si svarga ṛṣīn ārṣeyān gacha
sukṛtāṃ loke sīda tatra nau saṃskṛtam
samācinuṣvānusaṃprayāhy agne pathaḥ kalpaya devayānān
etaiḥ sukṛtair anu gachema yajñaṃ nāke tiṣṭhantam adhi saptaraśmau
yena devā jyotiṣā dyām udāyan brahmaudanaṃ paktvā sukṛtasya lokam
tena geṣma sukṛtasya lokaṃ svar ārohanto abhi nākam uttamam
bhavāśarvau mṛḍataṃ mābhi yātaṃ bhūtapatī paśupatī namo vām
pratihitām āyatāṃ mā vi srāṣṭaṃ mā no hiṃsiṣṭaṃ dvipado mā catuṣpadaḥ
śune kroṣṭre mā śarīrāṇi kartam aliklavebhyo gṛdhrebhyo ye ca kṛṣṇā aviṣyavaḥ
makṣikās te paśupate vayāṃsi te vighase mā vidanta
krandāya te prāṇāya yāś ca te bhava ropayaḥ
namas te rudra kṛṇmaḥ sahasrākṣāyāmartya
purastāt te namaḥ kṛṇma uttarād adharād uta
abhīvargād divas pary antarikṣāya te namaḥ
mukhāya te paśupate yāni cakṣūṃṣi te bhava
tvace rūpāya saṃdṛśe pratīcīnāya te namaḥ
aṅgebhyas ta udarāya jihvāyā āsyāya te
dadbhyo gandhāya te namaḥ
astrā nīlaśikhaṇḍena sahasrākṣeṇa vājinā
rudreṇārdhakaghātinā tena mā sam arāmahi
sa no bhavaḥ pari vṛṇaktu viśvata āpa ivāgniḥ pari vṛṇaktu no bhavaḥ
mā no 'bhi māṃsta namo astv asmai
catur namo aṣṭakṛtvo bhavāya daśa kṛtvaḥ paśupate namas te
taveme pañca paśavo vibhaktā gāvo aśvāḥ puruṣā ajāvayaḥ
tava catasraḥ pradiśas tava dyaus tava pṛthivī tavedam ugrorv antarikṣam
tavedaṃ sarvam ātmanvad yat prāṇat pṛthivīm anu
uruḥ kośo vasudhānas tavāyaṃ yasminn imā viśvā bhuvanāny antaḥ
sa no mṛḍa paśupate namas te paraḥ kroṣṭāro abhibhāḥ śvānaḥ paro yantv agharudo vikeśyaḥ
dhanur bibharṣi haritaṃ hiraṇyayaṃ sahasraghniṃ śatavadhaṃ śikhaṇḍin
rudrasyeṣuś carati devahetis tasyai namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ
yo 'bhiyāto nilayate tvāṃ rudra nicikīrṣati
paścād anuprayuṅkṣe taṃ viddhasya padanīr iva
bhavārudrau sayujā saṃvidānāv ubhāv ugrau carato vīryāya
tābhyāṃ namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ
namas te astv āyate namo astu parāyate
namas te rudra tiṣṭhata āsīnāyota te namaḥ
namaḥ sāyaṃ namaḥ prātar namo rātryā namo divā
bhavāya ca śarvāya cobhābhyām akaraṃ namaḥ
sahasrākṣam atipaśyaṃ purastād rudram asyantaṃ bahudhā vipaścitam
mopārāma jihvayeyamānam
śyāvāśvaṃ kṛṣṇam asitaṃ mṛṇantaṃ bhīmaṃ rathaṃ keśinaḥ pādayantam
pūrve pratīmo namo astv asmai
mā no 'bhi srā matyaṃ devahetiṃ mā naḥ krudhaḥ paśupate namas te
anyatrāsmad divyāṃ śākhāṃ vi dhūnu
mā no hiṃsīr adhi no brūhi pari ṇo vṛṅdhi mā krudhaḥ
mā tvayā sam arāmahi
mā no goṣu puruṣeṣu mā gṛdho no ajāviṣu
anyatrogra vi vartaya piyārūṇāṃ prajāṃ jahi
yasya takmā kāsikā hetir ekam aśvasyeva vṛṣaṇaḥ kranda eti
abhipūrvaṃ nirṇayate namo astv asmai
yo 'ntarikṣe tiṣṭhati viṣṭabhito 'yajvanaḥ pramṛṇan devapīyūn
tasmai namo daśabhiḥ śakvarībhiḥ
tubhyam āraṇyāḥ paśavo mṛgā vane hitā haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi
tava yakṣaṃ paśupate apsv antas tubhyaṃ kṣaranti divyā āpo vṛdhe
śiṃśumārā ajagarāḥ purīkayā jaṣā matsyā rajasā yebhyo asyasi
na te dūraṃ na pariṣṭhāsti te bhava sadyaḥ sarvāṃ pari paśyasi bhūmiṃ pūrvasmād dhaṃsy uttarasmint samudre
mā no rudra takmanā mā viṣeṇa mā naḥ saṃ srā divyenāgninā
anyatrāsmad vidyutaṃ pātayaitām
bhavo divo bhava īśe pṛthivyā bhava ā papra urv antarikṣam
tasyai namo yatamasyāṃ diśītaḥ
bhava rājan yajamānāya mṛḍa paśūnāṃ hi paśupatir babhūtha
yaḥ śraddadhāti santi devā iti catuṣpade dvipade 'sya mṛḍa
mā no mahāntam uta mā no arbhakaṃ mā no vahantam uta mā no vakṣyataḥ
mā no hiṃsīḥ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca svāṃ tanvaṃ rudra mā rīriṣo naḥ
rudrasyailabakārebhyo 'saṃsūktagilebhyaḥ
idaṃ mahāsyebhyaḥ śvabhyo akaraṃ namaḥ
namas te ghoṣiṇībhyo namas te keśinībhyaḥ
namo namaskṛtābhyo namaḥ saṃbhuñjatībhyaḥ
namas te deva senābhyaḥ svasti no abhayaṃ ca naḥ
tasyaudanasya bṛhaspatiḥ śiro brahma mukham
dyāvāpṛthivī śrotre sūryācandramasāv akṣiṇī saptaṛṣayaḥ prāṇāpānāḥ
cakṣur musalaṃ kāma ulūkhalam
ditiḥ śūrpam aditiḥ śūrpagrāhī vāto 'pāvinak
aśvāḥ kaṇā gāvas taṇḍulā maśakās tuṣāḥ
kabru phalīkaraṇāḥ śaro 'bhram
śyāmam ayo 'sya māṃsāni lohitam asya lohitam
trapu bhasma haritaṃ varṇaḥ puṣkaram asya gandhaḥ
khalaḥ pātraṃ sphyāv aṃsāv īṣe anūkye
āntrāṇi jatravo gudā varatrāḥ
iyam eva pṛthivī kumbhī bhavati rādhyamānasyaudanasya dyaur apidhānam
sītāḥ parśavaḥ sikatā ūbadhyam
ṛtaṃ hastāvanejanaṃ kulyopasecanam
ṛcā kumbhy adhihitārtvijyena preṣitā
brahmaṇā parigṛhītā sāmnā paryūḍhā
bṛhad āyavanaṃ rathantaraṃ darviḥ
ṛtavaḥ paktāra ārtavāḥ sam indhate
caruṃ pañcabilam ukhaṃ gharmo 'bhīndhe
odanena yajñavataḥ sarve lokāḥ samāpyāḥ
yasmint samudro dyaur bhūmis trayo 'varaparaṃ śritāḥ
yasya devā akalpantocchiṣṭe ṣaḍ aśītayaḥ
taṃ tvaudanasya pṛchāmi yo asya mahimā mahān
sa ya odanasya mahimānaṃ vidyāt
nālpa iti brūyān nānupasecana iti nedaṃ ca kiṃ ceti
yāvad dātābhimanasyeta tan nāti vadet
brahmavādino vadanti parāñcam odanaṃ prāśī3ḥ pratyañcā3m iti
tvam odanaṃ prāśī3s tvām odanā3 iti
parāñcaṃ cainaṃ prāśīḥ prāṇās tvā hāsyantīty enam āha
pratyañcaṃ cainaṃ prāśīr apānās tvā hāsyantīty enam āha
naivāham odanaṃ na mām odanaḥ
odana evaudanaṃ prāśīt
tataś cainam anyena śīrṣṇā prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
jyeṣṭhatas te prajā mariṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
bṛhaspatinā śīrṣṇā
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ śrotrābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
badhiro bhaviṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ śrotrābhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyām akṣībhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
andho bhaviṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
sūryācandramasābhyām akṣībhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyena mukhena prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
mukhatas te prajā mariṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
brahmaṇā mukhena
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyayā jihvayā prāśīr yayā caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
jihvā te mariṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
agner jihvayā
tayainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tayainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyair dantaiḥ prāśīr yaiś caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
dantās te śatsyantīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
ṛtubhir dantaiḥ
tair enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tair enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyaiḥ prāṇāpānaiḥ prāśīr yaiś caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
prāṇāpānās tvā hāsyantīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
saptaṛṣibhiḥ prāṇāpānaiḥ
tair enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tair enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyena vyacasā prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
rājayakṣmas tvā haniṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
antarikṣeṇa vyacasā
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyena pṛṣṭhena prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
vidyut tvā haniṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
divā pṛṣṭhena
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyenorasā prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
kṛṣyā na rātsyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
pṛthivyorasā
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyenodareṇa prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
udaradāras tvā haniṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
satyenodareṇa
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyena vastinā prāśīr yena caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
apsu mariṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
samudreṇa vastinā
tenainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tenainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyām ūrubhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
ūrū te mariṣyata ity enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
mitrāvaruṇayor ūrubhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyām aṣṭhīvadbhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
srāmo bhaviṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
tvaṣṭur aṣṭhīvadbhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ pādābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
bahucārī bhaviṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
aśvinoḥ pādābhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ prapadābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
sarpas tvā haniṣyatīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
savituḥ prapadābhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyābhyāṃ hastābhyāṃ prāśīr yābhyāṃ caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
brāhmaṇaṃ haniṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
ṛtasya hastābhyām
tābhyām enaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tābhyām enam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tataś cainam anyayā pratiṣṭhayā prāśīr yayā caitaṃ pūrva ṛṣayaḥ prāśnan
apratiṣṭhāno 'nāyatano mariṣyasīty enam āha
taṃ vā ahaṃ nārvāñcaṃ na parāñcaṃ na pratyañcam
satye pratiṣṭhāya
tayainaṃ prāśiṣaṃ tayainam ajīgamam
eṣa vā odanaḥ sarvāṅgaḥ sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ
sarvāṅga eva sarvaparuḥ sarvatanūḥ saṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
etad vai bradhnasya viṣṭapaṃ yad odanaḥ
bradhnaloko bhavati bradhnasya viṣṭapi śrayate ya evaṃ veda
etasmād vā odanāt trayastriṃśataṃ lokān nir amimīta prajāpatiḥ
teṣāṃ prajñānāya yajñam asṛjata
sa ya evaṃ viduṣa upadraṣṭā bhavati prāṇaṃ ruṇaddhi
na ca prāṇaṃ ruṇaddhi sarvajyāniṃ jīyate
na ca sarvajyāniṃ jīyate purainaṃ jarasaḥ prāṇo jahāti
prāṇāya namo yasya sarvam idaṃ vaśe
yo bhūtaḥ sarvasyeśvaro yasmint sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
namas te prāṇa krandāya namas te stanayitnave
namas te prāṇa vidyute namas te prāṇa varṣate
yat prāṇa stanayitnunābhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ
pra vīyante garbhān dadhate 'tho bahvīr vi jāyante
yat prāṇa ṛtāv āgate 'bhikrandaty oṣadhīḥ
sarvaṃ tadā pra modate yat kiṃ ca bhūmyām adhi
yadā prāṇo abhyavarṣīd varṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ mahīm
paśavas tat pra modante maho vai no bhaviṣyati
abhivṛṣṭā oṣadhayaḥ prāṇena sam avādiran
āyur vai naḥ prātītaraḥ sarvā naḥ surabhīr akaḥ
namas te astv āyate namo astu parāyate
namas te prāṇa tiṣṭhata āsīnāyota te namaḥ
namas te prāṇa prāṇate namo astv apānate
parācīnāya te namaḥ pratīcīnāya te namaḥ sarvasmai ta idaṃ namaḥ
yā te prāṇa priyā tanūr yo te prāṇa preyasī
atho yad bheṣajaṃ tava tasya no dhehi jīvase
prāṇaḥ prajā anu vaste pitā putram iva priyam
prāṇo ha sarvasyeśvaro yac ca prāṇati yac ca na
prāṇo mṛtyuḥ prāṇas takmā prāṇaṃ devā upāsate
prāṇo ha satyavādinam uttame loka ā dadhat
prāṇo virāṭ prāṇo deṣṭrī prāṇaṃ sarva upāsate
prāṇo ha sūryaś candramāḥ prāṇam āhuḥ prajāpatim
prāṇāpānau vrīhiyavāv anaḍvān prāṇa ucyate
yave ha prāṇa āhito 'pāno vrīhir ucyate
apānati prāṇati puruṣo garbhe antarā
yadā tvaṃ prāṇa jinvasy atha sa jāyate punaḥ
prāṇam āhur mātariśvānaṃ vāto ha prāṇa ucyate
prāṇe ha bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ ca prāṇe sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
ātharvaṇīr āṅgirasīr daivīr manuṣyajā uta
oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante yadā tvaṃ prāṇa jinvasi
yadā prāṇo abhyavarṣīd varṣeṇa pṛthivīṃ mahīm
oṣadhayaḥ pra jāyante 'tho yāḥ kāś ca vīrudhaḥ
yas te prāṇedaṃ veda yasmiṃś cāsi pratiṣṭhitaḥ
sarve tasmai baliṃ harān amuṣmiṃl loka uttame
yathā prāṇa balihṛtas tubhyaṃ sarvāḥ prajā imāḥ
evā tasmai baliṃ harān yas tvā śṛṇavat suśravaḥ
antar garbhaś carati devatāsv ābhūto bhūtaḥ sa u jāyate punaḥ
sa bhūto bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyat pitā putraṃ pra viveśā śacībhiḥ
ekaṃ pādaṃ not khidati salilād dhaṃsa uccaran
yad aṅga sa tam utkhiden naivādya na śvaḥ syāt
na rātrī nāhaḥ syān na vy uchet kadā cana
aṣṭācakraṃ vartata ekanemi sahasrākṣaraṃ pra puro ni paścā
ardhena viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna yad asyārdhaṃ katamaḥ sa ketuḥ
yo asya viśvajanmana īśe viśvasya ceṣṭataḥ
anyeṣu kṣipradhanvane tasmai prāṇa namo 'stu te
yo asya sarvajanmana īśe sarvasya ceṣṭataḥ
atandro brahmaṇā dhīraḥ prāṇo mānu tiṣṭhatu
ūrdhvaḥ supteṣu jāgāra nanu tiryaṅ ni padyate
na suptam asya supteṣv anu śuśrāva kaś cana
prāṇa mā mat paryāvṛto na mad anyo bhaviṣyasi
apāṃ garbham iva jīvase prāṇa badhnāmi tvā mayi
brahmacārīṣṇaṃś carati rodasī ubhe tasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavanti
sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca sa ācāryaṃ tapasā piparti
brahmacāriṇaṃ pitaro devajanāḥ pṛthag devā anusaṃyanti sarve
gandharvā enam anv āyan trayastriṃśat triśatāḥ ṣaṭsahasrāḥ sarvānt sa devāṃs tapasā piparti
ācārya upanayamāno brahmacāriṇaṃ kṛṇute garbham antaḥ
taṃ rātrīs tisra udare bibharti taṃ jātaṃ draṣṭum abhisaṃyanti devāḥ
iyaṃ samit pṛthivī dyaur dvitīyotāntarikṣaṃ samidhā pṛṇāti
brahmacārī samidhā mekhalayā śrameṇa lokāṃs tapasā piparti
pūrvo jāto brahmaṇo brahmacārī gharmaṃ vasānas tapasod atiṣṭhat
tasmāj jātaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brahma jyeṣṭhaṃ devāś ca sarve amṛtena sākam
brahmacāry eti samidhā samiddhaḥ kārṣṇaṃ vasāno dīkṣito dīrghaśmaśruḥ
sa sadya eti pūrvasmād uttaraṃ samudraṃ lokānt saṃgṛbhya muhur ācarikrat
brahmacārī janayan brahmāpo lokaṃ prajāpatiṃ parameṣṭhinaṃ virājam
garbho bhūtvāmṛtasya yonāv indro ha bhūtvāsurāṃs tatarha
ācāryas tatakṣa nabhasī ubhe ime urvī gambhīre pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca
te rakṣati tapasā brahmacārī tasmin devāḥ saṃmanaso bhavanti
imāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ brahmacārī bhikṣām ā jabhāra prathamo divaṃ ca
te kṛtvā samidhāv upāste tayor ārpitā bhuvanāni viśvā
arvāg anyaḥ paro anyo divas pṛṣṭhād guhā nidhī nihitau brāhmaṇasya
tau rakṣati tapasā brahmacārī tat kevalaṃ kṛṇute brahma vidvān
arvāg anya ito anyaḥ pṛthivyā agnī sameto nabhasī antareme
tayoḥ śrayante raśmayo 'dhi dṛḍhās tān ā tiṣṭhati tapasā brahmacārī
abhikrandan stanayann aruṇaḥ śitiṅgo bṛhac chepo 'nu bhūmau jabhāra
brahmacārī siñcati sānau retaḥ pṛthivyāṃ tena jīvanti pradiśaś catasraḥ
agnau sūrye candramasi mātariśvan brahmacāry apsu samidham ā dadhāti
tāsām arcīṃṣi pṛthag abhre caranti tāsām ājyaṃ puruṣo varṣam āpaḥ
ācāryo mṛtyur varuṇaḥ soma oṣadhayaḥ payaḥ
jīmūtā āsant satvānas tair idaṃ svar ābhṛtam
amā ghṛtaṃ kṛṇute kevalam ācāryo bhūtvā varuṇaḥ
yadyad aichat prajāpatau tad brahmacārī prāyachat svān mitro adhy ātmanaḥ
ācāryo brahmacārī brahmacārī prajāpatiḥ
prajāpatir vi rājati virāḍ indro 'bhavad vaśī
brahmacaryeṇa tapasā rājā rāṣṭraṃ vi rakṣati
ācāryo brahmacaryeṇa brahmacāriṇam ichate
brahmacaryeṇa kanyā yuvānaṃ vindate patim
anaḍvān brahmacaryeṇāśvo ghāsaṃ jigīṣati
brahmacaryeṇa tapasā devā mṛtyum apāghnata
indro ha brahmacaryeṇa devebhyaḥ svar ābharat
oṣadhayo bhūtabhavyam ahorātre vanaspatiḥ
saṃvatsaraḥ saha ṛtubhis te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ
pārthivā divyāḥ paśava āraṇyā grāmyāś ca ye
apakṣāḥ pakṣiṇaś ca ye te jātā brahmacāriṇaḥ
pṛthak sarve prājāpatyāḥ prāṇān ātmasu bibhrati
tānt sarvān brahma rakṣati brahmacāriṇy ābhṛtam
devānām etat pariṣūtam anabhyārūḍhaṃ carati rocamānam
tasmāj jātaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brahma jyeṣṭhaṃ devāś ca sarve amṛtena sākam
brahmacārī brahma bhrājad bibharti tasmin devā adhi viśve samotāḥ
prāṇāpānau janayann ād vyānaṃ vācaṃ mano hṛdayaṃ brahma medhām
cakṣuḥ śrotraṃ yaśo asmāsu dhehy annaṃ reto lohitam udaram
tāni kalpan brahmacārī salilasya pṛṣṭhe tapo 'tiṣṭhat tapyamānaḥ samudre
sa snāto babhruḥ piṅgalaḥ pṛthivyāṃ bahu rocate
agniṃ brūmo vanaspatīn oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ
indraṃ bṛhaspatiṃ sūryaṃ te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
brūmo rājānaṃ varuṇaṃ mitraṃ viṣṇum atho bhagam
aṃśaṃ vivasvantaṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
brūmo devaṃ savitāraṃ dhātāram uta pūṣaṇam
tvaṣṭāram agriyaṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
gandharvāpsaraso brūmo aśvinā brahmaṇaspatim
aryamā nāma yo devas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
ahorātre idaṃ brūmaḥ sūryācandramasāv ubhā
viśvān ādityān brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
vātaṃ brūmaḥ parjanyam antarikṣam atho diśaḥ
āśāś ca sarvā brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
muñcantu mā śapathyād ahorātre atho uṣāḥ
somo mā devo muñcatu yam āhuś candramā iti
pārthivā divyāḥ paśava āraṇyā uta ye mṛgāḥ
śakuntān pakṣiṇo brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
bhavāśarvāv idaṃ brūmo rudraṃ paśupatiś ca yaḥ
iṣūr yā eṣāṃ saṃvidma tā naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ
divaṃ brūmo nakṣatrāṇi bhūmiṃ yakṣāṇi parvatān
samudrā nadyo veśantās te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
saptaṛṣīn vā idaṃ brūmo 'po devīḥ prajāpatim
pitṝn yamaśreṣṭhān brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
ye devā diviṣado antarikṣasadaś ca ye
pṛthivyāṃ śakrā ye śritās te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
ādityā rudrā vasavo divi devā atharvāṇaḥ
aṅgiraso manīṣiṇas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
yajñaṃ brūmo yajamānam ṛcaḥ sāmāni bheṣajā
yajūṃṣi hotrā brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
pañca rājyāni vīrudhāṃ somaśreṣṭhāni brūmaḥ
darbho bhaṅgo yavaḥ sahas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
arāyān brūmo rakṣāṃsi sarpān puṇyajanān pitṝn
mṛtyūn ekaśataṃ brūmas te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
ṛtūn brūma ṛtupatīn ārtavān uta hāyanān
samāḥ saṃvatsarān māsāṃs te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
eta devā dakṣiṇataḥ paścāt prāñca udeta
purastād uttarāc chakrā viśve devāḥ sametya te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
viśvān devān idaṃ brūmaḥ satyasandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
viśvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
sarvān devān idaṃ brūmaḥ satyasandhān ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
sarvābhiḥ patnībhiḥ saha te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
bhūtaṃ brūmo bhūtapatiṃ bhūtānām uta yo vaśī
bhūtāni sarvā saṃgatya te no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
yā devīḥ pañca pradiśo ye devā dvādaśa ṛtavaḥ
saṃvatsarasya ye daṃṣṭrās te naḥ santu sadā śivāḥ
yan mātalī rathakrītam amṛtaṃ veda bheṣajam
tad indro apsu prāveśayat tad āpo datta bheṣajam
ucchiṣṭe nāma rūpaṃ cocchiṣṭe loka āhitaḥ
ucchiṣṭa indraś cāgniś ca viśvam antaḥ samāhitam
ucchiṣṭe dyāvāpṛthivī viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ samāhitam
āpaḥ samudra ucchiṣṭe candramā vāta āhitaḥ
sann ucchiṣṭe asaṃś cobhau mṛtyur vājaḥ prajāpatiḥ
laukyā ucchiṣṭa āyattā vraś ca draś cāpi śrīr mayi
dṛḍho dṛṃha sthiro nyo brahma viśvasṛjo daśa
nābhim iva sarvataś cakram ucchiṣṭe devatāḥ śritāḥ
ṛk sāma yajur ucchiṣṭa udgīthaḥ prastutaṃ stutam
hiṅkāra ucchiṣṭe svaraḥ sāmno meḍiś ca tan mayi
aindrāgnaṃ pāvamānaṃ mahānāmnīr mahāvratam
ucchiṣṭe yajñasyāṅgāny antar garbha iva mātari
rājasūyaṃ vājapeyam agniṣṭomaṣ tad adhvaraḥ
arkāśvamedhāv ucchiṣṭe jīvabarhir madintamaḥ
agnyādheyam atho dīkṣā kāmapraś chandasā saha
utsannā yajñāḥ satrāṇy ucchiṣṭe 'dhi samāhitāḥ
agnihotraṃ ca śraddhā ca vaṣaṭkāro vrataṃ tapaḥ
dakṣiṇeṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cocchiṣṭe 'dhi samāhitāḥ
ekarātro dvirātraḥ sadyaḥkrīḥ prakrīr ukthyaḥ
otaṃ nihitam ucchiṣṭe yajñasyāṇūni vidyayā
catūrātraḥ pañcarātraḥ ṣaḍrātraś cobhayaḥ saha
ṣoḍaśī saptarātraś cocchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve ye yajñā amṛte hitāḥ
pratīhāro nidhanaṃ viśvajic cābhijic ca yaḥ
sāhnātirātrāv ucchiṣṭe dvādaśāho 'pi tan mayi
sūnṛtā saṃnatiḥ kṣemaḥ svadhorjāmṛtaṃ sahaḥ
ucchiṣṭe sarve pratyañcaḥ kāmāḥ kāmena tātṛpuḥ
nava bhūmīḥ samudrā ucchiṣṭe 'dhi śritā divaḥ
ā sūryo bhāty ucchiṣṭe 'horātre api tan mayi
upahavyaṃ viṣūvantaṃ ye ca yajñā guhā hitāḥ
bibharti bhartā viśvasyocchiṣṭo janituḥ pitā
pitā janitur ucchiṣṭo 'soḥ pautraḥ pitāmahaḥ
sa kṣiyati viśvasyeśāno vṛṣā bhūmyām atighnyaḥ
ṛtaṃ satyaṃ tapo rāṣṭraṃ śramo dharmaś ca karma ca
bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyad ucchiṣṭe vīryaṃ lakṣmīr balaṃ bale
samṛddhir oja ākūtiḥ kṣatraṃ rāṣṭraṃ ṣaḍ urvyaḥ
saṃvatsaro 'dhy ucchiṣṭa iḍā praiṣā grahā haviḥ
caturhotāra āpriyaś cāturmāsyāni nīvidaḥ
ucchiṣṭe yajñā hotrāḥ paśubandhās tad iṣṭayaḥ
ardhamāsāś ca māsāś cārtavā ṛtubhiḥ saha
ucchiṣṭe ghoṣiṇīr āpa stanayitnuḥ śrutir mahī
śarkarāḥ sikatā aśmāna oṣadhayo vīrudhas tṛṇā
abhrāṇi vidyuto varṣam ucchiṣṭe saṃśritā śritā
rāddhiḥ prāptiḥ samāptir vyāptir maha edhatuḥ
atyāptir ucchiṣṭe bhūtiś cāhitā nihitā hitā
yac ca prāṇati prāṇena yac ca paśyati cakṣuṣā
ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ
ṛcaḥ sāmāni chandāṃsi purāṇaṃ yajuṣā saha
ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ
prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā
ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ
ānandā modāḥ pramudo 'bhīmodamudaś ca ye
ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ
devāḥ pitaro manuṣyā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye
ucchiṣṭāj jajñire sarve divi devā diviśritaḥ
yan manyur jāyām āvahat saṃkalpasya gṛhād adhi
ka āsaṃ janyāḥ ke varāḥ ka u jyeṣṭhavaro 'bhavat
tapaś caivāstāṃ karma cāntar mahaty arṇave
ta āsaṃ janyās te varā brahma jyeṣṭhavaro 'bhavat
daśa sākam ajāyanta devā devebhyaḥ purā
yo vai tān vidyāt pratyakṣaṃ sa vā adya mahad vadet
prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā
vyānodānau vāṅ manas te vā ākūtim āvahan
ajātā āsann ṛtavo 'tho dhātā bṛhaspatiḥ
indrāgnī aśvinā tarhi kaṃ te jyeṣṭham upāsata
tapaś caivāstāṃ karma cāntar mahaty arṇave
tapo ha jajñe karmaṇas tat te jyeṣṭham upāsata
yeta āsīd bhūmiḥ pūrvā yām addhātaya id viduḥ
yo vai tāṃ vidyān nāmathā sa manyeta purāṇavit
kuta indraḥ kutaḥ somaḥ kuto agnir ajāyata
kutas tvaṣṭā sam abhavat kuto dhātājāyata
indrād indraḥ somāt somo agner agnir ajāyata
tvaṣṭā ha jajñe tvaṣṭur dhātur dhātājāyata
ye ta āsan daśa jātā devā devebhyaḥ purā
putrebhyo lokaṃ dattvā kasmiṃs te loka āsate
yadā keśān asthi snāva māṃsaṃ majjānam ābharat
śarīraṃ kṛtvā pādavat kaṃ lokam anu prāviśat
kutaḥ keśān kutaḥ snāva kuto asthīny ābharat
aṅgā parvāṇi majjānaṃ ko māṃsaṃ kuta ābharat
saṃsico nāma te devā ye saṃbhārānt samabharan
sarvaṃ saṃsicya martyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan
ūrū pādāv aṣṭhīvantau śiro hastāv atho mukham
pṛṣṭīr barjahye pārśve kas tat sam adadhād ṛṣiḥ
śiro hastāv atho mukhaṃ jihvāṃ grīvāś ca kīkasāḥ
tvacā prāvṛtya sarvaṃ tat saṃdhā sam adadhān mahī
yat tac charīram aśayat saṃdhayā saṃhitaṃ mahat
yenedam adya rocate ko asmin varṇam ābharat
sarve devā upāśikṣan tad ajānād vadhūḥ satī
īśā vaśasya yā jāyā sāsmin varṇam ābharat
yadā tvaṣṭā vyatṛṇat pitā tvaṣṭur ya uttaraḥ
gṛhaṃ kṛtvā martyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan
svapno vai tandrīr nirṛtiḥ pāpmāno nāma devatāḥ
jarā khālatyaṃ pālityaṃ śarīram anu prāviśan
steyaṃ duṣkṛtaṃ vṛjinaṃ satyaṃ yajño yaśo bṛhat
balaṃ ca kṣatram ojaś ca śarīram anu prāviśan
bhūtiś ca vā abhūtiś ca rātayo 'rātayaś ca yāḥ
kṣudhaś ca sarvās tṛṣṇāś ca śarīram anu prāviśan
nindāś ca vā anindāś ca yac ca hanteti neti ca
śarīraṃ śraddhā dakṣiṇāśraddhā cānu prāviśan
vidyāś ca vā avidyāś ca yac cānyad upadeśyam
śarīraṃ brahma prāviśad ṛcaḥ sāmātho yajuḥ
ānandā modāḥ pramudo 'bhīmodamudaś ca ye
haso nariṣṭā nṛttāni śarīram anu prāviśan
ālāpāś ca pralāpāś cābhīlāpalapaś ca ye
śarīraṃ sarve prāviśann āyujaḥ prayujo yujaḥ
prāṇāpānau cakṣuḥ śrotram akṣitiś ca kṣitiś ca yā
vyānodānau vāṅ manaḥ śarīreṇa ta īyante
