āśiṣaś ca praśiṣaś ca saṃśiṣo viśiṣaś ca yāḥ
cittāni sarve saṃkalpāḥ śarīram anu prāviśan
āsteyīś ca vāsteyīś ca tvaraṇāḥ kṛpaṇāś ca yāḥ
guhyāḥ śukrā sthūlā apas tā bībhatsāv asādayan
asthi kṛtvā samidhaṃ tad aṣṭāpo asādayan
retaḥ kṛtvājyaṃ devāḥ puruṣam āviśan
yā āpo yāś ca devatā yā virāḍ brahmaṇā saha
śarīraṃ brahma prāviśac charīre 'dhi prajāpatiḥ
sūryaś cakṣur vātaḥ prāṇaṃ puruṣasya vi bhejire
athāsyetaram ātmānaṃ devāḥ prāyachann agnaye
tasmād vai vidvān puruṣam idaṃ brahmeti manyate
sarvā hy asmin devatā gāvo goṣṭha ivāsate
prathamena pramāreṇa tredhā viṣvaṅ vi gachati
ada ekena gachaty ada ekena gachatīhaikena ni ṣevate
apsu stīmāsu vṛddhāsu śarīram antarā hitam
tasmiṃ chavo 'dhy antarā tasmāc chavo 'dhy ucyate
ye bāhavo yā iṣavo dhanvanāṃ vīryāṇi ca
asīn paraśūn āyudhaṃ cittākūtaṃ ca yad dhṛdi
sarvaṃ tad arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya
ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvaṃ mitrā devajanā yūyam
saṃdṛṣṭā guptā vaḥ santu yā no mitrāṇy arbude
ut tiṣṭhatam ā rabhetām ādānasaṃdānābhyām
amitrāṇāṃ senā abhi dhattam arbude
arbudir nāma yo deva īśānaś ca nyarbudiḥ
yābhyām antarikṣam āvṛtam iyaṃ ca pṛthivī mahī
tābhyām indramedibhyām ahaṃ jitam anv emi senayā
ut tiṣṭha tvaṃ devajanārbude senayā saha
bhañjann amitrāṇāṃ senāṃ bhogebhiḥ pari vāraya
sapta jātān nyarbuda udārāṇāṃ samīkṣayan
tebhiṣ ṭvam ājye hute sarvair ut tiṣṭha senayā
pratighnānāśrumukhī kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu
vikeśī puruṣe hate radite arbude tava
saṃkarṣantī karūkaraṃ manasā putram ichantī
patiṃ bhrātaram āt svān radite arbude tava
aliklavā jāṣkamadā gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ
dhvāṅkṣāḥ śakunayas tṛpyantv amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava
atho sarvaṃ śvāpadaṃ makṣikā tṛpyatu krimiḥ
pauruṣeye 'dhi kuṇape radite arbude tava
ā gṛhṇītaṃ saṃ bṛhataṃ prāṇāpānān nyarbude
nivāśā ghoṣāḥ saṃ yantv amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava
ud vepaya saṃ vijantāṃ bhiyāmitrānt saṃ sṛja
urugrāhair bāhvaṅkair vidhyāmitrān nyarbude
muhyantv eṣāṃ bāhavaś cittākūtaṃ ca yad dhṛdi
maiṣām uc cheṣi kiṃ cana radite arbude tava
pratighnānāḥ saṃ dhāvantūraḥ paṭaurāv āghnānāḥ
aghāriṇīr vikeśyo rudatyaḥ puruṣe hate radite arbude tava
śvanvatīr apsaraso rūpakā utārbude
antaḥpātre rerihatīṃ riśāṃ durṇihitaiṣiṇīm
sarvās tā arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya
khaḍūre 'dhicaṅkramāṃ kharvikāṃ kharvavāsinīm
ya udārā antarhitā gandharvāpsarasaś ca ye
sarpā itarajanā rakṣāṃsi
caturdaṃṣṭrāṃ chyāvadataḥ kumbhamuṣkāṃ asṛṅmukhān
svabhyasā ye codbhyasāḥ
ud vepaya tvam arbude 'mitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ
jayaṃś ca jiṣṇuś cāmitrāṃ jayatām indramedinau
prablīno mṛditaḥ śayāṃ hato 'mitro nyarbude
agnijihvā dhūmaśikhā jayantīr yantu senayā
tayārbude praṇuttānām indro hantu varaṃvaram
amitrāṇāṃ śacīpatir māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana
ut kasantu hṛdayāny ūrdhvaḥ prāṇa ud īṣatu
śauṣkāsyam anu vartatām amitrān mota mitriṇaḥ
ye ca dhīrā ye cādhīrāḥ parāñco badhirāś ca ye
tamasā ye ca tūparā atho bastābhivāsinaḥ
sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya
arbudiś ca triṣandhiś cāmitrān no vi vidhyatām
yathaiṣām indra vṛtrahan hanāma śacīpate 'mitrāṇāṃ sahasraśaḥ
vanaspatīn vānaspatyān oṣadhīr uta vīrudhaḥ
gandharvāpsarasaḥ sarpān devān puṇyajanān pitṝn
sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude tvam amitrebhyo dṛśe kurūdārāṃś ca pra darśaya
īśāṃ vo maruto deva ādityo brahmaṇaspatiḥ
īśāṃ va indraś cāgniś ca dhātā mitraḥ prajāpatiḥ
īśāṃ va ṛṣayaś cakrur amitreṣu samīkṣayan radite arbude tava
teṣāṃ sarveṣām īśānā ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvam
mitrā devajanā yūyam imaṃ saṃgrāmaṃ saṃjitya yathālokaṃ vi tiṣṭhadhvam
ut tiṣṭhata saṃ nahyadhvam udārāḥ ketubhiḥ saha
sarpā itarajanā rakṣāṃsy amitrān anu dhāvata
īśāṃ vo veda rājyaṃ triṣandhe aruṇaiḥ ketubhiḥ saha
ye antarikṣe ye divi pṛthivyāṃ ye ca mānavāḥ
triṣandhes te cetasi durṇāmāna upāsatām
ayomukhāḥ sūcīmukhā atho vikaṅkatīmukhāḥ
kravyādo vātaraṃhasa ā sajantv amitrān vajreṇa triṣandhinā
antar dhehi jātaveda āditya kuṇapaṃ bahu
triṣandher iyaṃ senā suhitāstu me vaśe
ut tiṣṭha tvaṃ devajanārbude senayā saha
ayaṃ balir va āhutas triṣandher āhutiḥ priyā
śitipadī saṃ dyatu śaravyeyaṃ catuṣpadī
kṛtye 'mitrebhyo bhava triṣandheḥ saha senayā
dhūmākṣī saṃ patatu kṛdhukarṇī ca krośatu
triṣandheḥ senayā jite aruṇāḥ santu ketavaḥ
avāyantāṃ pakṣiṇo ye vayāṃsy antarikṣe divi ye caranti
śvāpado makṣikāḥ saṃ rabhantām āmādo gṛdhrāḥ kuṇape radantām
yām indreṇa saṃdhāṃ samadhatthā brahmaṇā ca bṛhaspate
tayāham indrasaṃdhayā sarvān devān iha huva ito jayata māmutaḥ
bṛhaspatir āṅgirasa ṛṣayo brahmasaṃśitāḥ
asurakṣayaṇaṃ vadhaṃ triṣandhiṃ divy āśrayan
yenāsau gupta āditya ubhāv indraś ca tiṣṭhataḥ
triṣandhiṃ devā abhajantaujase ca balāya ca
sarvāṃl lokānt sam ajayan devā āhutyānayā
bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso vajraṃ yam asiñcatāsurakṣayaṇaṃ vadham
bṛhaspatir āṅgiraso vajraṃ yam asiñcatāsurakṣayaṇaṃ vadham
tenāham amūṃ senāṃ ni limpāmi bṛhaspate 'mitrān hanmy ojasā
sarve devā atyāyanti ye aśnanti vaṣaṭkṛtam
imāṃ juṣadhvam āhutim ito jayata māmutaḥ
sarve devā atyāyantu triṣandher āhutiḥ priyā
saṃdhāṃ mahatīṃ rakṣata yayāgre asurā jitāḥ
vāyur amitrāṇām iṣvagrāṇy āñcatu
indra eṣāṃ bāhūn prati bhanaktu mā śakan pratidhām iṣum
āditya eṣām astraṃ vi nāśayatu candramā yutām agatasya panthām
yadi preyur devapurā brahma varmāṇi cakrire
tanūpānaṃ paripāṇaṃ kṛṇvānā yad upocire sarvaṃ tad arasaṃ kṛdhi
kravyādānuvartayan mṛtyunā ca purohitam
triṣandhe prehi senayā jayāmitrān pra padyasva
triṣandhe tamasā tvam amitrān pari vāraya
pṛṣadājyapraṇuttānāṃ māmīṣāṃ moci kaś cana
śitipadī saṃ patatv amitrāṇām amūḥ sicaḥ
muhyantv adyāmūḥ senā amitrāṇāṃ nyarbude
mūḍhā amitrā nyarbude jahy eṣāṃ varaṃvaram
anayā jahi senayā
yaś ca kavacī yaś cākavaco 'mitro yaś cājmani
jyāpāśaiḥ kavacapāśair ajmanābhihataḥ śayām
ye varmiṇo ye 'varmāṇo amitrā ye ca varmiṇaḥ
sarvāṃs tāṃ arbude hatāṃ chvāno 'dantu bhūmyām
ye rathino ye arathā asādā ye ca sādinaḥ
sarvān adantu tān hatān gṛdhrāḥ śyenāḥ patatriṇaḥ
sahasrakuṇapā śetām āmitrī senā samare vadhānām
vividdhā kakajākṛtā
marmāvidhaṃ roruvataṃ suparṇair adantu duścitaṃ mṛditaṃ śayānam
ya imāṃ pratīcīm āhutim amitro no yuyutsati
yāṃ devā anutiṣṭhanti yasyā nāsti virādhanam
tayendro hantu vṛtrahā vajreṇa triṣandhinā
satyaṃ bṛhad ṛtam ugraṃ dīkṣā tapo brahma yajñaḥ pṛthivīṃ dhārayanti
sā no bhūtasya bhavyasya patny uruṃ lokaṃ pṛthivī naḥ kṛṇotu
asaṃbādhaṃ madhyato mānavānāṃ yasyā udvataḥ pravataḥ samaṃ bahu
nānāvīryā oṣadhīr yā bibharti pṛthivī naḥ prathatāṃ rādhyatāṃ naḥ
yasyāṃ samudra uta sindhur āpo yasyām annaṃ kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
yasyām idaṃ jinvati prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmiḥ pūrvapeye dadhātu
yasyāś catasraḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyā yasyām annam kṛṣṭayaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
yā bibharti bahudhā prāṇad ejat sā no bhūmir goṣv apy anne dadhātu
yasyāṃ pūrve pūrvajanā vicakrire yasyāṃ devā asurān abhyavartayan
gavām aśvānāṃ vayasaś ca viṣṭhā bhagaṃ varcaḥ pṛthivī no dadhātu
viśvaṃbharā vasudhānī pratiṣṭhā hiraṇyavakṣā jagato niveśanī
vaiśvānaraṃ bibhratī bhūmir agnim indraṛṣabhā draviṇe no dadhātu
yāṃ rakṣanty asvapnā viśvadānīṃ devā bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm apramādam
sā no madhu priyaṃ duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā
yārṇave 'dhi salilam agra āsīt yāṃ māyābhir anvacaran manīṣiṇaḥ
yasyā hṛdayaṃ parame vyomant satyenāvṛtam amṛtaṃ pṛthivyāḥ
sā no bhūmis tviṣiṃ balaṃ rāṣṭre dadhātūttame
yasyām āpaḥ paricarāḥ samānīr ahorātre apramādaṃ kṣaranti
sā no bhūmir bhūridhārā payo duhām atho ukṣatu varcasā
yām aśvināv amimātāṃ viṣṇur yasyāṃ vicakrame
indro yāṃ cakra ātmane 'namitrāṃ śacīpatiḥ
sā no bhūmir vi sṛjatāṃ mātā putrāya me payaḥ
girayas te parvatā himavanto 'raṇyaṃ te pṛthivi syonam astu
babhruṃ kṛṣṇāṃ rohiṇīṃ viśvarūpāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīm indraguptām
ajīto 'hato akṣato 'dhy aṣṭhām pṛthivīm aham
yat te madhyaṃ pṛthivi yac ca nabhyaṃ yās ta ūrjas tanvaḥ saṃbabhūvuḥ
tāsu no dhehy abhi naḥ pavasva mātā bhūmiḥ putro ahaṃ pṛthivyāḥ parjanyaḥ pitā sa u naḥ pipartu
yasyāṃ vediṃ parigṛhṇanti bhūmyāṃ yasyāṃ yajñaṃ tanvate viśvakarmāṇaḥ
yasyāṃ mīyante svaravaḥ pṛthivyām ūrdhvāḥ śukrā āhutyāḥ purastāt
sā no bhūmir vardhayad vardhamānā
yo no dveṣat pṛthivi yaḥ pṛtanyād yo 'bhidāsān manasā yo vadhena
taṃ no bhūme randhaya pūrvakṛtvari
tvaj jātās tvayi caranti martyās tvaṃ bibharṣi dvipadas tvaṃ catuṣpadaḥ
taveme pṛthivi pañca mānavā yebhyo jyotir amṛtaṃ martyebhya udyant sūryo raśmibhir ātanoti
tā naḥ prajāḥ saṃ duhratāṃ samagrā vāco madhu pṛthivi dhehi mahyam
viśvasvaṃ mātaram oṣadhīnāṃ dhruvāṃ bhūmiṃ pṛthivīṃ dharmaṇā dhṛtām
śivāṃ syonām anu carema viśvahā
mahat sadhasthaṃ mahatī babhūvitha mahān vega ejathur vepathuṣ ṭe
mahāṃs tvendro rakṣaty apramādam
sā no bhūme pra rocaya hiraṇyasyeva saṃdṛśi mā no dvikṣata kaś cana
agnir bhūmyām oṣadhīṣv agnim āpo bibhraty agnir aśmasu
agnir antaḥ puruṣeṣu goṣv aśveṣv agnayaḥ
agnir diva ā tapaty agner devasyorv antarikṣam
agniṃ martāsa indhate havyavāhaṃ ghṛtapriyam
agnivāsāḥ pṛthivy asitajñūs tviṣīmantaṃ saṃśitaṃ mā kṛṇotu
bhūmyāṃ devebhyo dadati yajñaṃ havyam araṃkṛtam
bhūmyāṃ manuṣyā jīvanti svadhayānnena martyāḥ
sā no bhūmiḥ prāṇam āyur dadhātu jaradaṣṭiṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu
yas te gandhaḥ pṛthivi saṃbabhūva yaṃ bibhraty oṣadhayo yam āpaḥ
yaṃ gandharvā apsarasaś ca bhejire tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaś cana
yas te gandhaḥ puṣkaram āviveśa yaṃ saṃjabhruḥ sūryāyā vivāhe
amartyāḥ pṛthivi gandham agre tena mā surabhiṃ kṛṇu mā no dvikṣata kaś cana
yas te gandhaḥ puruṣeṣu strīṣu puṃsu bhago ruciḥ
yo aśveṣu vīreṣu yo mṛgeṣūta hastiṣu
kanyāyāṃ varco yad bhūme tenāsmāṃ api saṃ sṛja mā no dvikṣata kaś cana
śilā bhūmir aśmā pāṃsuḥ sā bhūmiḥ saṃdhṛtā dhṛtā
tasyai hiraṇyavakṣase pṛthivyā akaraṃ namaḥ
yasyāṃ vṛkṣā vānaspatyā dhruvās tiṣṭhanti viśvahā
pṛthivīṃ viśvadhāyasaṃ dhṛtām achāvadāmasi
udīrāṇā utāsīnās tiṣṭhantaḥ prakrāmantaḥ
padbhyāṃ dakṣiṇasavyābhyāṃ mā vyathiṣmahi bhūmyām
vimṛgvarīṃ pṛthivīm ā vadāmi kṣamāṃ bhūmiṃ brahmaṇā vāvṛdhānām
ūrjaṃ puṣṭaṃ bibhratīm annabhāgaṃ ghṛtaṃ tvābhi ni ṣīdema bhūme
śuddhā na āpas tanve kṣarantu yo naḥ sedur apriye taṃ ni dadhmaḥ
pavitreṇa pṛthivi mot punāmi
yās te prācīḥ pradiśo yā udīcīr yās te bhūme adharād yāś ca paścāt
syonās tā mahyaṃ carate bhavantu mā ni paptaṃ bhuvane śiśriyāṇaḥ
mā naḥ paścān mā purastān nudiṣṭhā mottarād adharād uta
svasti bhūme no bhava mā vidan paripanthino varīyo yāvayā vadham
yāvat te 'bhi vipaśyāmi bhūme sūryeṇa medinā
tāvan me cakṣur mā meṣṭottarāmuttarāṃ samām
yac chayānaḥ paryāvarte dakṣiṇaṃ sakhyam abhi bhūme pārśvam uttānās tvā pratīcīṃ yat pṛṣṭībhir adhiśemahe
mā hiṃsīs tatra no bhūme sarvasya pratiśīvari
yat te bhūme vikhanāmi kṣipraṃ tad api rohatu
mā te marma vimṛgvari mā te hṛdayam arpipam
grīṣmas te bhūme varṣāṇi śarad dhemantaḥ śiśiro vasantaḥ
ṛtavas te vihitā hāyanīr ahorātre pṛthivi no duhātām
yāpa sarpaṃ vijamānā vimṛgvarī yasyām āsann agnayo ye apsv antaḥ
parā dasyūn dadatī devapīyūn indraṃ vṛṇānā pṛthivī na vṛtram śakrāya dadhre vṛṣabhāya vṛṣṇe
yasyāṃ sadohavirdhāne yūpo yasyāṃ nimīyate
brahmāṇo yasyām arcanty ṛgbhiḥ sāmnā yajurvidaḥ yujyante yasyām ṛtvijaḥ somam indrāya pātave
yasyāṃ pūrve bhūtakṛta ṛṣayo gā udānṛcuḥ
sapta satreṇa vedhaso yajñena tapasā saha
sā no bhūmir ā diśatu yad dhanaṃ kāmayāmahe
bhago anuprayuṅktām indra etu purogavaḥ
yasyāṃ gāyanti nṛtyanti bhūmyāṃ martyā vyailabāḥ
yudhyante yasyām ākrando yasyām vadati dundubhiḥ
sā no bhūmiḥ pra ṇudatāṃ sapatnān asapatnaṃ mā pṛthivī kṛṇotu
yasyām annaṃ vrīhiyavau yasyā imāḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ
bhūmyai parjanyapatnyai namo 'stu varṣamedase
yasyāḥ puro devakṛtāḥ kṣetre yasyā vikurvate
prajāpatiḥ pṛthivīṃ viśvagarbhām āśāmāśāṃ raṇyāṃ naḥ kṛṇotu
nidhiṃ bibhratī bahudhā guhā vasu maṇiṃ hiraṇyaṃ pṛthivī dadātu me
vasūni no vasudā rāsamānā devī dadhātu sumanasyamānā
janaṃ bibhratī bahudhā vivācasaṃ nānādharmāṇaṃ pṛthivī yathaukasam
sahasraṃ dhārā draviṇasya me duhāṃ dhruveva dhenur anapasphurantī
yas te sarpo vṛścikas tṛṣṭadaṃśmā hemantajabdho bhṛmalo guhā śaye
krimir jinvat pṛthivi yadyad ejati prāvṛṣi tan naḥ sarpan mopa sṛpad yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa
ye te panthāno bahavo janāyanā rathasya vartmānasaś ca yātave
yaiḥ saṃcaranty ubhaye bhadrapāpās taṃ panthānaṃ jayemānamitram ataskaraṃ yac chivaṃ tena no mṛḍa
malvaṃ bibhratī gurubhṛd bhadrapāpasya nidhanaṃ titikṣuḥ
varāheṇa pṛthivī saṃvidānā sūkarāya vi jihīte mṛgāya
ye ta āraṇyāḥ paśavo mṛgā vane hitāḥ siṃhā vyāghrāḥ puruṣādaś caranti
ulaṃ vṛkaṃ pṛthivi duchunām ita ṛkṣīkāṃ rakṣo apa bādhayāsmat
ye gandharvā apsaraso ye cārāyāḥ kimīdinaḥ
piśācānt sarvā rakṣāṃsi tān asmad bhūme yāvaya
yāṃ dvipādaḥ pakṣiṇaḥ saṃpatanti haṃsāḥ suparṇāḥ śakunā vayāṃsi
yasyāṃ vāto mātariśveyate rajāṃsi kṛṇvaṃś cyāvayaṃś ca vṛkṣān
vātasya pravām upavām anu vāty arciḥ
yasyāṃ kṛṣṇam aruṇaṃ ca saṃhite ahorātre vihite bhūmyām adhi
varṣeṇa bhūmiḥ pṛthivī vṛtāvṛtā sā no dadhātu bhadrayā priye dhāmanidhāmani
dyauś ca ma idaṃ pṛthivī cāntarikṣaṃ ca me vyacaḥ
agniḥ sūrya āpo medhāṃ viśve devāś ca saṃ daduḥ
aham asmi sahamāna uttaro nāma bhūmyām
abhīṣāḍ asmi viśvāṣāḍ āśāmāśāṃ viṣāsahiḥ
ado yad devi prathamānā purastād devair uktā vyasarpo mahitvam
ā tvā subhūtam aviśat tadānīm akalpayathāḥ pradiśaś catasraḥ
ye grāmā yad araṇyaṃ yāḥ sabhā adhi bhūmyām
ye saṃgrāmāḥ samitayas teṣu cāru vadema te
aśva iva rajo dudhuve vi tān janān ya ākṣiyan pṛthivīṃ yād ajāyata
mandrāgretvarī bhuvanasya gopā vanaspatīnāṃ gṛbhir oṣadhīnām
yad vadāmi madhumat tad vadāmi yad īkṣe tad vananti mā
tviṣīmān asmi jūtimān avānyān hanmi dodhataḥ
śantivā surabhiḥ syonā kīlālodhnī payasvatī
bhūmir adhi bravītu me pṛthivī payasā saha
yām anvaichad dhaviṣā viśvakarmāntar arṇave rajasi praviṣṭām
bhujiṣyaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ guhā yad āvir bhoge abhavan mātṛmadbhyaḥ
tvam asy āvapanī janānām aditiḥ kāmadughā paprathānā
yat ta ūnaṃ tat ta ā pūrayāti prajāpatiḥ prathamajā ṛtasya
upasthās te anamīvā ayakṣmā asmabhyaṃ santu pṛthivi prasūtāḥ
dīrghaṃ na āyuḥ pratibudhyamānā vayaṃ tubhyaṃ balihṛtaḥ syāma
bhūme mātar ni dhehi mā bhadrayā supratiṣṭhitam
saṃvidānā divā kave śriyāṃ mā dhehi bhūtyām
naḍam ā roha na te atra loka idaṃ sīsaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ ta ehi
yo goṣu yakṣmaḥ puruṣeṣu yakṣmas tena tvaṃ sākam adharāṅ parehi
aghaśaṃsaduḥśaṃsābhyāṃ kareṇānukareṇa ca
yakṣmaṃ ca sarvaṃ teneto mṛtyuṃ ca nir ajāmasi
nir ito mṛtyuṃ nirṛtiṃ nir arātim ajāmasi
yo no dveṣṭi tam addhy agne akravyād yam u dviṣmas tam u te pra suvāmasi
yady agniḥ kravyād yadi vā vyāghra imaṃ goṣṭhaṃ praviveśānyokāḥ
taṃ māṣājyaṃ kṛtvā pra hiṇomi dūraṃ sa gachatv apsuṣado 'py agnīn
yat tvā kruddhāḥ pracakrur manyunā puruṣe mṛte
sukalpam agne tat tvayā punas tvod dīpayāmasi
punas tvādityā rudrā vasavaḥ punar brahmā vasunītir agne
punas tvā brahmaṇas patir ādhād dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya
yo agniḥ kravyāt praviveśa no gṛham imaṃ paśyann itaraṃ jātavedasam
taṃ harāmi pitṛyajñāya dūraṃ sa gharmam indhāṃ parame sadhasthe
kravyādam agniṃ pra hiṇomi dūram yamarājño gachatu ripravāhaḥ
ihāyam itaro jātavedā devo devebhyo havyaṃ vahatu prajānan
kravyādam agnim iṣito harāmi janān dṛṃhantaṃ vajreṇa mṛtyum
ni taṃ śāsmi gārhapatyena vidvān pitṝṇāṃ loke 'pi bhāgo astu
kravyādam agniṃ śaśamānam ukthyaṃ pra hiṇomi pathibhiḥ pitṛyāṇaiḥ
mā devayānaiḥ punar ā gā atraivaidhi pitṛṣu jāgṛhi tvam
sam indhate saṃkasukaṃ svastaye śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ
jahāti ripram aty ena eti samiddho agniḥ supunā punāti
devo agniḥ saṃkasuko divas pṛṣṭhāny āruhat
mucyamāno nir eṇaso 'mog asmāṃ aśastyāḥ
asmin vayaṃ saṃkasuke agnau riprāṇi mṛjmahe
abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat
saṃkasuko vikasuko nirṛtho yaś ca nisvaraḥ
te te yakṣmaṃ savedaso dūrād dūram anīnaśan
yo no aśveṣu vīreṣu yo no goṣv ajāviṣu
kravyādaṃ nir ṇudāmasi yo agnir janayopanaḥ
anyebhyas tvā puruṣebhyo gobhyo aśvebhyas tvā
niḥ kravyādaṃ nudāmasi yo agnir jīvitayopanaḥ
yasmin devā amṛjata yasmin manuṣyā uta
tasmin ghṛtastāvo mṛṣṭvā tvam agne divaṃ ruha
samiddho agna āhuta sa no mābhyapakramīḥ
atraiva dīdihi dyavi jyok ca sūryaṃ dṛśe
sīse mṛḍḍhvaṃ naḍe mṛḍḍhvam agnau saṃkasuke ca yat
atho avyāṃ rāmāyāṃ śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe
sīse malaṃ sādayitvā śīrṣaktim upabarhaṇe
avyām asiknyāṃ mṛṣṭvā śuddhā bhavata yajñiyāḥ
paraṃ mṛtyo anu parehi panthāṃ yas ta eṣa itaro devayānāt
cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmīheme vīrā bahavo bhavantu
ime jīvā vi mṛtair āvavṛtrann abhūd bhadrā devahutir no adya
prāñco agāma nṛtaye hasāya suvīrāso vidatham ā vadema
imaṃ jīvebhyaḥ paridhiṃ dadhāmi maiṣāṃ nu gād aparo artham etam
śataṃ jīvantaḥ śaradaḥ purūcīs tiro mṛtyuṃ dadhatām parvatena
ā rohatāyur jarasaṃ vṛṇānā anupūrvaṃ yatamānā yati stha
tān vas tvaṣṭā sujanimā sajoṣāḥ sarvam āyur nayatu jīvanāya
yathāhāny anupūrvaṃ bhavanti yatha rtava ṛtubhir yanti sākam
yathā na pūrvam aparo jahāty evā dhātar āyūṃṣi kalpayaiṣām
aśmanvatī rīyate saṃ rabhadhvaṃ vīrayadhvaṃ pra taratā sakhāyaḥ
atrā jahīta ye asan durevā anamīvān ut taremābhi vājān
ut tiṣṭhatā pra taratā sakhāyo 'śmanvatī nadī syandata iyam
atrā jahīta ye asann aśivāḥ śivānt syonān ut taremābhi vājān
vaiśvadevīṃ varcasā ā rabhadhvaṃ śuddhā bhavantaḥ śucayaḥ pāvakāḥ
atikrāmanto duritā padāni śataṃ himāḥ sarvavīrā madema
udīcīnaiḥ pathibhir vāyumadbhir atikrāmanto 'varān parebhiḥ
triḥ sapta kṛtva ṛṣayaḥ paretā mṛtyuṃ praty auhan padayopanena
mṛtyoḥ padaṃ yopayanta eta drāghīya āyuḥ prataraṃ dadhānāḥ
āsīnā mṛtyuṃ nudatā sadhasthe 'tha jīvāso vidatham ā vadema
imā nārīr avidhavāḥ supatnīr āñjanena sarpiṣā saṃ spṛśantām
anaśravo anamīvāḥ suratnā ā rohantu janayo yonim agre
vyākaromi haviṣāham etau tau brahmaṇā vy ahaṃ kalpayāmi
svadhāṃ pitṛbhyo ajarāṃ kṛṇomi dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi
yo no agniḥ pitaro hṛtsv antar āviveśāmṛto martyeṣu
mayy ahaṃ taṃ pari gṛhṇāmi devaṃ mā so asmān dvikṣata mā vayaṃ tam
apāvṛtya gārhapatyāt kravyādā preta dakṣiṇā
priyaṃ pitṛbhya ātmane brahmabhyaḥ kṛṇutā priyam
dvibhāgadhanam ādāya pra kṣiṇāty avartyā
agniḥ putrasya jyeṣṭhasya yaḥ kravyād anirāhitaḥ
yat kṛṣate yad vanute yac ca vasnena vindate
sarvaṃ martyasya tan nāsti kravyāc ced anirāhitaḥ
ayajñiyo hatavarcā bhavati nainena havir attave
chinatti kṛṣyā gor dhanād yaṃ kravyād anuvartate
muhur gṛdhyaiḥ pra vadaty ārtim martyo nītya
kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati
grāhyā gṛhāḥ saṃ sṛjyante striyā yan mriyate patiḥ
brahmaiva vidvān eṣyo yaḥ kravyādaṃ nirādadhat
yad ripraṃ śamalaṃ cakṛma yac ca duṣkṛtam
āpo mā tasmāc chumbhantv agneḥ saṃkasukāc ca yat
tā adharād udīcīr āvavṛtran prajānaitīḥ pathibhir devayānaiḥ
parvatasya vṛṣabhasyādhi pṛṣṭhe navāś caranti saritaḥ purāṇīḥ
agne akravyān niḥ kravyādaṃ nudā devayajanaṃ vaha
imaṃ kravyād ā viveśāyaṃ kravyādam anv agāt
vyāghrau kṛtvā nānānaṃ taṃ harāmi śivāparam
antardhir devānāṃ paridhir manuṣyāṇām agnir gārhapatya ubhayān antarā śritaḥ
jīvānām āyuḥ pra tira tvam agne pitṝṇāṃ lokam api gachantu ye mṛtāḥ
sugārhapatyo vitapann arātim uṣāmuṣāṃ śreyasīṃ dhehy asmai
sarvān agne sahamānaḥ sapatnān aiṣām ūrjaṃ rayim asmāsu dhehi
imam indraṃ vahniṃ paprim anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nir vakṣad duritād avadyāt
tenāpa hata śarum āpatantaṃ tena rudrasya pari pātāstām
anaḍvāhaṃ plavam anvārabhadhvaṃ sa vo nir vakṣad duritād avadyāt
ā rohata savitur nāvam etāṃ ṣaḍbhir urvībhir amatiṃ tarema
ahorātre anv eṣi bibhrat kṣemyas tiṣṭhan prataraṇaḥ suvīraḥ
anāturānt sumanasas talpa bibhraj jyog eva naḥ puruṣagandhir edhi
te devebhya ā vṛścante pāpaṃ jīvanti sarvadā
kravyād yān agnir antikād aśva ivānuvapate naḍam
ye 'śraddhā dhanakāmyā kravyādā samāsate
te vā anyeṣāṃ kumbhīṃ paryādadhati sarvadā
preva pipatiṣati manasā muhur ā vartate punaḥ
kravyād yān agnir antikād anuvidvān vitāvati
aviḥ kṛṣṇā bhāgadheyaṃ paśūnāṃ sīsaṃ kravyād api candraṃ ta āhuḥ
māṣāḥ piṣṭā bhāgadheyaṃ te havyam araṇyānyā gahvaraṃ sacasva
iṣīkāṃ jaratīm iṣṭvā tilpiñjaṃ daṇḍanaṃ naḍam
tam indra idhmam kṛtvā yamasyāgniṃ nirādadhau
pratyañcam arkaṃ pratyarpayitvā pravidvān panthāṃ vi hy āviveśa
parāmīṣām asūn dideśa dīrgheṇāyuṣā sam imānt sṛjāmi
pumān puṃso 'dhi tiṣṭha carmehi tatra hvayasva yatamā priyā te
yāvantāv agre prathamaṃ sameyathus tad vāṃ vayo yamarājye samānam
tāvad vāṃ cakṣus tati vīryāṇi tāvat tejas tatidhā vājināni
agniḥ śarīraṃ sacate yadaidho 'dhā pakvān mithunā saṃ bhavāthaḥ
sam asmiṃl loke sam u devayāne saṃ smā sametaṃ yamarājyeṣu
pūtau pavitrair upa tad dhvayethāṃ yadyad reto adhi vāṃ saṃbabhūva
āpas putrāso abhi saṃ viśadhvam imaṃ jīvaṃ jīvadhanyāḥ sametya
tāsāṃ bhajadhvam amṛtaṃ yam āhur odanaṃ pacati vāṃ janitrī
yaṃ vāṃ pitā pacati yaṃ ca mātā riprān nirmuktyai śamalāc ca vācaḥ
sa odanaḥ śatadhāraḥ svarga ubhe vy āpa nabhasī mahitvā
ubhe nabhasī ubhayāṃś ca lokān ye yajvanām abhijitāḥ svargāḥ
teṣāṃ jyotiṣmān madhumān yo agre tasmin putrair jarasi saṃ śrayethām
prācīṃprācīṃ pradiśam ā rabhethām etaṃ lokaṃ śraddadhānāḥ sacante
yad vāṃ pakvaṃ pariviṣṭam agnau tasya guptaye daṃpatī saṃ śrayethām
dakṣiṇāṃ diśam abhi nakṣamāṇau paryāvartethām abhi pātram etat
tasmin vāṃ yamaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃvidānaḥ pakvāya śarma bahulaṃ ni yachāt
pratīcī diśām iyam id varaṃ yasyāṃ somo adhipā mṛḍitā ca
tasyāṃ śrayethāṃ sukṛtaḥ sacethām adhā pakvān mithunā saṃ bhavāthaḥ
uttaraṃ rāṣṭraṃ prajayottarāvad diśām udīcī kṛṇavan no agram
pāṅktaṃ chandaḥ puruṣo babhūva viśvair viśvāṅgaiḥ saha saṃ bhavema
dhruveyaṃ virāṇ namo astv asyai śivā putrebhya uta mahyam astu
sā no devy adite viśvavāra irya iva gopā abhi rakṣa pakvam
piteva putrān abhi saṃ svajasva naḥ śivā no vātā iha vāntu bhūmau
yam odanaṃ pacato devate iha taṃ nas tapa uta satyaṃ ca vettu
yadyad kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna eha gatvā tsaran viṣaktaṃ bila āsasāda
yad vā dāsy ārdrahastā samaṅkta ulūkhalaṃ musalaṃ śumbhatāpaḥ
ayaṃ grāvā pṛthubudhno vayodhāḥ pūtaḥ pavitrair apa hantu rakṣaḥ
ā roha carma mahi śarma yacha mā daṃpatī pautram aghaṃ ni gātām
vanaspatiḥ saha devair na āgan rakṣaḥ piśācāṃ apabādhamānaḥ
sa uc chrayātai pra vadāti vācaṃ tena lokāṃ abhi sarvān jayema
sapta medhān paśavaḥ pary agṛhṇan ya eṣāṃ jyotiṣmāṃ uta yaś cakarśa
trayastriṃśad devatās tānt sacante sa naḥ svargam abhi neṣa lokam
svargaṃ lokam abhi no nayāsi saṃ jāyayā saha putraiḥ syāma
gṛhṇāmi hastam anu maitv atra mā nas tārīn nirṛtir mo arātiḥ
grāhiṃ pāpmānam ati tāṃ ayāma tamo vy asya pra vadāsi valgu
vānaspatya udyato mā jihiṃsīr mā taṇḍulaṃ vi śarīr devayantam
viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upa yāhy etam
varṣavṛddham upa yacha śūrpaṃ tuṣaṃ palāvān apa tad vinaktu
trayo lokāḥ saṃmitā brāhmaṇena dyaur evāsau pṛthivy antarikṣam
aṃśūn gṛbhītvānvārabhethām ā pyāyantāṃ punar ā yantu śūrpam
pṛthag rūpāṇi bahudhā paśūnām ekarūpo bhavasi saṃ samṛddhyā
etāṃ tvacaṃ lohinīṃ tāṃ nudasva grāvā śumbhāti malaga iva vastrā
pṛthivīṃ tvā pṛthivyām ā veśayāmi tanūḥ samānī vikṛtā ta eṣā
yadyad dyuttaṃ likhitam arpaṇena tena mā susror brahmaṇāpi tad vapāmi
janitrīva prati haryāsi sūnuṃ saṃ tvā dadhāmi pṛthivīṃ pṛthivyā
ukhā kumbhī vedyāṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā yajñāyudhair ājyenātiṣaktā
agniḥ pacan rakṣatu tvā purastād indro rakṣatu dakṣiṇato marutvān
varuṇas tvā dṛṃhād dharuṇe pratīcyā uttarāt tvā somaḥ saṃ dadātai
pūtāḥ pavitraiḥ pavante abhrād divaṃ ca yanti pṛthivīṃ ca lokān
tā jīvalā jīvadhanyāḥ pratiṣṭhāḥ pātra āsiktāḥ pary agnir indhām
ā yanti divaḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante bhūmyāḥ sacante adhy antarikṣam
śuddhāḥ satīs tā u śumbhanta eva tā naḥ svargam abhi lokaṃ nayantu
uteva prabhvīr uta saṃmitāsa uta śukrāḥ śucayaś cāmṛtāsaḥ
tā odanaṃ daṃpatibhyāṃ praśiṣṭā āpaḥ śikṣantīḥ pacatā sunāthāḥ
saṃkhyātā stokāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante prāṇāpānaiḥ saṃmitā oṣadhībhiḥ
asaṃkhyātā opyamānāḥ suvarṇāḥ sarvaṃ vyāpuḥ śucayaḥ śucitvam
ud yodhanty abhi valganti taptāḥ phenam asyanti bahulāṃś ca bindūn
yoṣeva dṛṣṭvā patim ṛtviyāyaitais taṇḍulair bhavatā sam āpaḥ
ut thāpaya sīdato budhna enān adbhir ātmānam abhi saṃ spṛśantām
amāsi pātrair udakaṃ yad etan mitās taṇḍulāḥ pradiśo yadīmāḥ
pra yacha parśuṃ tvarayā harausam ahiṃsanta oṣadhīr dāntu parvan
vāsāṃ somaḥ pari rājyaṃ babhūvāmanyutā no vīrudho bhavantu
navaṃ barhir odanāya stṛṇīta priyaṃ hṛdaś cakṣuṣo valgv astu
tasmin devāḥ saha daivīr viśantv imaṃ prāśnantv ṛtubhir niṣadya
vanaspate stīrṇam ā sīda barhir agniṣṭobhaiḥ saṃmito devatābhiḥ
tvaṣṭreva rūpaṃ sukṛtaṃ svadhityainā ehāḥ pari pātre dadṛśrām
ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīchāt svaḥ pakvenābhy aśnavātai
upainaṃ jīvān pitaraś ca putrā etaṃ svargaṃ gamayāntam agneḥ
dhartā dhriyasva dharuṇe pṛthivyā acyutaṃ tvā devatāś cyāvayantu
taṃ tvā daṃpatī jīvantau jīvaputrāv ud vāsayātaḥ pary agnidhānāt
sarvānt samāgā abhijitya lokān yāvantaḥ kāmāḥ sam atītṛpas tān
vi gāhethām āyavanaṃ ca darvir ekasmin pātre adhy ud dharainam
upa stṛṇīhi prathaya purastād ghṛtena pātram abhi ghārayaitat
vāśrevosrā taruṇaṃ stanasyum imaṃ devāso abhihiṅkṛṇota
upāstarīr akaro lokam etam uruḥ prathatām asamaḥ svargaḥ
tasmiṃ chrayātai mahiṣaḥ suparṇo devā enaṃ devatābhyaḥ pra yachān
yadyaj jāyā pacati tvat paraḥparaḥ patir vā jāye tvat tiraḥ
saṃ tat sṛjethāṃ saha vāṃ tad astu saṃpādayantau saha lokam ekam
yāvanto asyāḥ pṛthivīṃ sacante asmat putrāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ
sarvāṃs tāṃ upa pātre hvayethāṃ nābhiṃ jānānāḥ śiśavaḥ samāyān
vasor yā dhārā madhunā prapīnā ghṛtena miśrā amṛtasya nābhayaḥ
sarvās tā ava rundhe svargaḥ ṣaṣṭyāṃ śaratsu nidhipā abhīchāt
nidhiṃ nidhipā abhy enam ichād anīśvarā abhitaḥ santu ye 'nye
asmābhir datto nihitaḥ svargas tribhiḥ kāṇḍais trīnt svargān arukṣat
agnī rakṣas tapatu yad videvaṃ kravyād piśāca iha mā pra pāsta
nudāma enam apa rudhmo asmad ādityā enam aṅgirasaḥ sacantām
ādityebhyo aṅgirobhyo madhv idaṃ ghṛtena miśraṃ prati vedayāmi
śuddhahastau brāhmaṇasyānihatyaitaṃ svargaṃ sukṛtāv apītam
idaṃ prāpam uttamaṃ kāṇḍam asya yasmāl lokāt parameṣṭhī samāpa
ā siñca sarpir ghṛtavat sam aṅgdhy eṣa bhāgo aṅgiraso no atra
satyāya ca tapase devatābhyo nidhiṃ śevadhiṃ pari dadma etam
mā no dyūte 'va gān mā samityāṃ mā smānyasmā ut sṛjatā purā mat
ahaṃ pacāmy ahaṃ dadāmi mamed u karman karuṇe 'dhi jāyā
kaumāro loko ajaniṣṭa putro 'nvārabhethāṃ vaya uttarāvat
na kilbiṣam atra nādhāro asti na yan mitraiḥ samamamāna eti
anūnaṃ pātraṃ nihitaṃ na etat paktāraṃ pakvaḥ punar ā viśāti
priyaṃ priyāṇāṃ kṛṇavāma tamas te yantu yatame dviṣanti
dhenur anaḍvān vayovaya āyad eva pauruṣeyam apa mṛtyuṃ nudantu
sam agnayaḥ vidur anyo anyaṃ ya oṣadhīḥ sacate yaś ca sindhūn
yāvanto devā divy ātapanti hiraṇyaṃ jyotiḥ pacato babhūva
eṣā tvacāṃ puruṣe saṃ babhūvānagnāḥ sarve paśavo ye anye
kṣatreṇātmānaṃ pari dhāpayātho 'motaṃ vāso mukham odanasya
yad akṣeṣu vadā yat samityāṃ yad vā vadā anṛtaṃ vittakāmyā
samānaṃ tantum abhi samvasānau tasmint sarvaṃ śamalaṃ sādayāthaḥ
varṣaṃ vanuṣvāpi gacha devāṃs tvaco dhūmaṃ pary ut pātayāsi
viśvavyacā ghṛtapṛṣṭho bhaviṣyant sayonir lokam upa yāhy etam
tanvaṃ svargo bahudhā vi cakre yathā vida ātmann anyavarṇām
apājait kṛṣṇāṃ ruśatīṃ punāno yā lohinī tāṃ te agnau juhomi
prācyai tvā diśe 'gnaye 'dhipataye 'sitāya rakṣitra ādityāyeṣumate
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
dakṣiṇāyai tvā diśa indrāyādhipataye tiraścirājaye rakṣitre yamāyeṣumate
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
pratīcyai tvā diśe varuṇāyādhipataye pṛdākave rakṣitre 'nnāyeṣumate
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
udīcyai tvā diśe somāyādhipataye svajāya rakṣitre 'śanyā iṣumatyai
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
dhruvāyai tvā diśe viṣṇave 'dhipataye kalmāṣagrīvāya rakṣitra oṣadhībhya iṣumatībhyaḥ
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
ūrdhvāyai tvā diśe bṛhaspataye 'dhipataye śvitrāya rakṣitre varṣāyeṣumate
etaṃ pari dadmas taṃ no gopāyatāsmākam aitoḥ
diṣṭaṃ no atra jarase ni neṣaj jarā mṛtyave pari ṇo dadātv atha pakvena saha saṃ bhavema
dadāmīty eva brūyād anu cainām abhutsata
vaśāṃ brahmabhyo yācadbhyas tat prajāvad apatyavat
prajayā sa vi krīṇīte paśubhiś copa dasyati
ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati
kūṭayāsya saṃ śīryante śloṇayā kāṭam ardati
baṇḍayā dahyante gṛhāḥ kāṇayā dīyate svam
vilohito adhiṣṭhānāc chakno vindati gopatim
tathā vaśāyāḥ saṃvidyaṃ duradabhnā hy ucyase
pador asyā adhiṣṭhānād viklindur nāma vindati
anāmanāt saṃ śīryante yā mukhenopajighrati
yo asyāḥ karṇāv āskunoty ā sa deveṣu vṛścate
lakṣma kurva iti manyate kanīyaḥ kṛṇute svam
yad asyāḥ kasmai cid bhogāya bālān kaś cit prakṛntati
tataḥ kiśorā mriyante vatsāṃś ca ghātuko vṛkaḥ
yad asyā gopatau satyā loma dhvāṅkṣo ajīhiḍat
tataḥ kumārā mriyante yakṣmo vindaty anāmanāt
yad asyāḥ palpūlanaṃ śakṛd dāsī samasyati
tato 'parūpaṃ jāyate tasmād avyeṣyad enasaḥ
jāyamānābhi jāyate devānt sabrāhmaṇān vaśā
tasmād brahmabhyo deyaiṣā tad āhuḥ svasya gopanam
ya enāṃ vanim āyanti teṣāṃ devakṛtā vaśā
brahmajyeyaṃ tad abruvan ya enāṃ nipriyāyate
ya ārṣeyebhyo yācadbhyo devānāṃ gāṃ na ditsati
ā sa deveṣu vṛścate brāhmaṇānāṃ ca manyave
yo asya syād vaśābhogo anyām icheta tarhi saḥ
hiṃste adattā puruṣaṃ yācitāṃ ca na ditsati
yathā śevadhir nihito brāhmaṇānāṃ tathā vaśā
tām etad achāyanti yasmin kasmiṃś ca jāyate
svam etad achāyanti yad vaśāṃ brāhmaṇā abhi
yathainān anyasmin jinīyād evāsyā nirodhanam
cared evā traihāyaṇād avijñātagadā satī
vaśāṃ ca vidyān nārada brāhmaṇās tarhy eṣyāḥ
ya enām avaśām āha devānāṃ nihitaṃ nidhim
ubhau tasmai bhavāśarvau parikramyeṣum asyataḥ
yo asyā ūdho na vedātho asyā stanān uta
ubhayenaivāsmai duhe dātuṃ ced aśakad vaśām
duradabhnainam ā śaye yācitāṃ ca na ditsati
nāsmai kāmāḥ sam ṛdhyante yām adattvā cikīrṣati
devā vaśām ayācan mukhaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇam
teṣāṃ sarveṣām adadad dheḍaṃ ny eti mānuṣaḥ
heḍaṃ paśūnāṃ ny eti brāhmaṇebhyo 'dadad vaśām
devānāṃ nihitaṃ bhāgaṃ martyaś cen nipriyāyate
yad anye śataṃ yāceyur brāhmaṇā gopatiṃ vaśām
athaināṃ devā abruvann evaṃ ha viduṣo vaśā
ya evaṃ viduṣe 'dattvāthānyebhyo dadad vaśām
durgā tasmā adhiṣṭhāne pṛthivī sahadevatā
devā vaśām ayācan yasminn agre ajāyata
tām etāṃ vidyān nāradaḥ saha devair ud ājata
anapatyam alpapaśuṃ vaśā kṛṇoti pūruṣam
brāhmaṇaiś ca yācitām athaināṃ nipriyāyate
agnīṣomābhyāṃ kāmāya mitrāya varuṇāya ca
tebhyo yācanti brāhmaṇās teṣv ā vṛścate 'dadat
yāvad asyā gopatir nopaśṛṇuyād ṛcaḥ svayam
cared asya tāvad goṣu nāsya śrutvā gṛhe vaset
yo asyā ṛca upaśrutyātha goṣv acīcarat
āyuś ca tasya bhūtiṃ ca devā vṛścanti hīḍitāḥ
vaśā carantī bahudhā devānāṃ nihito nidhiḥ
āviṣ kṛṇuṣva rūpāṇi yadā sthāma jighāṃsati
āvir ātmānaṃ kṛṇute yadā sthāma jighāṃsati
atho ha brahmabhyo vaśā yāñcyāya kṛṇute manaḥ
manasā saṃ kalpayati tad devāṃ api gachati
tato ha brahmāṇo vaśām upaprayanti yācitum
svadhākāreṇa pitṛbhyo yajñena devatābhyaḥ
dānena rājanyo vaśāyā mātur heḍam na gachati
vaśā mātā rājanyasya tathā saṃbhūtam agraśaḥ
tasyā āhur anarpaṇaṃ yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate
yathājyaṃ pragṛhītam ālumpet sruco agnaye
evā ha brahmabhyo vaśām agnaya ā vṛścate 'dadat
puroḍāśavatsā sudughā loke 'smā upa tiṣṭhati
sāsmai sarvān kāmān vaśā pradaduṣe duhe
sarvān kāmān yamarājye vaśā pradaduṣe duhe
athāhur nārakaṃ lokaṃ nirundhānasya yācitām
pravīyamānā carati kruddhā gopataye vaśā
vehataṃ mā manyamāno mṛtyoḥ pāśeṣu badhyatām
yo vehataṃ manyamāno 'mā ca pacate vaśām
apy asya putrān pautrāṃś ca yācayate bṛhaspatiḥ
mahad eṣāva tapati carantī goṣu gaur api
atho ha gopataye vaśādaduṣe viṣaṃ duhe
priyaṃ paśūnāṃ bhavati yad brahmabhyaḥ pradīyate
atho vaśāyās tat priyaṃ yad devatrā haviḥ syāt
yā vaśā udakalpayan devā yajñād udetya
tāsāṃ viliptyaṃ bhīmām udākuruta nāradaḥ
tāṃ devā amīmāṃsanta vaśeyā3m avaśeti
tām abravīn nārada eṣā vaśānāṃ vaśatameti
kati nu vaśā nārada yās tvaṃ vettha manuṣyajāḥ
tās tvā pṛchāmi vidvāṃsaṃ kasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇaḥ
viliptyā bṛhaspate yā ca sūtavaśā vaśā
tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām
namas te astu nāradānuṣṭhu viduṣe vaśā
katamāsāṃ bhīmatamā yām adattvā parābhavet
viliptī yā bṛhaspate 'tho sūtavaśā vaśā
tasyā nāśnīyād abrāhmaṇo ya āśaṃseta bhūtyām
trīṇi vai vaśājātāni viliptī sūtavaśā vaśā
tāḥ pra yached brahmabhyaḥ so 'nāvraskaḥ prajāpatau
etad vo brāhmaṇā havir iti manvīta yācitaḥ
vaśāṃ ced enaṃ yāceyur yā bhīmādaduṣo gṛhe
devā vaśāṃ pary avadan na no 'dād iti hīḍitāḥ
etābhir ṛgbhir bhedaṃ tasmād vai sa parābhavat
utaināṃ bhedo nādadād vaśām indreṇa yācitaḥ
tasmāt taṃ devā āgaso 'vṛścann ahamuttare
ye vaśāyā adānāya vadanti parirāpiṇaḥ
indrasya manyave jālmā ā vṛścante acittyā
ye gopatiṃ parāṇīyāthāhur mā dadā iti
rudrasyāstāṃ te hetīṃ pari yanty acittyā
yadi hutaṃ yady ahutām amā ca pacate vaśām
devānt sabrāhmaṇān ṛtvā jihmo lokān nir ṛchati
śrameṇa tapasā sṛṣṭā brahmaṇā vittā rte śritā
satyenāvṛtā śriyā prāvṛtā yaśasā parīvṛtā
svadhayā parihitā śraddhayā paryūḍhā dīkṣayā guptā yajñe pratiṣṭhitā loko nidhanam
brahma padavāyaṃ brāhmaṇo 'dhipatiḥ
tām ādadānasya brahmagavīṃ jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya
apa krāmati sūnṛtā vīryaṃ punyā lakṣmīḥ
ojaś ca tejaś ca sahaś ca balaṃ ca vāk cendriyaṃ ca śrīś ca dharmaś ca
brahma ca kṣatraṃ ca rāṣṭraṃ ca viśaś ca tviṣiś ca yaśaś ca varcaś ca draviṇaṃ ca
āyuś ca rūpaṃ ca nāma ca kīrtiś ca prāṇaś cāpānaś ca cakṣuś ca śrotraṃ ca
payaś ca rasaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca rtaṃ ca satyaṃ ceṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca prajā ca paśavaś ca
tāni sarvāṇy apa krāmanti brahmagavīm ādadānasya jinato brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyasya
saiṣā bhīmā brahmagavy aghaviṣā sākṣāt kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā
sarvāṇy asyāṃ ghorāṇi sarve ca mṛtyavaḥ
sarvāṇy asyāṃ krūrāṇi sarve puruṣavadhāḥ
sā brahmajyaṃ devapīyuṃ brahmagavy ādīyamānā mṛtyoḥ padvīṣa ā dyati
meniḥ śatavadhā hi sā brahmajyasya kṣitir hi sā
tasmād vai brāhmaṇānāṃ gaur durādharṣā vijānatā
vajro dhāvantī vaiśvānara udvītā
hetiḥ śaphān utkhidantī mahādevo 'pekṣamāṇā
kṣurapavir īkṣamāṇā vāśyamānābhi sphūrjati
mṛtyur hiṅkṛṇvaty ugro devaḥ puchaṃ paryasyantī
sarvajyāniḥ karṇau varīvarjayantī rājayakṣmo mehantī
menir duhyamānā śīrṣaktir dugdhā
sedir upatiṣṭhantī mithoyodhaḥ parāmṛṣṭā
śaravyā mukhe 'pinahyamāna ṛtir hanyamānā
aghaviṣā nipatantī tamo nipatitā
anugachantī prāṇān upa dāsayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya
vairaṃ vikṛtyamānā pautrādyaṃ vibhājyamānā
devahetir hriyamāṇā vyṛddhir hṛtā
pāpmādhidhīyamānā pāruṣyam avadhīyamānā
viṣaṃ prayasyantī takmā prayastā
aghaṃ pracyamānā duṣvapnyaṃ pakvā
mūlabarhaṇī paryākriyamāṇā kṣitiḥ paryākṛtā
asaṃjñā gandhena śug uddhriyamāṇāśīviṣa uddhṛtā
abhūtir upahriyamāṇā parābhūtir upahṛtā
śarvaḥ kruddhaḥ piśyamānā śimidā piśitā
avartir aśyamānā nirṛtir aśitā
aśitā lokāc chinatti brahmagavī brahmajyam asmāc cāmuṣmāc ca
tasyā āhananaṃ kṛtyā menir āśasanaṃ valaga ūbadhyam
asvagatā parihṇutā
agniḥ kravyād bhūtvā brahmagavī brahmajyaṃ praviśyātti
sarvāsyāṅgā parvā mūlāni vṛścati
chinatty asya pitṛbandhu parā bhāvayati mātṛbandhu
vivāhāṃ jñātīnt sarvān api kṣāpayati brahmagavī brahmajyasya kṣatriyeṇāpunardīyamānā
avāstum enam asvagam aprajasaṃ karoty aparāparaṇo bhavati kṣīyate
ya evaṃ viduṣo brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyo gām ādatte
kṣipraṃ vai tasyāhanane gṛdhrāḥ kurvata ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasyādahanaṃ pari nṛtyanti keśinīr āghnānāḥ pāṇinorasi kurvāṇāḥ pāpam ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasya vāstuṣu vṛkāḥ kurvata ailabam
kṣipraṃ vai tasya pṛchanti yat tad āsī3d idaṃ nu tā3d iti
chindhy ā chindhi pra chindhy api kṣāpaya kṣāpaya
ādadānam āṅgirasi brahmajyam upa dāsaya
vaiśvadevī hy ucyase kṛtyā kūlbajam āvṛtā
oṣantī samoṣantī brahmaṇo vajraḥ
kṣurapavir mṛtyur bhūtvā vi dhāva tvam
ā datse jinatāṃ varca iṣṭaṃ pūrtaṃ cāśiṣaḥ
ādāya jītaṃ jītāya loke 'muṣmin pra yachasi
aghnye padavīr bhava brāhmaṇasyābhiśastyā
meniḥ śaravyā bhavāghād aghaviṣā bhava
aghnye pra śiro jahi brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ
tvayā pramūrṇaṃ mṛditam agnir dahatu duścitam
vṛśca pra vṛśca saṃ vṛśca daha pra daha saṃ daha
brahmajyaṃ devy aghnya ā mūlād anusaṃdaha
yathāyād yamasādanāt pāpalokān parāvataḥ
evā tvaṃ devy aghnye brahmajyasya kṛtāgaso devapīyor arādhasaḥ
vajreṇa śataparvaṇā tīkṣṇena kṣurabhṛṣṭinā
pra skandhān pra śiro jahi
lomāny asya saṃ chindhi tvacam asya vi veṣṭaya
māṃsāny asya śātaya snāvāny asya saṃ vṛha
asthīny asya pīḍaya majjānam asya nir jahi
sarvāsyāṅgā parvāṇi vi śrathaya
agnir enaṃ kravyāt pṛthivyā nudatām ud oṣatu vāyur antarikṣān mahato varimṇaḥ
sūrya enaṃ divaḥ pra ṇudatāṃ ny oṣatu
udehi vājin yo apsv antar idaṃ rāṣṭraṃ pra viśa sūnṛtāvat
yo rohito viśvam idaṃ jajāna sa tvā rāṣṭrāya subhṛtaṃ bibhartu
ud vāja ā gan yo apsv antar viśa ā roha tvadyonayo yāḥ
somaṃ dadhāno 'pa oṣadhīr gāś catuṣpado dvipada ā veśayeha
yūyam ugrā marutaḥ pṛśnimātara indreṇa yujā pra mṛṇīta śatrūn
ā vo rohitaḥ śṛṇavat sudānavas triṣaptāso marutaḥ svādusaṃmudaḥ
ruho ruroha rohita ā ruroha garbho janīnāṃ januṣām upastham
tābhiḥ saṃrabdham anv avindan ṣaḍ urvīr gātuṃ prapaśyann iha rāṣṭram āhāḥ
ā te rāṣṭram iha rohito 'hārṣīd vy āsthan mṛdho abhayaṃ te abhūt
tasmai te dyāvāpṛthivī revatībhiḥ kāmaṃ duhātām iha śakvarībhiḥ
rohito dyāvāpṛthivī jajāna tatra tantuṃ parameṣṭhī tatāna
tatra śiśriye 'ja ekapādo 'dṛṃhad dyāvāpṛthivī balena
rohito dyāvāpṛthivī adṛṃhat tena sva stabhitaṃ tena nākaḥ
tenāntarikṣaṃ vimitā rajāṃsi tena devā amṛtam anv avindan
vi rohito amṛśad viśvarūpaṃ samākurvāṇaḥ praruho ruhaś ca
divaṃ rūḍhvā mahatā mahimnā saṃ te rāṣṭram anaktu payasā ghṛtena
yās te ruhaḥ praruho yās ta āruho yābhir āpṛṇāsi divam antarikṣam
tāsāṃ brahmaṇā payasā vavṛdhāno viśi rāṣṭre jāgṛhi rohitasya
yas te viśas tapasaḥ saṃbabhūvur vatsaṃ gāyatrīm anu tā ihāguḥ
tās tvā viśantu manasā śivena saṃmātā vatso abhy etu rohitaḥ
ūrdhvo rohito adhi nāke asthād viśvā rūpāṇi janayan yuvā kaviḥ
tigmenāgnir jyotiṣā vi bhāti tṛtīye cakre rajasi priyāṇi
sahasraśṛṅgo vṛṣabho jātavedā ghṛtāhutaḥ somapṛṣṭhaḥ suvīraḥ
mā mā hāsīn nāthito net tvā jahāni gopoṣaṃ ca me vīrapoṣaṃ ca dhehi
rohito yajñasya janitā mukhaṃ ca rohitāya vācā śrotreṇa manasā juhomi
rohitaṃ devā yanti sumanasyamānāḥ sa mā rohaiḥ sāmityai rohayatu
rohito yajñaṃ vy adadhād viśvakarmaṇe tasmāt tejāṃsy upa memāny āguḥ
voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani
ā tvā ruroha bṛhaty uta paṅktir ā kakub varcasā jātavedaḥ
ā tvā rurohoṣṇihākṣaro vaṣaṭkāra ā tvā ruroha rohito retasā saha
ayaṃ vaste garbhaṃ pṛthivyā divaṃ vaste 'yam antarikṣam
ayaṃ bradhnasya viṣṭapi svar lokān vy ānaśe
vācas pate pṛthivī naḥ syonā syonā yonis talpā naḥ suśevā
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary agnir āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
vācas pata ṛtavaḥ pañca ye nau vaiśvakarmaṇāḥ pari ye saṃbabhūvuḥ
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pari rohita āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
vācas pate saumanasaṃ manaś ca goṣṭhe no gā janaya yoniṣu prajāḥ
ihaiva prāṇaḥ sakhye no astu taṃ tvā parameṣṭhin pary aham āyuṣā varcasā dadhātu
pari tvā dhāt savitā devo agnir varcasā mitrāvaruṇāv abhi tvā
sarvā arātīr avakrāmann ehīdaṃ rāṣṭram akaraḥ sunṛtāvat
yaṃ tvā pṛṣatī rathe praṣṭir vahati rohita
śubhā yāsi riṇann apaḥ
anuvratā rohiṇī rohitasya sūriḥ suvarṇā bṛhatī suvarcāḥ
tayā vājān viśvarūpāṃ jayema tayā viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhi ṣyāma
idaṃ sado rohiṇī rohitasyāsau panthāḥ pṛṣatī yena yāti
tāṃ gandharvāḥ kaśyapā un nayanti tāṃ rakṣanti kavayo 'pramādam
sūryasyāśvā harayaḥ ketumantaḥ sadā vahanty amṛtāḥ sukhaṃ ratham
ghṛtapāvā rohito bhrājamāno divaṃ devaḥ pṛṣatīm ā viveśa
yo rohito vṛṣabhas tigmaśṛṅgaḥ pary agniṃ pari sūryaṃ babhūva
yo viṣṭabhnāti pṛthivīṃ divaṃ ca tasmād devā adhi sṛṣṭīḥ sṛjante
rohito divam āruhan mahataḥ pary arṇavāt
sarvo ruroha rohito ruhaḥ
vi mimīṣva payasvatīṃ ghṛtācīṃ devānāṃ dhenur anapaspṛg eṣā
indraḥ somaṃ pibatu kṣemo astv agniḥ pra stautu vi mṛdho nudasva
samiddho agniḥ samidhāno ghṛtavṛddho ghṛtāhutaḥ
abhīṣāṭ viśvāṣāḍ agniḥ sapatnān hantu ye mama
hantv enān pra dahatv arir yo naḥ pṛtanyati
kravyādāgninā vayaṃ sapatnān pra dahāmasi
avācīnān ava jahīndra vajreṇa bāhumān
adhā sapatnān māmakān agnes tejobhir ādiṣi
agne sapatnān adharān pādayāsmad vyathayā sajātam utpipānaṃ bṛhaspate
indrāgnī mitrāvaruṇāv adhare padyantām apratimanyūyamānāḥ
udyaṃs tvaṃ deva sūrya sapatnān ava me jahi
avainān aśmanā jahi te yantv adhamaṃ tamaḥ
vatso virājo vṛṣabho matīnām ā ruroha śukrapṛṣṭho 'ntarikṣam
ghṛtenārkam abhy arcanti vatsaṃ brahma santaṃ brahmaṇā vardhayanti
divaṃ ca roha pṛthivīṃ ca roha rāṣṭraṃ ca roha draviṇaṃ ca roha
prajāṃ ca rohāmṛtaṃ ca roha rohitena tanvaṃ saṃ spṛṣasva
ye devā rāṣṭrabhṛto 'bhito yanti sūryam
taiṣ ṭe rohitaḥ samvidāno rāṣṭraṃ dadhātu sumanasyamānaḥ
ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti
tiraḥ samudram ati rocase 'rṇavam
rohite dyāvāpṛthivī adhi śrite vasujiti gojiti saṃdhanājiti
sahasraṃ yasya janimāni sapta ca voceyaṃ te nābhiṃ bhuvanasyādhi majmani
yaśā yāsi pradiśo diśaś ca yaśāḥ paśūnām uta carṣaṇīnām
yaśāḥ pṛthivyā adityā upasthe 'haṃ bhūyāsaṃ saviteva cāruḥ
amutra sann iha vetthetaḥ saṃs tāni paśyasi
itaḥ paśyanti rocanaṃ divi sūryaṃ vipaścitam
devo devān marcayasy antaś carasy arṇave
samānam agnim indhate taṃ viduḥ kavayaḥ pare
avaḥ pareṇa para enāvareṇa padā vatsaṃ bibratī gaur ud asthāt
sā kadrīcī kaṃ svid ardhaṃ parāgāt kva svit sūte nahi yūthe asmin
ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpady aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī
sahasrākṣarā bhuvanasya paṅktis tasyāḥ samudrā adhi vi kṣaranti
ārohan dyām amṛtaḥ prāva me vacaḥ
ut tvā yajñā brahmapūtā vahanty adhvagato harayas tvā vahanti
veda tat te amartya yat ta ākramaṇaṃ divi
yat te sadhasthaṃ parame vyoman
sūryo dyāṃ sūryaḥ pṛṭhivīṃ sūrya āpo'ti paśyati
sūryo bhūtasyaikaṃ cakṣur ā ruroha divaṃ mahīm
urvīr āsan paridhayo vedir bhūmir akalpata
tatraitāv agnī ādhatta himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ ca rohitaḥ
himaṃ ghraṃsaṃ cādhāya yūpān kṛtvā parvatān
varṣājyāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
svarvido rohitasya brahmaṇāgniḥ sam idhyate
tasmād ghraṃsas tasmād dhimas tasmād yajño 'jāyata
brahmaṇāgnī vāvṛdhānau brahmavṛddhau brahmāhutau
brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
satye anyaḥ samāhito 'psv anyaḥ sam idhyate
brahmeddhāv agnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
yaṃ vātaḥ pariśumbhati yaṃ vendro brahmaṇaspatiḥ
brahmeddhāvagnī ījāte rohitasya svarvidaḥ
vediṃ bhūmiṃ kalpayitvā divaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇām
ghraṃsaṃ tad agniṃ kṛtvā cakāra viśvam ātmanvad varṣeṇājyena rohitaḥ
varṣam ājam ghraṃso agnir vedir bhūmir akalpata
tatraitān parvatān agnir gīrbhir ūrdhvāṃ akalpayat
gīrbhir ūrdhvān kalpayitvā rohito bhūmim abravīt
tvayīdaṃ sarvaṃ jāyatāṃ yad bhūtaṃ yac ca bhāvyam
sa yajñaḥ prathamo bhūto bhavyo ajāyata
tasmād dha jajña idaṃ sarvaṃ yat kiṃ cedaṃ virocate rohitena ṛṣiṇābhṛtam
yaś ca gāṃ padā sphurati pratyaṅ sūryaṃ ca mehati
tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param
yo mābhichāyam atyeṣi māṃ cāgniṃ cāntarā
tasya vṛścāmi te mūlaṃ na chāyāṃ karavo 'param
yo adya deva sūrya tvāṃ ca māṃ cāntarāyati
duṣvapnyaṃ tasmiṃ chamalaṃ duritāni ca mṛjmahe
mā pra gāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñād indra sominaḥ
mānta sthur no arātayaḥ
yo yajñasya prasādhanas tantur deveṣv ātataḥ
tam āhutam aśīmahi
ud asya ketavo divi śukrā bhrājanta īrate
ādityasya nṛcakṣaso mahivratasya mīḍhuṣaḥ
diśāṃ prajñānāṃ svarayantam arciṣā supakṣam āśuṃ patayantam arṇave
stavāma sūryaṃ bhuvanasya gopāṃ yo raśmibhir diśa ābhāti sarvāḥ
yat prāṅ pratyaṅ svadhayā yāsi śībhaṃ nānārūpe ahanī karṣi māyayā
tad āditya mahi tat te mahi śravo yad eko viśvaṃ pari bhūma jāyase
vipaścitaṃ taraṇiṃ bhrājamānaṃ vahanti yaṃ haritaḥ sapta bahvīḥ
srutād yam attrir divam unnināya taṃ tvā paśyanti pariyāntam ājim
mā tvā dabhan pariyāntam ājiṃ svasti durgāṃ ati yāhi śībham
divaṃ ca sūrya pṛthivīṃ ca devīm ahorātre vimimāno yad eṣi
svasti te sūrya carase rathāya yenobhāv antau pariyāsi sadyaḥ
yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ
sukhaṃ sūrya ratham aṃśumantaṃ syonaṃ suvahnim adhi tiṣṭha vājinam
yaṃ te vahanti harito vahiṣṭhāḥ śatam aśvā yadi vā sapta bahvīḥ
sapta sūryo harito yātave rathe hiraṇyatvacaso bṛhatīr ayukta
amoci śukro rajasaḥ parastād vidhūya devas tamo divam āruhat
ut ketunā bṛhatā deva āgann apāvṛk tamo 'bhi jyotir aśrait
divyaḥ suparṇaḥ sa vīro vy akhyad aditeḥ putro bhuvanāni viśvā
udyan raśmīn ā tanuṣe viśvā rupāṇi puṣyasi
ubhā samudrau kratunā vi bhāsi sarvāṃl lokān paribhūr bhrājamānaḥ
pūrvāparaṃ carato māyayaitau śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto 'rṇavam
viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭe hairaṇyair anyaṃ harito vahanti
divi tvāttrir adhārayat sūryā māsāya kartave
sa eṣi sudhṛtas tapan viśvā bhūtāvacākaśat
ubhāv antau sam arṣasi vatsaḥ saṃmātarāv iva
nanv etad itaḥ purā brahma devā amī viduḥ
yat samudram anu śritaṃ tat siṣāsati sūryaḥ
adhvāsya vitato mahān pūrvaś cāparaś ca yaḥ
taṃ sam āpnoti jūtibhis tato nāpa cikitsati
tenāmṛtasya bhakṣaṃ devānāṃ nāva rundhate
ud u tyaṃ jātavedasaṃ devaṃ vahanti ketavaḥ
dṛśe viśvāya sūryam
apa tye tāyavo yathā nakṣatrā yanty aktubhiḥ
sūrāya viśvacakṣase
adṛśrann asya ketavo vi raśmayo janāṃ anu
bhrājanto agnayo yathā
taraṇir viśvadarśato jyotiṣkṛd asi sūrya
viśvam ā bhāsi rocana
pratyaṅ devānāṃ viśaḥ pratyaṅṅ ud eṣi mānuṣīḥ
pratyaṅ viśvaṃ svar dṛśe
yenā pāvaka cakṣasā bhuraṇyantaṃ janāṃ anu
tvaṃ varuṇa paśyasi
vi dyām eṣi rajas pṛthv ahar mimāno aktubhiḥ
paśyan janmāni sūrya
sapta tvā harito rathe vahanti deva sūrya
śociṣkeśaṃ vicakṣaṇam
ayukta sapta śundhyuvaḥ sūro rathasya naptyaḥ
tābhir yāti svayuktibhiḥ
rohito divam āruhat tapasā tapasvī
sa yonim aiti sa u jāyate punaḥ sa devānām adhipatir babhūva
yo viśvacarṣaṇir uta viśvatomukho yo viśvataspāṇir uta viśvataspṛthaḥ
saṃ bāhubhyāṃ bharati saṃ patatrair dyāvāpṛthivī janayan deva ekaḥ
ekapād dvipado bhūyo vi cakrame dvipāt tripādam abhy eti paścāt
dvipād dha ṣaṭpado bhūyo vi cakrame ta ekapadas tanvaṃ sam āsate
atandro yāsyan harito yad āsthād dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ
ketumān udyant sahamāno rajāṃsi viśvā āditya pravato vi bhāsi
baṇ mahāṃ asi sūrya baḍ āditya mahāṃ asi
mahāṃs te mahato mahimā tvam āditya mahāṃ asi
rocase divi rocase antarikṣe pataṅga pṛthivyāṃ rocase rocase apsv antaḥ
ubhā samudrau rucyā vy āpitha devo devāsi mahiṣaḥ svarjit
arvāṅ parastāt prayato vyadhva āśur vipaścit patayan pataṅgaḥ
viṣṇur vicittaḥ śavasādhitiṣṭhan pra ketunā sahate viśvam ejat
citrāś cikitvān mahiṣaḥ suparṇa ārocayan rodasī antarikṣam
ahorātre pari sūryaṃ vasāne prāsya viśvā tirato vīryāṇi
tigmo vibhrājan tanvaṃ śiśāno 'raṃgamāsaḥ pravato rarāṇaḥ
jyotiṣmān pakṣī mahiṣo vayodhā viśvā āsthāt pradiśaḥ kalpamānaḥ
citraṃ devānām ketur anīkaṃ jyotiṣmān pradiśaḥ sūrya udyan
divākaro 'ti dyumnais tamāṃsi viśvātārīd duritāni śukraḥ
citraṃ devānām ud agād anīkaṃ cakṣur mitrasya varuṇasyāgneḥ
āprād dyāvāpṛthivī antarikṣaṃ sūrya ātmā jagatas tasthuṣaś ca
uccā patantam aruṇaṃ suparṇaṃ madhye divas taraṇiṃ bhrājamānam
paśyama tvā savitāraṃ yam āhur ajasraṃ jyotir yad avindad attriḥ
divas pṛṣṭhe dhāvamānaṃ suparṇam adityāḥ putraṃ nāthakāma upa yāmi bhītaḥ
sa naḥ sūrya pra tira dīrgham āyur mā riṣāma sumatau te syāma
sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam
sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā
rohitaḥ kālo abhavad rohito 'gre prajāpatiḥ
rohito yajñānāṃ mukhaṃ rohitaḥ svar ābharat
rohito loko abhavad rohito 'ty atapad divam
rohito raśmibhir bhūmiṃ samudram anu saṃ carat
sarvā diśaḥ sam acarad rohito 'dhipatir divaḥ
divaṃ samudram ād bhūmiṃ sarvaṃ bhūtaṃ vi rakṣati
ārohan chukro bṛhatīr atandro dve rūpe kṛṇute rocamānaḥ
citraś cikitvān mahiṣo vātamāyā yāvato lokān abhi yad vibhāti
abhy anyad eti pary anyad asyate 'horātrābhyāṃ mahiṣaḥ kalpamānaḥ
sūryaṃ vayaṃ rajasi kṣiyantaṃ gātuvidaṃ havāmahe nādhamānāḥ
pṛthivīpro mahiṣo nādhamānasya gātur adabdhacakṣuḥ pari viśvaṃ babhūva
viśvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi
pary asya mahimā pṛthivīṃ samudraṃ jyotiṣā vibhrājan pari dyām antarikṣam
sarvaṃ saṃpaśyant suvidatro yajatra idaṃ śṛṇotu yad ahaṃ bravīmi
abodhy agniḥ samidhā janānāṃ prati dhenum ivāyatīm uṣasam
yahvā iva pra vayām ujjihānāḥ pra bhānavaḥ sisrate nākam acha
ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī jajāna yo drāpim kṛtvā bhuvanāni vaste
yasmin kṣiyanti pradiśaḥ ṣaḍ urvīr yāḥ pataṅgo anu vicākaśīti
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
yasmād vātā ṛtuthā pavante yasmāt samudrā adhi vikṣaranti
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
yo mārayati prāṇayati yasmāt prāṇanti bhuvanāni viśvā
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
yaḥ prāṇena dyāvāpṛthivī tarpayaty apānena samudrasya jaṭharaṃ yaḥ piparti
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
yasmin virāṭ parameṣṭhī prajāpatir agnir vaiśvānaraḥ saha paṅktyā śritaḥ
yaḥ parasya prāṇaṃ paramasya teja ādade
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
yasmin ṣaḍ urvīḥ pañca diśo adhiśritāś catasra āpo yajñasya trayo 'kṣarāḥ
yo antarā rodasī kruddhaś cakṣuṣaikṣata
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇam jināti
yo annādo annapatir babhūva brahmaṇas patir uta yaḥ
bhūto bhaviṣyat bhuvanasya yas patiḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ahorātrair vimitaṃ triṃśadaṅgaṃ trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ yo nirmimīte
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
kṛsṇaṃ niyānaṃ harayaḥ suparṇā apo vasānā divam ut patanti
ta āvavṛtrant sadanād ṛtasya
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
yat te candraṃ kaśyapa rocanāvad yat saṃhitaṃ puṣkalaṃ citrabhānu yasmint sūryā ārpitāḥ sapta sākam
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
bṛhad enam anu vaste purastād rathaṃtaraṃ prati gṛhṇāti paścāt
jyotir vasāne sadam apramādam
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
bṛhad anyataḥ pakṣa āsīd rathaṃtaram anyataḥ sabale sadhrīcī
yad rohitam ajanayanta devāḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
sa varuṇaḥ sāyam agnir bhavati sa mitro bhavati prātar udyan
sa savitā bhūtvāntarikṣeṇa yāti sa indro bhūtvā tapati madhyato divam
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
sahasrāhṇyaṃ viyatāv asya pakṣau harer haṃsasya patataḥ svargam
sa devānt sarvān urasy upadadya saṃpaśyan yāti bhuvanāni viśvā
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ayaṃ sa devo apsv antaḥ sahasramūlaḥ paruśāko attriḥ
ya idaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ jajāna
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
śukraṃ vahanti harayo raghuṣyado devaṃ divi varcasā bhrājamānam
yasyordhvā divaṃ tanvas tapanty arvāṅ suvarṇaiḥ paṭarair vi bhāti
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
yenādityān haritaḥ samvahanti yena yajñena bahavo yanti prajānantaḥ
yad ekaṃ jyotir bahudhā vibhāti
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
sapta yuñjanti ratham ekacakram eko aśvo vahati saptanāmā
trinābhi cakram ajaram anarvaṃ yatremā viśvā bhuvanādhi tasthuḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
aṣṭadhā yukto vahati vahnir ugraḥ pitā devānāṃ janitā matīnām
ṛtasya tantuṃ manasā mimānaḥ sarvā diśaḥ pavate mātariśvā
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
saṃyañcaṃ tantuṃ pradiśo 'nu sarvā antar gāyatryām amṛtasya garbhe
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
nimrucas tisro vyuṣo ha tisras trīṇi rajāṃsi divo aṅga tisraḥ
vidmā te agne tredhā janitraṃ tredhā devānāṃ janimāni vidma
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
vi ya aurṇot pṛthivīṃ jāyamāna ā samudram adadhāt antarikṣe
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ud vepaya rohita pra kṣiṇīhi brahmajyasya prati muñca pāśān
tvam agne kratubhiḥ ketubhir hito 'rkaḥ samiddha ud arocathā divi
kim abhy ārcan marutaḥ pṛśnimātaro yad rohitam ajanayanta devāḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ya ātmadā baladā yasya viśva upāsate praśiṣaṃ yasya devāḥ
yo 'syeśe dvipado yaś catuṣpadaḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
ekapād dvipado bhūyo vi cakrame dvipāt tripādam abhy eti paścāt
catuṣpāc cakre dvipadām abhisvare saṃpaśyan paṅktim upatiṣṭhamānaḥ
tasya devasya kruddhasyaitad āgo ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ jināti
kṛṣṇāyaḥ putro arjuno rātryā vatso 'jāyata
sa ha dyām adhi rohati ruho ruroha rohitaḥ
sa eti savitā svar divas pṛṣṭhe 'vacākaśat
raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ
sa dhātā sa vidhartā sa vāyur nabha ucchritam
so 'ryamā sa varuṇaḥ sa rudraḥ sa mahādevaḥ
so agniḥ sa u sūryaḥ sa u eva mahāyamaḥ
taṃ vatsā upa tiṣṭhanty ekaśīrṣāṇo yutā daśa
paścāt prāñca ā tanvanti yad udeti vi bhāsati
tasyaiṣa māruto gaṇaḥ sa eti śikyākṛtaḥ
raśmibhir nabha ābhṛtaṃ mahendra ety āvṛtaḥ
tasyeme nava kośā viṣṭambhā navadhā hitāḥ
sa prajābhyo vi paśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na
tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva
ete asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti
kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca
ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda
na dvitīyo na tṛtīyaś caturtho nāpy ucyate
na pañcamo na ṣaṣṭhaḥ saptamo nāpy ucyate
nāṣṭamo na navamo daśamo nāpy ucyate
sa sarvasmai vi paśyati yac ca prāṇati yac ca na
tam idaṃ nigataṃ sahaḥ sa eṣa eka ekavṛd eka eva
sarve asmin devā ekavṛto bhavanti
brahma ca tapaś ca kīrtiś ca yaśaś cāmbhaś ca nabhaś ca brāhmaṇavarcasaṃ cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca
bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca śraddhā ca ruciś ca svargaś ca svadhā ca
ya etaṃ devam ekavṛtaṃ veda
sa eva mṛtyuḥ so 'mṛtaṃ so 'bhvaṃ sa rakṣaḥ
sa rudro vasuvanir vasudeye namovāke vaṣaṭkāro 'nu saṃhitaḥ
tasyeme sarve yātava upa praśiṣam āsate
tasyāmū sarvā nakṣatrā vaśe candramasā saha
sa vā ahno 'jāyata tasmād ahar ajāyata
sa vai rātryā ajāyata tasmād rātrir ajāyata
sa vā antarikṣād ajāyata tasmād antarikṣam ajāyata
sa vai vāyor ajāyata tasmād vāyur ajāyata
sa vai divo 'jāyata tasmād dyaur adhi ajāyata
sa vai digbhyo 'jāyata tasmād diśo 'jāyanta
sa vai bhūmer ajāyata tasmād bhūmir ajāyata
sa vā agner ajāyata tasmād agnir ajāyata
sa vā adbhyo 'jāyata tasmād āpo 'jāyanta
sa vā ṛgbhyo 'jāyata tasmād ṛco 'jāyanta
sa vai yajñād ajāyata tasmād yajño 'jāyata
sa yajñas tasya yajñaḥ sa yajñasya śiras kṛtam
sa stanayati sa vi dyotate sa u aśmānam asyati
pāpāya vā bhadrāya vā puruṣāyāsurāya vā
yad vā kṛṇoṣy oṣadhīr yad vā varṣasi bhadrayā yad vā janyam avīvṛdhaḥ
tāvāṃs te maghavan mahimopo te tanvaḥ śatam
upo te badhve baddhāni yadi vāsi nyarbudam
bhūyān indro namurād bhūyān indrāsi mṛtyubhyaḥ
bhūyān arātyāḥ śacyāḥ patis tvam indrāsi vibhūḥ prabhūr iti tvopāsmahe vayam
namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata
annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena
ambho amo mahaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam
ambho aruṇaṃ rajataṃ rajaḥ saha iti tvopāsmahe vayam
uruḥ pṛthuḥ subhūr bhuva iti tvopāsmahe vayam
pratho varo vyaco loka iti tvopāsmahe vayam
bhavadvasur idadvasuḥ saṃyadvasur āyadvasur iti tvopāsmahe vayam
namas te astu paśyata paśya mā paśyata
annādyena yaśasā tejasā brāhmaṇavarcasena
satyenottabhitā bhūmiḥ sūryeṇottabhitā dyauḥ
ṛtenādityās tiṣṭhanti divi somo adhi śritaḥ
somenādityā balinaḥ somena pṛthivī mahī
atho nakṣatrāṇām eṣām upasthe soma āhitaḥ
somaṃ manyate papivān yat saṃpiṃṣanty oṣadhim
somaṃ yaṃ brahmāṇo vidur na tasyāśnāti pārthivaḥ
yat tvā soma prapibanti tata ā pyāyase punaḥ
vāyuḥ somasya rakṣitā samānāṃ māsa ākṛtiḥ
āchadvidhānair gupito bārhataiḥ soma rakṣitaḥ
grāvṇām ic chṛṇvan tiṣṭhasi na te aśnāti pārthivaḥ
cittir ā upabarhaṇaṃ cakṣur ā abhyañjanam
dyaur bhūmiḥ kośa āsīd yad ayāt sūryā patim
raibhy āsīd anudeyī nārāśaṃsī nyocanī
suryāyā bhadram id vāso gāthayati pariṣkṛtā
stomā āsan pratidhayaḥ kurīraṃ chanda opaśaḥ
sūryāyā aśvinā varāgnir āsīt purogavaḥ
somo vadhūyur abhavad aśvināstām ubhā varā
sūryāṃ yat patye śaṃsantīṃ manasā savitādadāt
mano asyā ana āsīd dyaur āsīd uta chadiḥ
śukrāv anaḍvāhāv āstāṃ yad ayāt sūryā patim
ṛksāmābhyām abhihitau gāvau te sāmanāv aitām
śrotre te cakre āstāṃ divi panthāś carācaraḥ
śucī te cakre yātyā vyāno akṣa āhataḥ
ano manasmayaṃ sūryārohat prayatī patim
sūryāyā vahatuḥ prāgāt savitā yam avāsṛjat
maghāsu hanyante gāvaḥ phalgunīṣu vy uhyate
yad aśvinā pṛchamānāv ayātaṃ tricakreṇa vahatuṃ sūryāyāḥ
kvaikaṃ cakraṃ vām āsīt kva deṣṭrāya tasthathuḥ
yad ayātaṃ śubhas patī vareyaṃ sūryām upa
viśve devā anu tad vām ajānan putraḥ pitaram avṛṇīta pūṣā
dve te cakre sūrye brahmāṇa ṛtuthā viduḥ
athaikaṃ cakraṃ yad guhā tad addhātaya id viduḥ
aryamaṇaṃ yajāmahe subandhuṃ pativedanam
urvārukam iva bandhanāt preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ
preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ subaddhām amutas karam
yatheyam indra mīḍhvaḥ suputrā subhagāsati
pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ
ṛtasya yonau sukṛtasya loke syonaṃ te astu sahasaṃbhalāyai
bhagas tveto nayatu hastagṛhyāśvinā tvā pra vahatāṃ rathena
gṛhān gacha gṛhapatnī yathāso vaśinī tvaṃ vidatham ā vadāsi
iha priyaṃ prajāyai te sam ṛdhyatām asmin gṛhe gārhapatyāya jāgṛhi
enā patyā tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasvātha jirvir vidatham ā vadāsi
ihaiva staṃ mā vi yauṣṭaṃ viśvam āyur vy aśnutam
krīḍantau putrair naptṛbhir modamānau svastakau
pūrvāparaṃ carato māyaitau śiśū krīḍantau pari yāto 'rṇavam
viśvānyo bhuvanā vicaṣṭa ṛtūṃr anyo vidadhaj jāyase navaḥ
navonavo bhavasi jāyamāno 'hnāṃ ketur uṣasām eṣy agram
bhāgaṃ devebhyo vi dadhāsy āyan pra candramas tirase dīrgham āyuḥ
parā dehi śāmulyaṃ brahmabhyo vi bhajā vasu
kṛtyaiṣā padvatī bhūtvā jāyā viśate patim
nīlalohitaṃ bhavati kṛtyāsaktir vy ajyate
edhante asyā jñātayaḥ patir bandheṣu badhyate
aślīlā tanūr bhavati ruśatī pāpayāmuyā
patir yad vadhvo vāsasaḥ svam aṅgam abhyūrṇute
āśasanaṃ viśasanam atho adhivikartanam
sūryāyāḥ paśya rūpāṇi tāni brahmota śumbhati
tṛṣṭam etat kaṭukam apāṣṭhavad viṣavan naitad attave
sūryāṃ yo brahmā veda sa id vādhūyam arhati
sa it tat syonaṃ harati brahmā vāsaḥ sumaṅgalam
prāyaścittiṃ yo adhyeti yena jāyā na riṣyati
yuvaṃ bhagaṃ saṃ bharataṃ samṛddham ṛtaṃ vadantāv ṛtodyeṣu
brahmaṇas pate patim asyai rocaya cāru saṃbhalo vadatu vācam etām
ihed asātha na paro gamāthemaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā vardhayātha
śubhaṃ yatīr usriyāḥ somavarcaso viśve devāḥ krann iha vo manāṃsi
imaṃ gāvaḥ prajayā saṃ viśāthāyaṃ devānāṃ na mināti bhāgam
asmai vaḥ pūṣā marutaś ca sarve asmai vo dhātā savitā suvāti
anṛkṣarā ṛjavaḥ santu panthano yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti no vareyam
saṃ bhagena sam aryamṇā saṃ dhātā sṛjatu varcasā
yac ca varco akṣeṣu surāyāṃ ca yad āhitam
yad goṣv aśvinā varcas tenemāṃ varcasāvatam
yena mahānaghnyā jaghanam aśvinā yena vā surā
yenākṣā abhyaṣicyanta tenemāṃ varcasāvatam
yo anidhmo dīdayad apsv antar yaṃ viprāsa īḍate adhvareṣu
apāṃ napān madhumatīr apo dā yābhir indro vāvṛdhe vīryāvān
idam ahaṃ ruśantaṃ grābhaṃ tanūdūṣim apohāmi
yo bhadro rocanas tam ud acāmi
āsyai brāhmaṇāḥ snapanīr harantv avīraghnīr ud ajantv āpaḥ
aryamṇo agniṃ pary etu pūṣan pratīkṣante śvaśuro devaraś ca
śaṃ te hiraṇyaṃ śam u santv āpaḥ śaṃ methir bhavatu śaṃ yugasya tardma
śaṃ ta āpaḥ śatapavitrā bhavantu śam u patyā tanvaṃ saṃ spṛśasva
khe rathasya khe 'nasaḥ khe yugasya śatakrato
apālām indra triṣ pūtvākṛṇoḥ sūryatvacam
āśāsānā saumanasaṃ prajāṃ saubhāgyaṃ rayim
patyur anuvratā bhūtvā saṃ nahyasvāmṛtāya kam
yathā sindhur nadīnāṃ sāmrājyaṃ suṣuve vṛṣā
evā tvaṃ samrājñy edhi patyur astaṃ paretya
samrājñy edhi śvaśureṣu samrājñy uta devṛṣu
nanānduḥ samrājñy edhi samrājñy uta śvaśrvāḥ
yā akṛntann avayan yāś ca tatnire yā devīr antāṃ abhito 'dadanta
tās tvā jarase saṃ vyayantv āyuṣmatīdaṃ pari dhatsva vāsaḥ
jīvaṃ rudanti vi nayanty adhvaraṃ dīrghām anu prasitiṃ dīdhyur naraḥ
vāmaṃ pitṛbhyo ya idaṃ samīrire mayaḥ patibhyo janaye pariṣvaje
syonaṃ dhruvaṃ prajāyai dhārayāmi te 'śmānaṃ devyāḥ pṛthivyā upasthe
tam ā tiṣṭhānumādyā suvarcā dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
yenāgnir asyā bhūmyā hastaṃ jagrāha dakṣiṇam
tena gṛhṇāmi te hastaṃ mā vyathiṣṭhā mayā saha prajayā ca dhanena ca
devas te savitā hastaṃ gṛhṇātu somo rājā suprajasaṃ kṛṇotu
agniḥ subhagāṃ jatavedāḥ patye patnīṃ jaradaṣṭim kṛṇotu
gṛhṇāmi te saubhagatvāya hastaṃ mayā patyā jaradaṣṭir yathāsaḥ
bhago aryamā savitā puraṃdhir mahyaṃ tvādur gārhapatyāya devāḥ
bhagas te hastam agrahīt savitā hastam agrahīt
patnī tvam asi dharmaṇāhaṃ gṛhapatis tava
mameyam astu poṣyā mahyaṃ tvādād bṛhaspatiḥ
mayā patyā prajāvati saṃ jīva śaradaḥ śatam
tvaṣṭā vāso vy adadhāc chubhe kaṃ bṛhaspateḥ praśiṣā kavīnām
tenemāṃ nārīṃ savitā bhagaś ca sūryām iva pari dhattāṃ prajayā
indrāgnī dyāvāpṛthivī mātariśvā mitrāvaruṇā bhago aśvinobhā
bṛhaspatir maruto brahma soma imāṃ nāriṃ prajayā vardhayantu
bṛhaspatiḥ prathamaḥ sūryāyāḥ śīrṣe keśāṃ akalpayat
tenemām aśvinā nārīṃ patye saṃ śobhayāmasi
idaṃ tad rūpaṃ yad avasta yoṣā jāyāṃ jijñāse manasā carantīm
tām anv artiṣye sakhibhir navagvaiḥ ka imān vidvān vi cacarta pāśān
ahaṃ vi ṣyāmi mayi rūpam asyā vedad it paśyan manasaḥ kulāyam
na steyam admi manasod amucye svayaṃ śrathnāno varuṇasya pāśān
pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitā suśevāḥ
uruṃ lokaṃ sugam atra panthāṃ kṛṇomi tubhyaṃ sahapatnyai vadhu
ud yachadhvam apa rakṣo hanāthemaṃ nārīṃ sukṛte dadhāta
dhātā vipaścit patim asyai viveda bhago rājā pura etu prajānan
bhagas tatakṣa caturaḥ pādān bhagas tatakṣa catvāry uṣpalāni
tvaṣṭā pipeśa madhyato 'nu vardhrānt sā no astu sumaṅgalī
sukiṃśukaṃ vahatuṃ viśvarūpaṃ hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvṛtaṃ sucakram
ā roha sūrye amṛtasya lokaṃ syonaṃ patibhyo vahatuṃ kṛṇu tvam
abhrātṛghnīṃ varuṇāpaśughnīṃ bṛhaspate
indrāpatighnīm putriṇīm āsmabhyaṃ savitar vaha
mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ kumāryaṃ sthūṇe devakṛte pathi
śālāyā devyā dvāraṃ syonaṃ kṛṇmo vadhūpatham
brahmāparaṃ yujyatāṃ brahma pūrvaṃ brahmāntato madhyato brahma sarvataḥ
anāvyādhāṃ devapurāṃ prapadya śivā syonā patiloke vi rāja
tubhyam agre pary avahant sūryāṃ vahatunā saha
sa naḥ patibhyo jāyāṃ dā agne prajayā saha
punaḥ patnīm agnir adād āyuṣā saha varcasā
dīrghāyur asyā yaḥ patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
somasya jāyā prathamaṃ gandharvas te 'paraḥ patiḥ
tṛtīyo agniṣ ṭe patis turīyas te manuṣyajāḥ
somo dadad gandharvāya gandharvo dadad agnaye
rayiṃ ca putrāṃs cādād agnir mahyam atho imām
ā vām agant sumatir vājinīvasū ny aśvinā hṛtsu kāmā araṃsata
abhūtaṃ gopā mithunā śubhas patī priyā aryamṇo duryāṃ aśīmahi
sā mandasānā manasā śivena rayiṃ dhehi sarvavīraṃ vacasyam
sugaṃ tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ śubhas patī sthāṇuṃ pathiṣṭhām apa durmatiṃ hatam
yā oṣadhayo yā nadyo yāni kṣetrāṇi yā vanā
tās tvā vadhu prajāvatīṃ patye rakṣantu rakṣasaḥ
emaṃ panthām arukṣāma sugaṃ svastivāhanam
yasmin vīro na riṣyaty anyeṣāṃ vindate vasu
idaṃ su me naraḥ śṛṇuta yayāśiṣā daṃpatī vāmam aśnutaḥ
ye gandharvā apsarasaś ca devīr eṣu vānaspatyeṣu ye 'dhi tasthuḥ
syonās te asyai vadhvai bhavantu mā hiṃsiṣur vahatum uhyamānam
ye vadhvaś candraṃ vahatuṃ yakṣmā yanti janāṃ anu
punas tān yajñiyā devā nayantu yata āgatāḥ
mā vidan paripanthino ya āsīdanti daṃpatī
sugena durgam atītām apa drāntv arātayaḥ
saṃ kāśayāmi vahatuṃ brahmaṇā gṛhair aghoreṇa cakṣuṣā mitriyeṇa
paryāṇaddhaṃ viśvarūpaṃ yad asti syonaṃ patibhyaḥ savitā tat kṛṇotu
śivā nārīyam astam āgann imaṃ dhātā lokam asyai dideśa
tām aryamā bhago aśvinobhā prajāpatiḥ prajayā vardhayantu
ātmanvaty urvarā nārīyam āgan tasyāṃ naro vapata bījam asyām
sā vaḥ prajāṃ janayad vakṣaṇābhyo bibhratī dugdham ṛṣabhasya retaḥ
prati tiṣṭha virāḍ asi viṣṇur iveha sarasvati
sinīvāli pra jāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat
ud va ūrmiḥ śamyā hantv āpo yoktrāṇi muñcata
māduṣkṛtau vyenasāv aghnyāv aśunam āratām
aghoracakṣur apatighnī syonā śagmā suśevā suyamā gṛhebhyaḥ
vīrasūr devṛkāmā saṃ tvayaidhiṣīmahi sumasyamānā
adevṛghny apatighnīhaidhi śivā paśubhyaḥ suyamā suvarcāḥ
prajāvatī vīrasūr devṛkāmā syonemam agniṃ gārhapatyaṃ saparya
ut tiṣṭhetaḥ kim ichantīdam āgā ahaṃ tveḍe abhibhūḥ svād gṛhāt
śūnyaiṣī nirṛte yājaganthot tiṣṭhārāte pra pata meha raṃsthāḥ
yadā gārhapatyam asaparyait pūrvam agniṃ vadhūr iyam
adhā sarasvatyai nāri pitṛbhyaś ca namas kuru
śarma varmaitad ā harāsyai nāryā upastire
sinīvāli pra jāyatāṃ bhagasya sumatāv asat
yaṃ balbajaṃ nyasyatha carma copastṛṇīthana
tad ā rohatu suprajā yā kanyā vindate patim
upa stṛṇīhi balbajam adhi carmaṇi rohite
tatropaviśya suprajā imam agniṃ saparyatu
ā roha carmopa sīdāgnim eṣa devo hanti rakṣāṃsi sarvā
iha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai sujyaiṣṭhyo bhavat putras ta eṣaḥ
vi tiṣṭhantāṃ mātur asyā upasthān nānārūpāḥ paśavo jāyamānāḥ
sumaṅgaly upa sīdemam agniṃ saṃpatnī prati bhūṣeha devān
sumaṅgalī prataraṇī gṛhāṇāṃ suśevā patye śvaśurāya śaṃbhūḥ
syonā śvaśrvai pra gṛhān viśemān
syonā bhava śvaśurebhyaḥ syonā patye gṛhebhyaḥ
syonāsyai sarvasyai viśe syonā puṣṭāyaiṣāṃ bhava
sumaṅgalīr iyaṃ vadhūr imāṃ sameta paśyata
saubhāgyam asyai dattvā daurbhāgyair viparetana
yā durhārdo yuvatayo yāś ceha jaratīr api
varco nv asyai saṃ dattāthāstaṃ viparetana
rukmaprastaraṇaṃ vahyaṃ viśvā rūpāṇi bibhratam
ārohat sūryā sāvitrī bṛhate saubhagāya kam
ā roha talpaṃ sumanasyamāneha prajāṃ janaya patye asmai
indrāṇīva subudhā budhyamānā jyotiragrā uṣasaḥ prati jāgarāsi
devā agre ny apadyanta patnīḥ sam aspṛśanta tanvas tanūbhiḥ
sūryeva nāri viśvarūpā mahitvā prajāvatī patyā saṃ bhaveha
ut tiṣṭheto viśvāvaso namaseḍāmahe tvā
jāmim icha pitṛṣadaṃ nyaktāṃ sa te bhāgo januṣā tasya viddhi
apsarasaḥ sadhamādaṃ madanti havirdhānam antarā sūryaṃ ca
tās te janitram abhi tāḥ parehi namas te gandharvartunā kṛṇomi
namo gandharvasya namase namo bhāmāya cakṣuṣe ca kṛṇmaḥ
viśvāvaso brahmaṇā te namo 'bhi jāyā apsarasaḥ parehi
rāyā vayaṃ sumanasaḥ syāmod ito gandharvam āvīvṛtāma
agant sa devaḥ paramaṃ sadhastham aganma yatra pratiranta āyuḥ
saṃ pitarāv ṛtviye sṛjethāṃ mātā pitā ca retaso bhavāthaḥ
marya iva yoṣām adhi rohayaināṃ prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha puṣyataṃ rayim
tāṃ pūṣaṃ chivatamām erayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyā vapanti
yā na ūrū uśatī viśrayāti yasyām uśantaḥ praharema śepaḥ
ā rohorum upa dhatsva hastaṃ pari ṣvajasva jāyāṃ sumanasyamānaḥ
prajāṃ kṛṇvāthām iha modamānau dīrghaṃ vām āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
ā vāṃ prajāṃ janayatu prajāpatir ahorātrābhyāṃ sam anaktv aryamā
adurmaṅgalī patilokam ā viśemaṃ śaṃ no bhava dvipade śaṃ catuṣpade
devair dattaṃ manunā sākam etad vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram
yo brahmaṇe cikituṣe dadāti sa id rakṣāṃsi talpāni hanti
yaṃ me datto brahmabhāgaṃ vadhūyor vādhūyaṃ vāso vadhvaś ca vastram
yuvaṃ brahmaṇe 'numanyamānau bṛhaspate sākam indraś ca dattam
syonād yoner adhi badhyamānau hasāmudau mahasā modamānau
sugū suputrau sugṛhau tarātho jīvāv uṣaso vibhātīḥ
navaṃ vasānaḥ surabhiḥ suvāsā udāgāṃ jīva uṣaso vibhātīḥ
āṇḍāt patatrīvāmukṣi viśvasmād enasas pari
śumbhanī dyāvāpṛthivī antisumne mahivrate
āpaḥ sapta susruvur devīs tā no muñcantv aṃhasaḥ
sūryāyai devebhyo mitrāya varuṇāya ca
ye bhūtasya pracetasas tebhya idam akaraṃ namaḥ
ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ
saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ
apāsmat tama uchatu nīlaṃ piśaṅgam uta lohitaṃ yat
nirdahanī yā pṛṣātaky asmin tāṃ sthāṇāv adhy ā sajāmi
yāvatīḥ kṛtyā upavāsane yāvanto rājño varuṇasya pāśāḥ
vyṛddhayo yā asamṛddhayo yā asmin tā sthāṇāv adhi sādayāmi
yā me priyatamā tanūḥ sā me bibhāya vāsasaḥ
tasyāgre tvaṃ vanaspate nīviṃ kṛṇuṣva mā vayaṃ riṣāma
ye antā yāvatīḥ sico ya otavo ye ca tantavaḥ
vāso yat patnībhir utaṃ tan na syonam upa spṛśāt
uśatīḥ kanyalā imāḥ pitṛlokāt patiṃ yatīḥ
ava dīkṣām asṛkṣata svāhā
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
varco goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
tejo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
bhajo goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
yaśo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
payo goṣu praviṣṭaṃ yat tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
bṛhaspatināvasṛṣṭāṃ viśve devā adhārayan
raso goṣu praviṣṭo yas tenemāṃ saṃ sṛjāmasi
yadīme keśino janā gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvanto 'gham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām
yadīyaṃ duhitā tava vikeśy arudad gṛhe rodena kṛṇvaty agham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām
yaj jāmayo yad yuvatayo gṛhe te samanartiṣū rodena kṛṇvatīr agham
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām
yat te prajāyāṃ paśuṣu yad vā gṛheṣu niṣṭhitam aghakṛdbhir aghaṃ kṛtam
agniṣ ṭvā tasmād enasaḥ savitā ca pra muñcatām
iyaṃ nāry upa brūte pūlyāny āvapantikā
dīrghāyur astu me patir jīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
ihemāv indra saṃ nuda cakravākeva daṃpatī
prajayainau svastakau viśvam āyur vy aśnutām
yad āsandyām upadhāne yad vopavāsane kṛtam
vivāhe kṛtyāṃ yāṃ cakrur āsnāne tāṃ ni dadhmasi
yad duṣkṛtaṃ yac chamalaṃ vivāhe vahatau ca yat
tat saṃbhalasya kambale mṛjmahe duritaṃ vayam
saṃbhale malaṃ sādayitvā kambale duritaṃ vayam
abhūma yajñiyāḥ śuddhāḥ pra ṇa āyūṃṣi tāriṣat
kṛtrimaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ śatadan ya eṣaḥ
apāsyāḥ keśyaṃ malam apa śīrṣaṇyaṃ likhāt
aṅgādaṅgād vayam asyā apa yakṣmaṃ ni dadhmasi
tan mā prāpat pṛthivīṃ mota devān divaṃ mā prāpad urv antarikṣam
apo mā prāpan malam etad agne yamam mā prāpat pitṝṃś ca sarvān
saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasā pṛthivyāḥ saṃ tvā nahyāmi payasauṣadhīnām
saṃ tvā nahyāmi prajayā dhanena sā saṃnaddhā sanuhi vājam emam
amo 'ham asmi sā tvaṃ sāmāham asmy ṛk tvaṃ dyaur ahaṃ pṛthivī tvam
tāv iha saṃ bhavāva prajām ā janayāvahai
janiyanti nāv agravaḥ putriyanti sudānavaḥ
ariṣṭāsū sacevahi bṛhate vājasātaye
ye pitaro vadhūdarśā imaṃ vahatum āgaman
te asyai vadhvai saṃpatnyai prajāvac charma yachantu
yedaṃ pūrvāgan raśanāyamānā prajām asyai draviṇaṃ ceha dattvā
tāṃ vahantv agatasyānu panthāṃ virāḍ iyaṃ suprajā aty ajaiṣīt
pra budhyasva subudhā budhyamānā dīrghāyutvāya śataśāradāya
gṛhān gacha gṛhapatnī yathāso dīrghaṃ ta āyuḥ savitā kṛṇotu
vrātya āsīd īyamāna eva sa prajāpatiṃ sam airayat
sa prajāpatiḥ suvarṇam ātmann apaśyat tat prājanayat
tad ekam abhavat tal lalāmam abhavat tan mahad abhavat taj jyeṣṭham abhavat tad brahmābhavat tat tapo 'bhavat tat satyam abhavat tena prājāyata
so 'vardhata sa mahān abhavat sa mahādevo 'bhavat
sa devānām īśāṃ pary ait sa īśāno 'bhavat
sa ekavrātyo 'bhavat sa dhanur ādatta tad evendradhanuḥ
nīlam asyodaraṃ lohitaṃ pṛṣṭham
nīlenaivāpriyaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ prorṇoti lohitena dviṣantaṃ vidhyatīti brahmavādino vadanti
sa ud atiṣṭhat sa prācīṃ diśam anu vy acalat
taṃ bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cādityāś ca viśve ca devā anuvyacalan
bṛhate ca vai sa rathantarāya cādityebhyaś ca viśvebhyaś ca devebhya ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati
bṛhataś ca vai sa rathantarasya cādityānāṃ ca viśveṣāṃ ca devānāṃ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasya prācyāṃ diśi śraddhā puṃścalī mitro māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ
bhūtaṃ ca bhaviṣyac ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau
ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda
sa ud atiṣṭhat sa dakṣiṇāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
taṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca yajñaś ca yajamānaś ca paśavaś cānuvyacalan
yajñāyajñiyāya ca vai sa vāmadevyāya ca yajñāya ca yajamānāya ca paśubhyaś cā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati
yajñāyajñiyasya ca vai sa vāmadevyasya ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ diśy uṣāḥ puṃścalī mantro māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ
amāvāsyā ca paurṇamāsī ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau
ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda
sa ud atiṣṭhat sa pratīcīṃ diśam anu vy acalat
taṃ vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cāpaś ca varuṇaś ca rājānuvyacalan
vairūpāya ca vai sa vairājāya cādbhyaś ca varuṇāya ca rājña ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati
vairūpasya ca vai sa vairājasya cāpāṃ ca varuṇasya ca rājñaḥ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasya pratīcyāṃ diśīrā puṃścalī haso māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ
ahaś ca rātrī ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau
ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda
sa ud atiṣṭhat sa udīcīṃ diśam anu vy acalat
taṃ śyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ ca saptarṣayaś ca somaś ca rājānuvyacalan
śyaitāya ca vai sa naudhasāya ca saptarṣibhyaś ca somāya ca rājña ā vṛścate ya evaṃ vidvāṃsaṃ vrātyam upavadati
śyaitasya ca vai sa naudhasasya ca saptarṣīṇāṃ ca somasya ca rājñaḥ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasyodīcyāṃ diśi vidyut puṃścalī stanayitnur māgadho vijñānaṃ vāso 'har uṣṇīṣaṃ rātrī keśā haritau pravartau kalmalir maṇiḥ
śrutaṃ ca viśrutaṃ ca pariṣkandau mano vipathaṃ mātariśvā ca pavamānaś ca vipathavāhau vātaḥ sārathī reṣmā pratodaḥ kīrtiś ca yaśaś ca puraḥsarau
ainaṃ kīrtir gachaty ā yaśo gachati ya evaṃ veda
sa saṃvatsaram ūrdhvo 'tiṣṭhat taṃ devā abruvan vrātya kiṃ nu tiṣṭhasīti
so 'bravīd āsandīṃ me saṃ bharantv iti
tasmai vrātyāyāsandīṃ sam abharan
tasyā grīṣmaś ca vasantaś ca dvau pādāv āstāṃ śarac ca varṣāś ca dvau
bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānūcye āstāṃ yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ ca tiraścye
ṛcaḥ prāñcas tantavo yajūṃṣi tiryañcaḥ
veda āstaraṇaṃ brahmopabarhaṇam
sāmāsāda udgītho 'paśrayaḥ
tām āsandīṃ vrātya ārohat
tasya devajanāḥ pariṣkandā āsant saṃkalpāḥ prahāyyā viśvāni bhūtāny upasadaḥ
viśvāny evāsya bhūtāny upasado bhavanti ya evaṃ veda
tasmai prācyā diśaḥ
vāsantau māsau goptārāv akurvan bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
vāsantāv enaṃ māsau prācyā diśo gopāyato bṛhac ca rathantaraṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmai dakṣiṇāyā diśaḥ
graiṣmau māsau goptārāv akurvan yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
graiṣmāv enaṃ māsau dakṣiṇāyā diśo gopāyato yajñāyajñiyaṃ ca vāmadevyaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmai pratīcyā diśaḥ
vārṣikau māsau goptārāv akurvan vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
vārṣikāv enaṃ māsau pratīcyā diśo gopāyato vairūpaṃ ca vairājaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmā udīcyā diśaḥ
śāradau māsau goptārāv akurvaṃ chyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
śāradāv enaṃ māsāv udīcyā diśo gopāyataḥ śyaitaṃ ca naudhasaṃ cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmai dhruvāyā diśaḥ
haimanau māsau goptārāv akurvan bhūmiṃ cāgniṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
haimanāv enaṃ māsau dhruvāyā diśo gopāyato bhūmiś cāgniś cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmā ūrdhvāyā diśaḥ
śaiśirau māsau goptārāv akurvan divaṃ cādityaṃ cānuṣṭhātārau
śaiśirāv enaṃ māsāv ūrdhvāyā diśo gopāyato dyauś cādityaś cānu tiṣṭhato ya evaṃ veda
tasmai prācyā diśo antardeśād bhavam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
bhava enam iṣvāsaḥ prācyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmai dakṣiṇāyā diśo antardeśāc charvam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
śarva enam iśvāso dakṣiṇāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmai pratīcyā diśo antardeśāt paśupatim iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
paśupatir enam iṣvāsaḥ pratīcyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmā udīcyā diśo antardeśād ugraṃ devam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
ugra enaṃ deva iṣvāsa udīcyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmai dhruvāyā diśo antardeśād rudram iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
rudra enam iṣvāso dhruvāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmā ūrdhvāyā diśo antardeśān mahādevam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
mahādeva enam iṣvāsa ūrdhvāyā diśo antardeśād anuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
tasmai sarvebhyo antardeśebhya īśānam iṣvāsam anuṣṭhātāram akurvan
īśāna enam iṣvāsaḥ sarvebhyo antardeśebhyo 'nuṣṭhātānu tiṣṭhati nainaṃ śarvo na bhavo neśāno nāsya paśūn na samānān hinasti ya evaṃ veda
sa dhruvāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
taṃ bhūmiś cāgniś cauṣadhayaś ca vanaspatayaś ca vānaspatyāś ca vīrudhaś cānuvyacalan
bhūmeś ca vai so 'gneś cauṣadhīnāṃ ca vanaspatīnāṃ ca vānaspatyānāṃ ca vīrudhāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa ūrdhvāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
tam ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ ca sūryaś ca candraś ca nakṣatrāṇi cānuvyacalan
ṛtasya ca vai sa satyasya ca sūryasya ca candrasya ca nakṣatrāṇāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa uttamāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
tam ṛcaś ca sāmāni ca yajūṃṣi ca brahma cānuvyacalan
ṛcāṃ ca vai sa sāmnāṃ ca yajuṣāṃ ca brahmaṇaś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa bṛhatīṃ diśam anu vy acalat
tam itihāsaś ca purāṇaṃ ca gāthāś ca nārāśaṃsīś cānuvyacalan
itihāsasya ca vai sa purāṇasya ca gāthānāṃ ca nārāśaṃsīnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa paramāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
tam āhavanīyaś ca gārhapatyaś ca dakṣiṇāgniś ca yajñaś ca yajamānaś ca paśavaś cānuvyacalan
āhavanīyasya ca vai sa gārhapatyasya ca dakṣiṇāgneś ca yajñasya ca yajamānasya ca paśūnāṃ ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
so 'nādiṣṭāṃ diśam anu vy acalat
tam ṛtavaś cārtavāś ca lokāś ca laukyāś ca māsāś cārdhamāsāś cāhorātre cānuvyacalan
ṛtūnāṃ ca vai sa ārtavānāṃ ca lokānāṃ ca laukyānāṃ ca māsānāṃ cārdhamāsānāṃ cāhorātrayoś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
so 'nāvṛttāṃ diśam anu vy acalat tato nāvartsyann amanyata
taṃ ditiś cāditiś ceḍā cendrāṇī cānuvyacalan
diteś ca vai so 'diteś ceḍāyāś cendrāṇyāś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa diśo 'nu vy acalat taṃ virāḍ anu vy acalat sarve ca devāḥ sarvāś ca devatāḥ
virājaś ca vai sa sarveṣāṃ ca devānāṃ sarvāsāṃ ca devatānāṃ priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa sarvān antardeśān anu vy acalat
taṃ prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaś cānuvyacalan
prajāpateś ca vai sa parameṣṭhinaś ca pituś ca pitāmahasya ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa mahimā sadrur bhūtvāntaṃ pṛthivyā agachat samudro 'bhavat
taṃ prajāpatiś ca parameṣṭhī ca pitā ca pitāmahaś cāpaś ca śraddhā ca varṣaṃ bhūtvānuvyavartayanta
ainam āpo gachanty ainaṃ śraddhā gachaty ainaṃ varṣaṃ gachati ya evaṃ veda
taṃ śraddhā ca yajñaś ca lokaś cānnaṃ cānnādyaṃ ca bhūtvābhiparyāvartanta
ainaṃ śraddhā gachaty ainaṃ yajño gachaty ainaṃ loko gachaty ainam annaṃ gachaty ainam annādyaṃ gachati ya evaṃ veda
so 'rajyata tato rājanyo 'jāyata
sa viśaḥ sabandhūn annam annādyam abhyudatiṣṭhat
viśāṃ ca vai sa sabandhūnāṃ cānnasya cānnādyasya ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sa viśo 'nu vy acalat
taṃ sabhā ca samitiś ca senā ca surā cānuvyacalan
sabhāyāś ca vai sa samiteś ca senāyāś ca surāyāś ca priyaṃ dhāma bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo rājño 'tithir gṛhān āgachet
śreyāṃsam enam ātmano mānayet tathā kṣatrāya nā vṛścate tathā rāṣṭrāya nā vṛścate
ato vai brahma ca kṣatraṃ cod atiṣṭhatāṃ te abrūtāṃ kaṃ pra viśāveti
bṛhaspatim eva brahma praviśatv indraṃ kṣatraṃ tathā vā iti
ato vai bṛhaspatim eva brahma prāviśad indraṃ kṣatram
iyaṃ vā u pṛthivī bṛhaspatir dyaur evendraḥ
ayaṃ vā u agnir brahmāsāv ādityaḥ kṣatram
ainaṃ brahma gachati brahmavarcasī bhavati
yaḥ pṛthivīṃ bṛhaspatim agniṃ brahma veda
ainam indriyaṃ gachatīndriyavān bhavati
ya ādityaṃ kṣatraṃ divam indraṃ veda
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo 'tithir gṛhān āgachet
svayam enam abhyudetya brūyād vrātya kvāvātsīr vrātyodakaṃ vrātya tarpayantu vrātya yathā te priyaṃ tathāstu vrātya yathā te vaśas tathāstu vrātya yathā te nikāmas tathāstv iti
yad enam āha vrātya kvāvātsīr iti patha eva tena devayānān ava rundhe
yad enam āha vrātyodakam ity apa eva tenāva rundhe
yad enam āha vrātya tarpayantv iti prāṇam eva tena varṣīyāṃsaṃ kurute
yad enam āha vrātya yathā te priyaṃ tathāstv iti priyam eva tenāva rundhe
ainaṃ priyaṃ gachati priyaḥ priyasya bhavati ya evaṃ veda
yad enam āha vrātya yathā te vaśas tathāstv iti vaśam eva tenāva rundhe
ainaṃ vaśo gachati vaśī vaśināṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
yad enam āha vrātya yathā te nikāmas tathāstv iti nikāmam eva tenāva rundhe
ainaṃ nikāmo gachati nikāme nikāmasya bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātya uddhṛteṣv agniṣv adhiśrite 'gnihotre 'tithir gṛhān āgachet
svayam enam abhyudetya brūyād vrātyāti sṛja hoṣyāmīti
sa cātisṛjej juhuyān na cātisṛjen na juhuyāt
sa ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenātisṛṣṭo juhoti
pra pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti pra devayānam
na deveṣv ā vṛścate hutam asya bhavati
pary asyāsmiṃl loka āyatanaṃ śiṣyate ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenātisṛṣṭo juhoti
atha ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenānatisṛṣṭo juhoti
na pitṛyāṇaṃ panthāṃ jānāti na devayānam
ā deveṣu vṛścate ahutam asya bhavati
nāsyāsmiṃl loka āyatanaṃ śiṣyate ya evaṃ viduṣā vrātyenānatisṛṣṭo juhoti
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātya ekāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati
ye pṛthivyāṃ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo dvitīyāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati
ye 'ntarikṣe puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyas tṛtīyāṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati
ye divi puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyaś caturthīṃ rātrim atithir gṛhe vasati
ye puṇyānāṃ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe
tad yasyaivaṃ vidvān vrātyo 'parimitā rātrīr atithir gṛhe vasati
ya evāparimitāḥ puṇyā lokās tān eva tenāva rundhe
